#include <iostream>\n#include <iomanip>\nusing namespace std;\n\nvoid printArray(int arr[], int size, int highlight1 = -1, int highlight2 = -1) {\n    for (int i = 0; i < size; ++i) {\n        if (i == highlight1 || i == highlight2) {\n            cout << \"[\" << setw(3) << arr[i] << \"] \";\n        } else {\n            cout << setw(5) << arr[i] << \" \";\n        }\n    }\n    cout << endl;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    const int SIZE = 8;\n    int arr[SIZE] = {64, 34, 25, 12, 22, 11, 90, 45};\n    \n    cout << \"Исходный массив:\";\n    printArray(arr, SIZE);\n    cout << endl;\n    \n    bool swapped;\n    for (int pass = 0; pass < SIZE - 1; ++pass) {\n        swapped = false;\n        cout << \"Проход \" << pass + 1 << \":\\n\";\n        \n        for (int i = 0; i < SIZE - 1 - pass; ++i) {\n            cout << \"  Сравниваем элементы \" << i << \" и \" << i+1 << \": \";\n            printArray(arr, SIZE, i, i+1);\n            \n            if (arr[i] > arr[i + 1]) {\n                // Меняем элементы местами\n                int temp = arr[i];\n                arr[i] = arr[i + 1];\n                arr[i + 1] = temp;\n                swapped = true;\n                cout << \"  -> Меняем местами. Новый массив: \";\n                printArray(arr, SIZE, i, i+1);\n            } else {\n                cout << \"  -> Не меняем (правильный порядок).\\n\";\n            }\n        }\n        \n        cout << \"  После прохода \" << pass + 1 << \": \";\n        printArray(arr, SIZE);\n        cout << \"  На этом проходе были обмены: \" << (swapped ? \"Да\" : \"Нет\") << \"\\n\\n\";\n        \n        if (!swapped) {\n            cout << \"Массив уже отсортирован. Досрочный выход.\\n\";\n            break;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    cout << \"Отсортированный массив:\";\n    printArray(arr, SIZE);\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n\nclass A {\nprivate:\n int secret;\npublic:\n A(int s) : secret(s) {}\n friend class B;\n};\n\nclass B {\nprivate:\n int bValue;\npublic:\n B(int v) : bValue(v) {}\n int getASecret(const A& a) const { return a.secret; } // Добавлен const\n friend class C;\n int getBValue() const { return bValue; }\n};\n\nclass C {\npublic:\n void showAll(const A& a, const B& b) {\n std::cout << \"Секрет A: \" << b.getASecret(a) << std::endl;\n std::cout << \"Значение B: \" << b.getBValue() << std::endl;\n }\n};\n\nint main() {\n A objA(42);\n B objB(100);\n C objC;\n std::cout << \"Доступ из B: \" << objB.getASecret(objA) << std::endl;\n objC.showAll(objA, objB);\n return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <stdexcept>\n#include <cmath>\n#include <numeric>\n#include <limits>\n\nint compute_gcd(int a, int b) {\n    // Проверка на нулевые значения\n    if (a == 0 && b == 0) {\n        throw std::invalid_argument(\"GCD is undefined for both arguments being zero\");\n    }\n    \n    // Проверка на переполнение\n    if (a == std::numeric_limits<int>::min() && b == -1) {\n        throw std::overflow_error(\"GCD calculation would cause integer overflow\");\n    }\n    \n    if (b == std::numeric_limits<int>::min() && a == -1) {\n        throw std::overflow_error(\"GCD calculation would cause integer overflow\");\n    }\n    \n    // Используем abs для отрицательных чисел\n    a = std::abs(a);\n    b = std::abs(b);\n    \n    // Используем стандартную функцию gcd из C++17\n    return std::gcd(a, b);\n}\n\nint main() {\n    try {\n        std::cout << \"GCD of 48 and 18: \" << compute_gcd(48, 18) << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"GCD of -48 and 18: \" << compute_gcd(-48, 18) << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"GCD of 17 and 13: \" << compute_gcd(17, 13) << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"GCD of 0 and 5: \" << compute_gcd(0, 5) << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"GCD of 5 and 0: \" << compute_gcd(5, 0) << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"GCD of 0 and 0: \" << compute_gcd(0, 0) << std::endl;\n    } catch (const std::invalid_argument& e) {\n        std::cout << \"Invalid argument: \" << e.what() << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    try {\n        std::cout << \"GCD with overflow: \" << compute_gcd(std::numeric_limits<int>::min(), -1) << std::endl;\n    } catch (const std::overflow_error& e) {\n        std::cout << \"Overflow error: \" << e.what() << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <cmath>\nusing namespace std;\n\nint main() {\n double a, b, c;\n cout << \"Введите три положительных числа:\";\n cin >> a >> b >> c;\n \n if (a <= 0 || b <= 0 || c <= 0) {\n cout << \"Ошибка: числа должны быть положительными!\" << endl;\n return 1;\n }\n \n double mean = (a + b + c) / 3.0;\n double variance = (a * a + b * b + c * c) / 3.0 - mean * mean;\n double std_dev = sqrt(variance);\n double cv = (std_dev / mean) * 100.0;\n \n cout << \"Коэффициент вариации: \" << cv << \"%\" << endl;\n return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n\nvoid calculateAverage(int arr[], int size, double& average) {\n    int sum = 0;\n    for (int i = 0; i < size; i++) {\n        sum += arr[i];\n    }\n    average = static_cast<double>(sum) / size;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    int numbers[] = {1, 2, 3, 4, 5};\n    double avg;\n    \n    calculateAverage(numbers, 5, avg);\n    std::cout << \"Среднее значение: \" << avg << std::endl;\n    \n    int otherNumbers[] = {10, 20, 30};\n    calculateAverage(otherNumbers, 3, avg);\n    std::cout << \"Среднее значение второго массива: \" << avg << std::endl;\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <cmath>\n#include <iomanip>\n\nunion MoneyAmount {\n    struct {\n        long long minor_units;\n    } precise;\n    \n    struct {\n        double amount;\n    } floating;\n    \n    struct {\n        int dollars;\n        int cents;\n    } usd;\n    \n    struct {\n        int euros;\n        int euro_cents;\n    } eur;\n    \n    struct {\n        int rubles;\n        int kopecks;\n    } rub;\n    \n    MoneyAmount(double amount = 0.0) {\n        floating.amount = amount;\n        convert_to_precise();\n        convert_to_currencies();\n    }\n    \n    void convert_to_precise() {\n        precise.minor_units = static_cast<long long>(std::round(floating.amount * 100.0));\n    }\n    \n    void convert_to_currencies() {\n        usd.dollars = static_cast<int>(floating.amount);\n        usd.cents = static_cast<int>(std::round((floating.amount - usd.dollars) * 100.0));\n        \n        eur.euros = usd.dollars;\n        eur.euro_cents = usd.cents;\n        \n        double rub_amount = floating.amount * 90.0;\n        rub.rubles = static_cast<int>(rub_amount);\n        rub.kopecks = static_cast<int>(std::round((rub_amount - rub.rubles) * 100.0));\n    }\n    \n    void set_usd(int dollars, int cents) {\n        usd.dollars = dollars;\n        usd.cents = cents;\n        floating.amount = dollars + cents / 100.0;\n        convert_to_precise();\n        convert_to_currencies();\n    }\n    \n    void set_eur(int euros, int euro_cents) {\n        eur.euros = euros;\n        eur.euro_cents = euro_cents;\n        floating.amount = euros + euro_cents / 100.0;\n        convert_to_precise();\n        convert_to_currencies();\n    }\n    \n    void add(const MoneyAmount& other) {\n        precise.minor_units += other.precise.minor_units;\n        floating.amount = precise.minor_units / 100.0;\n        convert_to_currencies();\n    }\n    \n    void subtract(const MoneyAmount& other) {\n        precise.minor_units -= other.precise.minor_units;\n        floating.amount = precise.minor_units / 100.0;\n        convert_to_currencies();\n    }\n    \n    void print() const {\n        std::cout << std::fixed << std::setprecision(2);\n        std::cout << \"Финансовая сумма:\" << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"  Точно (копейки): \" << precise.minor_units << \" коп.\" << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"  С плавающей точкой: \" << floating.amount << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"  USD: $\" << usd.dollars << \".\" << std::setfill('0') << std::setw(2) << usd.cents << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"  EUR: €\" << eur.euros << \".\" << std::setfill('0') << std::setw(2) << eur.euro_cents << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"  RUB: \" << rub.rubles << \",\" << std::setfill('0') << std::setw(2) << rub.kopecks << \" руб.\" << std::endl;\n        std::cout << std::setfill(' ');\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    std::cout << \"Финансовые суммы в разных валютах:\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"===================================\" << std::endl;\n    \n    MoneyAmount amount1(123.45);\n    MoneyAmount amount2;\n    amount2.set_usd(50, 75);\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\nСумма 1 (из double):\" << std::endl;\n    amount1.print();\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\nСумма 2 (из USD):\" << std::endl;\n    amount2.print();\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\nОперации:\" << std::endl;\n    MoneyAmount total = amount1;\n    total.add(amount2);\n    std::cout << \"amount1 + amount2:\" << std::endl;\n    total.print();\n    \n    MoneyAmount diff = amount1;\n    diff.subtract(amount2);\n    std::cout << \"\\namount1 - amount2:\" << std::endl;\n    diff.print();\n    \n    MoneyAmount amount3;\n    amount3.set_eur(100, 0);\n    std::cout << \"\\nСумма в евро:\" << std::endl;\n    amount3.print();\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\nРазмер MoneyAmount: \" << sizeof(MoneyAmount) << \" байт\" << std::endl;\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <unistd.h>\n#include <iostream>\nint main() {\n    uid_t uid = getuid();\n    gid_t gid = getgid();\n    std::cout << \"User ID: \" << uid << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"Group ID: \" << gid << std::endl;\n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <string>\n#include <sstream>\n#include <cctype>\n#include <vector>\n\nstd::string rleCompress(const std::string& input) {\n    if(input.empty()) return \"\";\n    \n    std::stringstream compressed;\n    int count = 1;\n    char current = input[0];\n    \n    for(size_t i = 1; i < input.length(); i++) {\n        if(input[i] == current) {\n            count++;\n        } else {\n            if(count > 1 || !std::isalnum(current)) {\n                compressed << '\\\\' << count << current;\n            } else {\n                compressed << current;\n            }\n            current = input[i];\n            count = 1;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // Обработка последней последовательности\n    if(count > 1 || !std::isalnum(current)) {\n        compressed << '\\\\' << count << current;\n    } else {\n        compressed << current;\n    }\n    \n    return compressed.str();\n}\n\nstd::string rleDecompress(const std::string& compressed) {\n    std::stringstream decompressed;\n    \n    for(size_t i = 0; i < compressed.length(); i++) {\n        if(compressed[i] == '\\\\' && i + 1 < compressed.length()) {\n            // Извлекаем число\n            int count = 0;\n            size_t j = i + 1;\n            while(j < compressed.length() && std::isdigit(compressed[j])) {\n                count = count * 10 + (compressed[j] - '0');\n                j++;\n            }\n            \n            if(j < compressed.length() && count > 0) {\n                char ch = compressed[j];\n                decompressed << std::string(count, ch);\n                i = j;\n            } else {\n                // Некорректный формат\n                decompressed << compressed[i];\n            }\n        } else {\n            decompressed << compressed[i];\n        }\n    }\n    \n    return decompressed.str();\n}\n\nint main() {\n    std::vector<std::string> tests = {\n        \"aaaaabbbcccdde\",\n        \"abc\",\n        \"aaaaaaaaaa\",\n        \"a\",\n        \"\",\n        \"111222333444555\",\n        \"ab\\\\cd\", // Специальный символ\n        \"Hello World!!!\"\n    };\n    \n    std::cout << \"Run-Length Encoding Test:\\n\";\n    for(const std::string& test : tests) {\n        std::string compressed = rleCompress(test);\n        std::string decompressed = rleDecompress(compressed);\n        \n        std::cout << \"Original: \\\"\" << test << \"\\\"\" << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"Compressed: \\\"\" << compressed << \"\\\"\" << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"Decompressed: \\\"\" << decompressed << \"\\\"\" << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"Match: \" << (test == decompressed ? \"YES\" : \"NO\") << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"Compression ratio: \" << (test.empty() ? 0.0 : compressed.length() * 100.0 / test.length()) << \"%\" << std::endl;\n        std::cout << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    // Тест с повторяющимися escape-символами\n    std::string tricky = \"\\\\\\\\\\\\5x\\\\3y\";\n    std::cout << \"Tricky test:\\n\";\n    std::cout << \"Original: \\\"\" << tricky << \"\\\"\" << std::endl;\n    std::string comp = rleCompress(tricky);\n    std::cout << \"Compressed: \\\"\" << comp << \"\\\"\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"Decompressed: \\\"\" << rleDecompress(comp) << \"\\\"\" << std::endl;\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <vector>\n#include <queue>\n#include <mutex>\n#include <condition_variable>\n#include <chrono>\n#include <stdexcept>\n#include <thread>\n\nclass DatabaseConnectionPool {\n    struct Connection {\n        int id;\n        std::chrono::steady_clock::time_point last_used;\n        bool in_use;\n        Connection(int i) : id(i), in_use(false) {}\n        bool is_expired(std::chrono::seconds timeout) const {\n            return std::chrono::steady_clock::now() - last_used > timeout;\n        }\n    };\n    std::vector<Connection> connections;\n    std::queue<int> available;\n    std::mutex mtx;\n    std::condition_variable cv;\n    std::chrono::seconds timeout;\n    void cleanup_expired() {\n        for (auto& conn : connections) {\n            if (!conn.in_use && conn.is_expired(timeout)) {\n                std::cout << \"Connection \" << conn.id << \" expired and removed\" << std::endl;\n                conn.in_use = true; // пометить как удаляемую\n            }\n        }\n    }\npublic:\n    DatabaseConnectionPool(size_t size, std::chrono::seconds t = std::chrono::seconds(30))\n        : timeout(t) {\n        for (size_t i = 0; i < size; ++i) {\n            connections.emplace_back(i);\n            available.push(i);\n        }\n        std::cout << \"Connection pool created with \" << size << \" connections\" << std::endl;\n    }\n    class ConnectionHandle {\n        DatabaseConnectionPool& pool;\n        int conn_id;\n    public:\n        ConnectionHandle(DatabaseConnectionPool& p, int id) : pool(p), conn_id(id) {\n            pool.connections[conn_id].in_use = true;\n            pool.connections[conn_id].last_used = std::chrono::steady_clock::now();\n            std::cout << \"Acquired connection \" << conn_id << std::endl;\n        }\n        ~ConnectionHandle() {\n            {\n                std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(pool.mtx);\n                pool.connections[conn_id].in_use = false;\n                pool.connections[conn_id].last_used = std::chrono::steady_clock::now();\n                pool.available.push(conn_id);\n            }\n            pool.cv.notify_one();\n            std::cout << \"Released connection \" << conn_id << std::endl;\n        }\n        void execute(const std::string& query) {\n            std::cout << \"Connection \" << conn_id << \" executing: \" << query << std::endl;\n        }\n        ConnectionHandle(const ConnectionHandle&) = delete;\n        ConnectionHandle& operator=(const ConnectionHandle&) = delete;\n    };\n    ConnectionHandle acquire() {\n        std::unique_lock<std::mutex> lock(mtx);\n        cv.wait(lock, [this] {\n            cleanup_expired();\n            return !available.empty();\n        });\n        int id = available.front();\n        available.pop();\n        return ConnectionHandle(*this, id);\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    DatabaseConnectionPool pool(3, std::chrono::seconds(5));\n    std::vector<std::thread> threads;\n    for (int i = 0; i < 5; ++i) {\n        threads.emplace_back([&pool, i] {\n            auto conn = pool.acquire();\n            conn.execute(\"SELECT * FROM table\");\n            std::this_thread::sleep_for(std::chrono::milliseconds(100));\n        });\n    }\n    for (auto& t : threads) t.join();\n    return 0;\n}
#include <sys/ipc.h>\n#include <sys/shm.h>\n#include <sys/sem.h>\n#include <sys/wait.h>\n#include <unistd.h>\n#include <iostream>\n#include <cstring>\n#include <string>\n#include <ctime>\n#include <stdexcept>\n#include <vector>\n#include <algorithm>\nusing namespace std;\n\nunion semun {\n int val;\n struct semid_ds *buf;\n unsigned short *array;\n};\n\nclass DistributedCache {\n struct CacheEntry {\n char key[32];\n char value[128];\n time_t timestamp;\n };\n \n int shmid;\n int semid;\n CacheEntry* cache;  // Указатель на массив записей\n static const int MAX_ENTRIES = 100;\n \n void sem_wait(int sem_num) {\n struct sembuf op;\n op.sem_num = static_cast<unsigned short>(sem_num);\n op.sem_op = -1;\n op.sem_flg = 0;\n semop(semid, &op, 1);\n }\n \n void sem_signal(int sem_num) {\n struct sembuf op;\n op.sem_num = static_cast<unsigned short>(sem_num);\n op.sem_op = 1;\n op.sem_flg = 0;\n semop(semid, &op, 1);\n }\n \npublic:\n DistributedCache(key_t key) {\n // Создаем или получаем разделяемую память\n shmid = shmget(key, sizeof(CacheEntry) * MAX_ENTRIES, 0666 | IPC_CREAT);\n if (shmid == -1) {\n throw runtime_error(\"shmget failed\");\n }\n \n // Присоединяем разделяемую память\n cache = (CacheEntry*)shmat(shmid, nullptr, 0);\n if (cache == (void*)-1) {\n throw runtime_error(\"shmat failed\");\n }\n \n // Создаем или получаем набор семафоров (2 семафора)\n semid = semget(key, 2, 0666 | IPC_CREAT);\n if (semid == -1) {\n throw runtime_error(\"semget failed\");\n }\n \n // Инициализируем семафоры\n union semun arg;\n arg.val = 1;  // Семафор 0 - для взаимного исключения\n if (semctl(semid, 0, SETVAL, arg) == -1) {\n throw runtime_error(\"semctl SETVAL failed for semaphore 0\");\n }\n \n arg.val = 0;  // Семафор 1 - для счетчика элементов\n if (semctl(semid, 1, SETVAL, arg) == -1) {\n throw runtime_error(\"semctl SETVAL failed for semaphore 1\");\n }\n \n // Инициализация разделяемой памяти (только если создали новый)\n if (shmctl(shmid, IPC_STAT, nullptr) != -1) {\n // Инициализируем только если shared memory только что создана\n memset(cache, 0, sizeof(CacheEntry) * MAX_ENTRIES);\n }\n \n cout << \"Cache initialized with \" << MAX_ENTRIES << \" entries\" << endl;\n }\n \n ~DistributedCache() {\n // Отсоединяем разделяемую память\n if (cache != (void*)-1) {\n shmdt(cache);\n }\n }\n \n void put(const string& key, const string& value) {\n sem_wait(0); // Блокировка для записи\n \n int empty_slot = -1;\n for(int i = 0; i < MAX_ENTRIES; i++) {\n if(cache[i].key[0] == '\\0') {\n empty_slot = i;\n break;\n }\n }\n \n if(empty_slot == -1) {\n // Если нет свободных слотов, используем простую стратегию LRU\n empty_slot = 0;\n time_t oldest = cache[0].timestamp;\n for(int i = 1; i < MAX_ENTRIES; i++) {\n if(cache[i].timestamp < oldest) {\n oldest = cache[i].timestamp;\n empty_slot = i;\n }\n }\n cout << \"[CACHE] Replacing oldest entry at slot \" << empty_slot << endl;\n }\n \n // Сохраняем данные\n strncpy(cache[empty_slot].key, key.c_str(), 31);\n cache[empty_slot].key[31] = '\\0';\n \n strncpy(cache[empty_slot].value, value.c_str(), 127);\n cache[empty_slot].value[127] = '\\0';\n \n cache[empty_slot].timestamp = time(nullptr);\n \n cout << \"[CACHE] Put: \" << key << \" -> \" << value \n << \" at slot \" << empty_slot << endl;\n \n sem_signal(0); // Разблокировка\n sem_signal(1); // Уведомляем читателей (увеличиваем счетчик)\n }\n \n string get(const string& key) {\n // Ждем, пока появится хотя бы один элемент\n struct sembuf op;\n op.sem_num = 1;\n op.sem_op = -1;\n op.sem_flg = 0;\n \n // Проверяем, есть ли элементы\n int sem_val = semctl(semid, 1, GETVAL);\n if (sem_val > 0) {\n semop(semid, &op, 1); // Уменьшаем счетчик\n } else {\n // Если элементов нет, просто пропускаем ожидание\n }\n \n sem_wait(0); // Блокировка для чтения\n \n string result;\n for(int i = 0; i < MAX_ENTRIES; i++) {\n if(strcmp(cache[i].key, key.c_str()) == 0) {\n result = cache[i].value;\n cache[i].timestamp = time(nullptr); // Обновляем время доступа\n break;\n }\n }\n \n sem_signal(0); // Разблокировка\n \n if (!result.empty()) {\n cout << \"[CACHE] Get \" << key << \": \" << result << endl;\n } else {\n cout << \"[CACHE] Get \" << key << \": NOT FOUND\" << endl;\n // Возвращаем счетчик, т.к. элемент не найден\n sem_signal(1);\n }\n \n return result;\n }\n \n void remove(const string& key) {\n sem_wait(0); // Блокировка\n \n bool found = false;\n for(int i = 0; i < MAX_ENTRIES; i++) {\n if(strcmp(cache[i].key, key.c_str()) == 0) {\n cache[i].key[0] = '\\0';\n cache[i].value[0] = '\\0';\n cache[i].timestamp = 0;\n found = true;\n \n // Уменьшаем счетчик элементов\n struct sembuf op;\n op.sem_num = 1;\n op.sem_op = -1;\n op.sem_flg = 0;\n semop(semid, &op, 1);\n \n cout << \"[CACHE] Removed: \" << key << endl;\n break;\n }\n }\n \n if (!found) {\n cout << \"[CACHE] Remove \" << key << \": NOT FOUND\" << endl;\n }\n \n sem_signal(0); // Разблокировка\n }\n \n void clear() {\n sem_wait(0); // Блокировка\n \n memset(cache, 0, sizeof(CacheEntry) * MAX_ENTRIES);\n \n // Сбрасываем счетчик элементов в 0\n union semun arg;\n arg.val = 0;\n semctl(semid, 1, SETVAL, arg);\n \n sem_signal(0); // Разблокировка\n \n cout << \"[CACHE] All entries cleared\" << endl;\n }\n \n void stats() {\n sem_wait(0); // Блокировка\n \n int count = 0;\n int empty = 0;\n time_t now = time(nullptr);\n \n for(int i = 0; i < MAX_ENTRIES; i++) {\n if(cache[i].key[0] != '\\0') {\n count++;\n } else {\n empty++;\n }\n }\n \n sem_signal(0); // Разблокировка\n \n cout << \"[CACHE STATS] Total entries: \" << count << endl;\n cout << \"[CACHE STATS] Empty slots: \" << empty << endl;\n cout << \"[CACHE STATS] Cache size: \" << MAX_ENTRIES << endl;\n }\n};\n\nint main() {\n try {\n cout << \"=== Distributed Cache with Shared Memory and Semaphores ===\" << endl;\n \n DistributedCache cache(1234);\n \n // Создаем несколько процессов для демонстрации\n vector<pid_t> pids;\n \n for (int i = 0; i < 3; i++) {\n pid_t pid = fork();\n \n if (pid == 0) {\n // Дочерний процесс\n cout << \"[PROCESS \" << getpid() << \"] Started\" << endl;\n \n // Каждый процесс пишет свои данные\n string key = \"key\" + to_string(i);\n string value = \"value_from_process_\" + to_string(getpid());\n \n cache.put(key, value);\n \n // Читаем данные других процессов\n for (int j = 0; j < 3; j++) {\n string read_key = \"key\" + to_string(j);\n string result = cache.get(read_key);\n if (!result.empty()) {\n cout << \"[PROCESS \" << getpid() << \"] Read \" << read_key \n << \": \" << result << endl;\n }\n }\n \n cout << \"[PROCESS \" << getpid() << \"] Finished\" << endl;\n _exit(0);\n } else if (pid > 0) {\n pids.push_back(pid);\n }\n }\n \n // Родительский процесс\n cout << \"[PARENT] Waiting for child processes...\" << endl;\n \n // Ждем завершения дочерних процессов\n for (pid_t pid : pids) {\n waitpid(pid, nullptr, 0);\n }\n \n // Выводим статистику\n cout << \"\\n[PARENT] Final cache statistics:\" << endl;\n cache.stats();\n \n // Тестируем удаление\n cache.remove(\"key0\");\n cache.stats();\n \n // Очистка\n cache.clear();\n cache.stats();\n \n cout << \"\\n=== Test completed successfully ===\" << endl;\n \n } catch (const exception& e) {\n cerr << \"Error: \" << e.what() << endl;\n return 1;\n }\n \n return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <cmath>\nusing namespace std;\n\nint main() {\n double number;\n const double epsilon = 1e-10;\n const int max_iterations = 1000;\n \n cout << \"Введите положительное число:\";\n cin >> number;\n \n if (number < 0) {\n cout << \"Ошибка: невозможно вычислить квадратный корень из отрицательного числа\" << endl;\n return 1;\n }\n \n if (number == 0) {\n cout << \"Квадратный корень из 0 равен 0\" << endl;\n return 0;\n }\n \n double guess = number / 2.0;\n int iterations = 0;\n \n while (fabs(guess * guess - number) > epsilon && iterations < max_iterations) {\n guess = (guess + number / guess) / 2.0;\n iterations++;\n }\n \n cout << \"Приближённое значение квадратного корня из \" << number << \" = \" << guess << endl;\n cout << \"Количество итераций: \" << iterations << endl;\n \n return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <string>\nusing namespace std;\n\nclass BankAccount {\nprivate:\n    string accountNumber;\n    string ownerName;\n    double balance;\n    \npublic:\n    BankAccount(const string& accNum, const string& owner, double initialBalance) \n        : accountNumber(accNum), ownerName(owner), balance(initialBalance) {\n        if (balance < 0) balance = 0;\n    }\n    \n    bool deposit(double amount) {\n        if (amount > 0) {\n            balance += amount;\n            cout << \"На счет \" << accountNumber << \" внесено: \" << amount << endl;\n            return true;\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n    \n    bool withdraw(double amount) {\n        if (amount > 0 && balance >= amount) {\n            balance -= amount;\n            cout << \"Со счета \" << accountNumber << \" снято: \" << amount << endl;\n            return true;\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n    \n    void printInfo() const {\n        cout << \"Счет: \" << accountNumber << endl;\n        cout << \"Владелец: \" << ownerName << endl;\n        cout << \"Баланс: \" << balance << \" руб.\" << endl;\n    }\n    \n    string getAccountNumber() const { return accountNumber; }\n    string getOwnerName() const { return ownerName; }\n    double getBalance() const { return balance; }\n};\n\nclass Bank {\nprivate:\n    static const int MAX_ACCOUNTS = 100;\n    BankAccount* accounts[MAX_ACCOUNTS];\n    int accountCount;\n    \npublic:\n    Bank() : accountCount(0) {\n        for (int i = 0; i < MAX_ACCOUNTS; i++) {\n            accounts[i] = nullptr;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    bool addAccount(BankAccount* account) {\n        if (accountCount >= MAX_ACCOUNTS) {\n            cout << \"Достигнуто максимальное количество счетов\" << endl;\n            return false;\n        }\n        accounts[accountCount++] = account;\n        cout << \"Счет \" << account->getAccountNumber() << \" добавлен в банк\" << endl;\n        return true;\n    }\n    \n    BankAccount* findAccount(const string& accountNumber) const {\n        for (int i = 0; i < accountCount; i++) {\n            if (accounts[i] && accounts[i]->getAccountNumber() == accountNumber) {\n                return accounts[i];\n            }\n        }\n        return nullptr;\n    }\n    \n    double getTotalBalance() const {\n        double total = 0.0;\n        for (int i = 0; i < accountCount; i++) {\n            if (accounts[i]) {\n                total += accounts[i]->getBalance();\n            }\n        }\n        return total;\n    }\n    \n    void printAllAccounts() const {\n        cout << \"\\n=== ВСЕ СЧЕТА В БАНКЕ ===\" << endl;\n        for (int i = 0; i < accountCount; i++) {\n            if (accounts[i]) {\n                accounts[i]->printInfo();\n                cout << \"---\" << endl;\n            }\n        }\n        cout << \"Общий баланс банка: \" << getTotalBalance() << \" руб.\" << endl;\n    }\n    \n    int getAccountCount() const { return accountCount; }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    Bank bank;\n    \n    BankAccount acc1(\"12345\", \"Иван Иванов\", 1000.0);\n    BankAccount acc2(\"67890\", \"Петр Петров\", 5000.0);\n    BankAccount acc3(\"54321\", \"Анна Сидорова\", 3000.0);\n    \n    bank.addAccount(&acc1);\n    bank.addAccount(&acc2);\n    bank.addAccount(&acc3);\n    \n    bank.printAllAccounts();\n    \n    BankAccount* found = bank.findAccount(\"67890\");\n    if (found) {\n        cout << \"\\nНайден счет:\" << endl;\n        found->printInfo();\n        found->deposit(1000.0);\n    }\n    \n    cout << \"\\nОбщий баланс после пополнения: \" << bank.getTotalBalance() << endl;\n    \n    // Поиск несуществующего счета\n    BankAccount* notFound = bank.findAccount(\"00000\");\n    if (!notFound) {\n        cout << \"Счет не найден\" << endl;\n    }\n    \n    // Демонстрация снятия средств\n    found = bank.findAccount(\"12345\");\n    if (found) {\n        found->withdraw(500.0);\n        cout << \"Новый баланс счета \" << found->getAccountNumber() << \": \" << found->getBalance() << endl;\n    }\n    \n    // Финансовая статистика\n    cout << \"\\n=== ФИНАНСОВАЯ СТАТИСТИКА ===\" << endl;\n    cout << \"Количество счетов: \" << bank.getAccountCount() << endl;\n    cout << \"Общий баланс: \" << bank.getTotalBalance() << \" руб.\" << endl;\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <type_traits>\n#include <utility>\n#include <string>\nusing namespace std;\n\n// Для C++17 используем SFINAE вместо концептов\n// В C++20 было бы: template<typename T> concept Addable = ...\n\ntemplate<typename T, typename = void>\nstruct is_addable : false_type {};\n\ntemplate<typename T>\nstruct is_addable<T, void_t<decltype(declval<T>() + declval<T>())>> : true_type {};\n\ntemplate<typename T>\nconstexpr bool is_addable_v = is_addable<T>::value;\n\ntemplate<typename T, typename = void>\nstruct is_comparable : false_type {};\n\ntemplate<typename T>\nstruct is_comparable<T, void_t<decltype(declval<T>() < declval<T>()), decltype(declval<T>() > declval<T>())>> : true_type {};\n\ntemplate<typename T>\nconstexpr bool is_comparable_v = is_comparable<T>::value;\n\n// Определение класса Point ВНЕ main()\nstruct Point {\n    int x, y;\n    Point(int x = 0, int y = 0) : x(x), y(y) {}\n    Point operator+(const Point& other) const {\n        return Point(x + other.x, y + other.y);\n    }\n    bool operator<(const Point& other) const {\n        return (x < other.x) || (x == other.x && y < other.y);\n    }\n    bool operator>(const Point& other) const {\n        return (x > other.x) || (x == other.x && y > other.y);\n    }\n};\n\n// Оператор вывода для Point (определяем отдельно)\nostream& operator<<(ostream& os, const Point& p) {\n    return os << \"Point(\" << p.x << \",\" << p.y << \")\";\n}\n\n// Функция для Addable типов\n// Вариант 1: enable_if в возвращаемом типе\ntemplate<typename T>\ntypename enable_if<is_addable_v<T>, T>::type add(T a, T b) {\n    return a + b;\n}\n\n// Вариант 2: static_assert для понятного сообщения об ошибке\ntemplate<typename T>\nT safe_add(T a, T b) {\n    static_assert(is_addable_v<T>, \"Type must support addition (+ operator)\");\n    return a + b;\n}\n\n// Функция для Comparable типов\ntemplate<typename T>\ntypename enable_if<is_comparable_v<T>, T>::type getMax(T a, T b) {\n    return (a > b) ? a : b;\n}\n\ntemplate<typename T>\nT safe_getMax(T a, T b) {\n    static_assert(is_comparable_v<T>, \"Type must support comparison (< and > operators)\");\n    return (a > b) ? a : b;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    cout << \"=== Проверка сложения ===\" << endl;\n    cout << \"add(3, 4) = \" << add(3, 4) << endl;\n    cout << \"add(2.5, 1.5) = \" << add(2.5, 1.5) << endl;\n    cout << \"safe_add(10, 20) = \" << safe_add(10, 20) << endl;\n    \n    cout << endl << \"=== Проверка сравнения ===\" << endl;\n    cout << \"getMax(5, 3) = \" << getMax(5, 3) << endl;\n    cout << \"getMax(2.1, 3.4) = \" << getMax(2.1, 3.4) << endl;\n    cout << \"safe_getMax(100, 50) = \" << safe_getMax(100, 50) << endl;\n    \n    // Проверка наших type traits\n    cout << endl << \"=== Проверка type traits ===\" << endl;\n    cout << \"is_addable_v<int> = \" << boolalpha << is_addable_v<int> << endl;\n    cout << \"is_addable_v<double> = \" << is_addable_v<double> << endl;\n    cout << \"is_addable_v<const char*> = \" << is_addable_v<const char*> << endl;\n    cout << \"is_addable_v<string> = \" << is_addable_v<string> << endl;\n    \n    cout << \"is_comparable_v<int> = \" << is_comparable_v<int> << endl;\n    cout << \"is_comparable_v<double> = \" << is_comparable_v<double> << endl;\n    cout << \"is_comparable_v<string> = \" << is_comparable_v<string> << endl;\n    \n    // Примеры с пользовательским типом Point\n    cout << endl << \"=== Пользовательский тип Point ===\" << endl;\n    Point p1(1, 2), p2(3, 4);\n    cout << \"is_addable_v<Point> = \" << is_addable_v<Point> << endl;\n    cout << \"is_comparable_v<Point> = \" << is_comparable_v<Point> << endl;\n    cout << \"add(p1, p2) = \" << add(p1, p2) << endl;\n    cout << \"getMax(p1, p2) = \" << getMax(p1, p2) << endl;\n    \n    // Проверка с другими типами\n    cout << endl << \"=== Проверка с string ===\" << endl;\n    string s1 = \"Hello\", s2 = \"World\";\n    cout << \"is_addable_v<string> = \" << is_addable_v<string> << endl;\n    cout << \"is_comparable_v<string> = \" << is_comparable_v<string> << endl;\n    cout << \"add(s1, s2) = \" << add(s1, s2) << endl;\n    cout << \"getMax(s1, s2) = \" << getMax(s1, s2) << endl;\n    \n    // Демонстрация ошибок компиляции\n    cout << endl << \"=== Демонстрация ошибок компиляции ===\" << endl;\n    cout << \"Следующие вызовы вызовут ошибки (раскомментируйте для проверки):\" << endl;\n    \n    // Раскомментируйте для проверки ошибок компиляции:\n    // struct NoOps {};\n    // NoOps #include <iostream>\n#include <chrono>\n#include <thread>\nusing namespace std;\nusing namespace chrono;\n\nvoid long_operation() {\n    this_thread::sleep_for(milliseconds(500));\n}\n\nint main() {\n    auto start = high_resolution_clock::now();\n    \n    long_operation();\n    \n    auto end = high_resolution_clock::now();\n    auto duration = duration_cast<milliseconds>(end - start);\n    \n    cout << \"Операция заняла: \" << duration.count() << \" мс\" << endl;\n    \n    auto now = system_clock::now();\n    time_t now_time = system_clock::to_time_t(now);\n    cout << \"Текущее время: \" << ctime(&now_time);\n    \n    steady_clock::time_point steady_start = steady_clock::now();\n    this_thread::sleep_for(milliseconds(100));\n    steady_clock::time_point steady_end = steady_clock::now();\n    \n    auto steady_duration = duration_cast<microseconds>(steady_end - steady_start);\n    cout << \"Steady clock duration: \" << steady_duration.count() << \" мкс\" << endl;\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <vector>\n#include <queue>\n#include <climits>\n#include <unordered_map>\n\nstd::vector<int> dijkstra(const std::vector<std::unordered_map<int, int>>& graph, int source) {\n    int n = graph.size();\n    std::vector<int> dist(n, INT_MAX);\n    std::vector<bool> visited(n, false);\n    \n    dist[source] = 0;\n    \n    // Минимальная куча пар (расстояние, вершина)\n    std::priority_queue<std::pair<int, int>, std::vector<std::pair<int, int>>, std::greater<std::pair<int, int>>> pq;\n    pq.push({0, source});\n    \n    while (!pq.empty()) {\n        int u = pq.top().second;\n        pq.pop();\n        \n        if (visited[u]) continue;\n        visited[u] = true;\n        \n        for (const auto& neighbor : graph[u]) {\n            int v = neighbor.first;\n            int weight = neighbor.second;\n            \n            if (!visited[v] && dist[u] != INT_MAX && dist[u] + weight < dist[v]) {\n                dist[v] = dist[u] + weight;\n                pq.push({dist[v], v});\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    return dist;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    int n = 5;\n    std::vector<std::unordered_map<int, int>> graph(n);\n    \n    graph[0][1] = 10;\n    graph[0][4] = 5;\n    graph[1][2] = 1;\n    graph[1][4] = 2;\n    graph[2][3] = 4;\n    graph[3][2] = 6;\n    graph[3][0] = 7;\n    graph[4][1] = 3;\n    graph[4][2] = 9;\n    graph[4][3] = 2;\n    \n    int source = 0;\n    std::vector<int> distances = dijkstra(graph, source);\n    \n    std::cout << \"Кратчайшие расстояния от вершины \" << source << \":\" << std::endl;\n    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {\n        if (distances[i] == INT_MAX) {\n            std::cout << \"Вершина \" << i << \": недостижима\" << std::endl;\n        } else {\n            std::cout << \"Вершина \" << i << \": \" << distances[i] << std::endl;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <string>\n#include <cstdlib>\n#include <ctime>\n\nclass Playlist {\nprivate:\n    std::string songs[20];\n    int songCount;\n    const int MAX_SONGS = 20;\n    \npublic:\n    Playlist() : songCount(0) {\n        for (int i = 0; i < MAX_SONGS; i++) songs[i] = \"\";\n        std::srand(std::time(0));\n    }\n    \n    bool addSong(const std::string& songName) {\n        if (songName.empty()) {\n            std::cout << \"Название песни не может быть пустым\" << std::endl;\n            return false;\n        }\n        if (songCount >= MAX_SONGS) {\n            std::cout << \"Плейлист полен! Максимум \" << MAX_SONGS << \" песен\" << std::endl;\n            return false;\n        }\n        songs[songCount++] = songName;\n        std::cout << \"Добавлена песня: \" << songName << std::endl;\n        return true;\n    }\n    \n    bool removeSong(int index) {\n        if (index < 0 || index >= songCount) {\n            std::cout << \"Неверный индекс песни\" << std::endl;\n            return false;\n        }\n        std::cout << \"Удалена песня: \" << songs[index] << std::endl;\n        for (int i = index; i < songCount - 1; i++) {\n            songs[i] = songs[i + 1];\n        }\n        songs[songCount - 1] = \"\";\n        songCount--;\n        return true;\n    }\n    \n    void shuffle() {\n        if (songCount < 2) {\n            std::cout << \"Недостаточно песен для перемешивания\" << std::endl;\n            return;\n        }\n        for (int i = 0; i < songCount; i++) {\n            int j = std::rand() % songCount;\n            std::string temp = songs[i];\n            songs[i] = songs[j];\n            songs[j] = temp;\n        }\n        std::cout << \"Плейлист перемешан!\" << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    void play() const {\n        if (songCount == 0) {\n            std::cout << \"Плейлист пуст\" << std::endl;\n            return;\n        }\n        std::cout << \"\\n=== Воспроизведение плейлиста ===\" << std::endl;\n        for (int i = 0; i < songCount; i++) {\n            std::cout << i + 1 << \". \" << songs[i] << std::endl;\n        }\n        std::cout << \"Всего песен: \" << songCount << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    void clear() {\n        for (int i = 0; i < songCount; i++) {\n            songs[i] = \"\";\n        }\n        songCount = 0;\n        std::cout << \"Плейлист очищен\" << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    int findSong(const std::string& songName) const {\n        for (int i = 0; i < songCount; i++) {\n            if (songs[i] == songName) {\n                return i;\n            }\n        }\n        return -1;\n    }\n    \n    void playSong(int index) const {\n        if (index < 0 || index >= songCount) {\n            std::cout << \"Неверный индекс песни\" << std::endl;\n            return;\n        }\n        std::cout << \"Сейчас играет: \" << songs[index] << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    int getSongCount() const { return songCount; }\n    int getMaxSongs() const { return MAX_SONGS; }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    Playlist myPlaylist;\n    \n    myPlaylist.addSong(\"Bohemian Rhapsody\");\n    myPlaylist.addSong(\"Imagine\");\n    myPlaylist.addSong(\"Hotel California\");\n    myPlaylist.addSong(\"Stairway to Heaven\");\n    \n    myPlaylist.play();\n    \n    myPlaylist.shuffle();\n    myPlaylist.play();\n    \n    int index = myPlaylist.findSong(\"Imagine\");\n    if (index != -1) {\n        std::cout << \"\\nПесня 'Imagine' найдена на позиции \" << index + 1 << std::endl;\n        myPlaylist.playSong(index);\n    }\n    \n    myPlaylist.removeSong(1);\n    myPlaylist.play();\n    \n    // Добавляем песни до лимита\n    for (int i = 0; i < 20; i++) {\n        myPlaylist.addSong(\"Песня \" + std::to_string(i));\n    }\n    \n    myPlaylist.clear();\n    myPlaylist.play();\n    \n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\nusing namespace std;\n\nclass Date {\n    int day, month, year;\n    bool isLeap(int y) const { return (y % 4 == 0 && y % 100 != 0) || (y % 400 == 0); }\n    int daysInMonth() const {\n        int days[] = {31,28,31,30,31,30,31,31,30,31,30,31};\n        if (month == 2 && isLeap(year)) return 29;\n        return days[month - 1];\n    }\n    void normalize() {\n        while (day > daysInMonth()) {\n            day -= daysInMonth();\n            month++;\n            if (month > 12) { month = 1; year++; }\n        }\n        while (day < 1) {\n            month--;\n            if (month < 1) { month = 12; year--; }\n            day += daysInMonth();\n        }\n    }\npublic:\n    Date(int d = 1, int m = 1, int y = 2000) : day(d), month(m), year(y) { normalize(); }\n    Date& operator++() { day++; normalize(); return *this; }\n    Date operator++(int) { Date temp = *this; ++(*this); return temp; }\n    Date& operator--() { day--; normalize(); return *this; }\n    Date operator--(int) { Date temp = *this; --(*this); return temp; }\n    int operator-(const Date& other) const { // разница в днях (упрощённо)\n        return (year - other.year) * 365 + (month - other.month) * 30 + (day - other.day);\n    }\n    bool operator==(const Date& other) const { return day==other.day && month==other.month && year==other.year; }\n    bool operator!=(const Date& other) const { return !(*this == other); }\n    bool operator<(const Date& other) const {\n        if (year != other.year) return year < other.year;\n        if (month != other.month) return month < other.month;\n        return day < other.day;\n    }\n    bool operator>(const Date& other) const { return other < *this; }\n    friend ostream& operator<<(ostream& os, const Date& d) {\n        return os << d.day << '/' << d.month << '/' << d.year;\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    Date d1(15, 1, 2023), d2(20, 1, 2023);\n    cout << \"d1: \" << d1 << endl;\n    cout << \"d2: \" << d2 << endl;\n    ++d1;\n    cout << \"++d1: \" << d1 << endl;\n    --d2;\n    cout << \"--d2: \" << d2 << endl;\n    cout << \"d1 - d2: \" << (d1 - d2) << \" days\" << endl;\n    cout << \"d1 < d2: \" << (d1 < d2) << endl;\n    return 0;\n}

#include <sys/inotify.h>\n#include <unistd.h>\n#include <iostream>\n#include <cstring>\n#include <limits.h>\nusing namespace std;\n\nint main() {\n    int fd = inotify_init();\n    if(fd == -1) {\n        perror(\"inotify_init\");\n        return 1;\n    }\n    \n    int wd = inotify_add_watch(fd, \".\", IN_MODIFY | IN_CREATE | IN_DELETE | IN_ATTRIB);\n    if(wd == -1) {\n        perror(\"inotify_add_watch\");\n        close(fd);\n        return 1;\n    }\n    \n    cout << \"Monitoring current directory...\" << endl;\n    \n    const size_t EVENT_SIZE = sizeof(struct inotify_event);\n    const size_t BUFFER_SIZE = (EVENT_SIZE + NAME_MAX + 1) * 16;\n    char buffer[BUFFER_SIZE];\n    \n    while(true) {\n        ssize_t len = read(fd, buffer, BUFFER_SIZE);\n        if(len == -1) {\n            perror(\"read\");\n            break;\n        }\n        \n        ssize_t i = 0;\n        while(i < len) {\n            struct inotify_event* event = (struct inotify_event*)(buffer + i);\n            \n            if(event->mask & IN_CREATE) {\n                cout << \"File created: \" << event->name << endl;\n            } \n            if(event->mask & IN_MODIFY) {\n                cout << \"File modified: \" << event->name << endl;\n            } \n            if(event->mask & IN_DELETE) {\n                cout << \"File deleted: \" << event->name << endl;\n            }\n            if(event->mask & IN_ATTRIB) {\n                cout << \"File attributes changed: \" << event->name << endl;\n            }\n            \n            i += EVENT_SIZE + event->len;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    inotify_rm_watch(fd, wd);\n    close(fd);\n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <cmath>\n\nstruct Triangle {\n    double sideA, sideB, sideC;\n    \n    bool isRightAngled() const {\n        double a2 = sideA * sideA;\n        double b2 = sideB * sideB;\n        double c2 = sideC * sideC;\n        \n        return (std::abs(a2 + b2 - c2) < 0.001) ||\n               (std::abs(a2 + c2 - b2) < 0.001) ||\n               (std::abs(b2 + c2 - a2) < 0.001);\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    Triangle triangle1 = {3, 4, 5};\n    Triangle triangle2 = {5, 5, 5};\n    \n    std::cout << \"Треугольник 3-4-5 прямоугольный: \" << (triangle1.isRightAngled() ? \"да\" : \"нет\") << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"Треугольник 5-5-5 прямоугольный: \" << (triangle2.isRightAngled() ? \"да\" : \"нет\") << std::endl;\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <vector>\nusing namespace std;\n\nint removeDuplicates(vector<int>& nums) {\n    if (nums.empty()) return 0;\n    int k = 1;\n    for (int i = 1; i < nums.size(); i++) {\n        if (nums[i] != nums[i - 1]) {\n            nums[k] = nums[i];\n            k++;\n        }\n    }\n    return k;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    vector<int> nums = {0,0,1,1,1,2,2,3,3,4};\n    int newLength = removeDuplicates(nums);\n    cout << \"New length: \" << newLength << endl;\n    for (int i = 0; i < newLength; i++) cout << nums[i] << \" \";\n    cout << endl;\n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <vector>\n\nclass UnionFind {\n    std::vector<int> parent, rank;\npublic:\n    UnionFind(int n) {\n        parent.resize(n);\n        rank.resize(n, 0);\n        for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {\n            parent[i] = i;\n        }\n    }\n    int find(int x) {\n        if (parent[x] != x) {\n            parent[x] = find(parent[x]);\n        }\n        return parent[x];\n    }\n    void unite(int x, int y) {\n        int rootX = find(x);\n        int rootY = find(y);\n        if (rootX == rootY) return;\n        if (rank[rootX] < rank[rootY]) {\n            parent[rootX] = rootY;\n        } else if (rank[rootX] > rank[rootY]) {\n            parent[rootY] = rootX;\n        } else {\n            parent[rootY] = rootX;\n            rank[rootX]++;\n        }\n    }\n    bool connected(int x, int y) {\n        return find(x) == find(y);\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    UnionFind uf(5);\n    uf.unite(0, 1);\n    uf.unite(1, 2);\n    std::cout << \"0 и 2 соединены? \" << (uf.connected(0, 2) ? \"Да\" : \"Нет\") << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"0 и 3 соединены? \" << (uf.connected(0, 3) ? \"Да\" : \"Нет\") << std::endl;\n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <string>\nusing namespace std;\n\nclass InventoryItem {\nprivate:\n    int id;\n    string name;\n    int stock; // текущий запас\n    int reorderLevel; // уровень для повторного заказа\n    \npublic:\n    InventoryItem(int itemId, string itemName, int initialStock, int reorder = 5) \n        : id(itemId), name(itemName), stock(initialStock), reorderLevel(reorder) {\n        if (stock < 0) stock = 0;\n        if (reorderLevel < 0) reorderLevel = 0;\n    }\n    \n    bool sell(int quantity) {\n        if (quantity <= 0) {\n            cout << \"Количество должно быть положительным\" << endl;\n            return false;\n        }\n        if (quantity > stock) {\n            cout << \"Недостаточно товара на складе. Доступно: \" << stock << endl;\n            return false;\n        }\n        stock -= quantity;\n        cout << \"Продано \" << quantity << \" единиц товара '\" << name << \"'\" << endl;\n        checkReorderNeed();\n        return true;\n    }\n    \n    void restock(int quantity) {\n        if (quantity > 0) {\n            stock += quantity;\n            cout << \"Запас пополнен на \" << quantity << \" единиц. Теперь: \" << stock << endl;\n        } else {\n            cout << \"Количество для пополнения должно быть положительным\" << endl;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    void checkReorderNeed() const {\n        if (stock <= reorderLevel) {\n            cout << \"ВНИМАНИЕ: Товар '\" << name << \"' (ID: \" << id \n                 << \") требует заказа! Запас: \" << stock \n                 << \", уровень заказа: \" << reorderLevel << endl;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    void setReorderLevel(int newLevel) {\n        if (newLevel >= 0) {\n            reorderLevel = newLevel;\n            cout << \"Уровень заказа для товара '\" << name << \"' установлен в \" << newLevel << endl;\n            checkReorderNeed();\n        } else {\n            cout << \"Уровень заказа не может быть отрицательным\" << endl;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    void printInfo() const {\n        cout << \"ID: \" << id << endl;\n        cout << \"Наименование: \" << name << endl;\n        cout << \"Текущий запас: \" << stock << endl;\n        cout << \"Уровень для заказа: \" << reorderLevel << endl;\n        cout << \"Требуется заказ? \" << (stock <= reorderLevel ? \"Да\" : \"Нет\") << endl;\n    }\n    \n    int getId() const { return id; }\n    string getName() const { return name; }\n    int getStock() const { return stock; }\n    int getReorderLevel() const { return reorderLevel; }\n    \n    bool isLowStock() const {\n        return stock <= reorderLevel;\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    InventoryItem item1(101, \"Молоток\", 10, 3);\n    item1.printInfo();\n    \n    item1.sell(5);\n    item1.sell(4); // после этой продажи запас опустится до 1, что ниже уровня заказа\n    \n    item1.restock(20);\n    item1.printInfo();\n    \n    item1.setReorderLevel(10);\n    item1.sell(15); // запас опустится ниже нового уровня заказа\n    \n    InventoryItem item2(102, \"Гвозди\", 2, 5);\n    item2.printInfo(); // сразу показывает необходимость заказа\n    \n    // Попытка продать больше, чем есть\n    item2.sell(5);\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <sys/types.h>\n#include <sys/socket.h>\n#include <netinet/in.h>\n#include <arpa/inet.h>\n#include <unistd.h>\n#include <iostream>\n#include <cstring>\nvoid handle_tcp(int client_fd) {\n    const char* msg = \"TCP response\\n\";\n    send(client_fd, msg, strlen(msg), 0);\n    close(client_fd);\n}\nvoid handle_udp(int udp_fd) {\n    char buffer[1024];\n    sockaddr_in client_addr;\n    socklen_t len = sizeof(client_addr);\n    recvfrom(udp_fd, buffer, sizeof(buffer), 0, (struct sockaddr*)&client_addr, &len);\n    const char* msg = \"UDP response\\n\";\n    sendto(udp_fd, msg, strlen(msg), 0, (struct sockaddr*)&client_addr, len);\n}\nint main() {\n    int tcp_fd = socket(AF_INET, SOCK_STREAM, 0);\n    int udp_fd = socket(AF_INET, SOCK_DGRAM, 0);\n    sockaddr_in addr;\n    addr.sin_family = AF_INET;\n    addr.sin_port = htons(8888);\n    addr.sin_addr.s_addr = INADDR_ANY;\n    bind(tcp_fd, (struct sockaddr*)&addr, sizeof(addr));\n    bind(udp_fd, (struct sockaddr*)&addr, sizeof(addr));\n    listen(tcp_fd, 5);\n    if(fork() == 0) {\n        close(tcp_fd);\n        handle_udp(udp_fd);\n        exit(0);\n    }\n    std::cout << \"Server listening on TCP/UDP port 8888\" << std::endl;\n    while(true) {\n        int client_fd = accept(tcp_fd, NULL, NULL);\n        if(fork() == 0) {\n            close(udp_fd);\n            close(tcp_fd);\n            handle_tcp(client_fd);\n            exit(0);\n        }\n        close(client_fd);\n    }\n    close(tcp_fd);\n    close(udp_fd);\n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <filesystem>\n#include <string>\n#include <vector>\n#include <regex>\n#include <chrono>\n#include <iomanip>\n#include <ctime>\nusing namespace std;\nnamespace fs = filesystem;\n\nclass FileSearcher {\n    vector<fs::path> results;\n    \n    bool matchPattern(const string& filename, const string& pattern) {\n        // Преобразуем шаблон с * и ? в regex\n        string regex_pattern;\n        for (char c : pattern) {\n            if (c == '*') {\n                regex_pattern += \".*\";\n            } else if (c == '?') {\n                regex_pattern += \".\";\n            } else if (c == '.' || c == '(' || c == ')' || c == '[' || c == ']' || \n                       c == '{' || c == '}' || c == '\\\\' || c == '^' || c == '$' || \n                       c == '|' || c == '+' || c == '*') {\n                regex_pattern += '\\\\';\n                regex_pattern += c;\n            } else {\n                regex_pattern += c;\n            }\n        }\n        \n        regex re(regex_pattern, regex::icase);\n        return regex_match(filename, re);\n    }\n    \n    void searchRecursive(const fs::path& dir, const string& pattern, bool recursive) {\n        try {\n            for (const auto& entry : fs::directory_iterator(dir)) {\n                if (entry.is_regular_file()) {\n                    if (matchPattern(entry.path().filename().string(), pattern)) {\n                        results.push_back(entry.path());\n                    }\n                } else if (recursive && entry.is_directory()) {\n                    searchRecursive(entry.path(), pattern, recursive);\n                }\n            }\n        } catch (const fs::filesystem_error& e) {\n            cerr << \"Error accessing \" << dir << \": \" << e.what() << endl;\n        }\n    }\n    \npublic:\n    void search(const string& start_dir, const string& pattern, bool recursive = true) {\n        results.clear();\n        searchRecursive(start_dir, pattern, recursive);\n    }\n    \n    void printResults(bool show_details = false) {\n        if (results.empty()) {\n            cout << \"No files found.\" << endl;\n            return;\n        }\n        \n        cout << \"Found \" << results.size() << \" file(s):\" << endl;\n        \n        for (const auto& path : results) {\n            if (show_details) {\n                try {\n                    auto ftime = fs::last_write_time(path);\n                    auto size = fs::file_size(path);\n                    \n                    // Преобразуем время файла\n                    auto sctp = chrono::time_point_cast<chrono::system_clock::duration>(\n                        ftime - fs::file_time_type::clock::now() + chrono::system_clock::now());\n                    time_t cftime = chrono::system_clock::to_time_t(sctp);\n                    \n                    cout << put_time(localtime(&cftime), \"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S\") << \"  \";\n                    cout << setw(10) << size << \" bytes  \";\n                } catch (...) {\n                    cout << \"[Error accessing info]  \";\n                }\n            }\n            cout << path << endl;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    const vector<fs::path>& getResults() const {\n        return results;\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    FileSearcher searcher;\n    \n    cout << \"Searching for *.txt files...\" << endl;\n    searcher.search(\".\", \"*.txt\", true);\n    searcher.printResults(true);\n    \n    cout << endl << \"Searching for test*.cpp files...\" << endl;\n    searcher.search(\".\", \"test*.cpp\", true);\n    searcher.printResults(false);\n    \n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n\nclass Date {\n    int day, month, year;\n    bool isLeap() const { return (year % 4 == 0 && year % 100 != 0) || (year % 400 == 0); }\n    int daysInMonth() const {\n        int days[] = {31,28,31,30,31,30,31,31,30,31,30,31};\n        if(month == 2 && isLeap()) return 29;\n        return days[month - 1];\n    }\n    void normalize() {\n        while(day > daysInMonth()) {\n            day -= daysInMonth();\n            month++;\n            if(month > 12) { month = 1; year++; }\n        }\n        while(day < 1) {\n            month--;\n            if(month < 1) { month = 12; year--; }\n            day += daysInMonth();\n        }\n    }\npublic:\n    Date(int d = 1, int m = 1, int y = 2000) : day(d), month(m), year(y) { normalize(); }\n    Date& operator++() { day++; normalize(); return *this; }\n    Date operator++(int) { Date temp = *this; ++(*this); return temp; }\n    Date& operator--() { day--; normalize(); return *this; }\n    Date operator--(int) { Date temp = *this; --(*this); return temp; }\n    Date& operator+=(int days) { for(int i = 0; i < days; i++) ++(*this); return *this; }\n    Date& operator-=(int days) { for(int i = 0; i < days; i++) --(*this); return *this; }\n    int operator-(const Date& other) const { // разница в днях (упрощенно)\n        return (year - other.year) * 365 + (month - other.month) * 30 + (day - other.day);\n    }\n    friend std::ostream& operator<<(std::ostream& os, const Date& d) {\n        return os << d.day << \"/\" << d.month << \"/\" << d.year;\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    Date d(15, 1, 2023);\n    std::cout << \"Initial: \" << d << std::endl;\n    ++d;\n    std::cout << \"After ++: \" << d << std::endl;\n    d += 10;\n    std::cout << \"After += 10: \" << d << std::endl;\n    Date d2(1, 2, 2023);\n    std::cout << \"Difference: \" << (d2 - d) << \" days\" << std::endl;\n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <vector>\n#include <stdexcept>\n#include <cmath>\n#include <algorithm>\n\nclass PolynomialException : public std::runtime_error {\npublic:\n    PolynomialException(const std::string& msg) : std::runtime_error(msg) {}\n};\n\nclass Polynomial {\nprivate:\n    std::vector<double> coefficients;  // coefficients[i] = коэффициент при x^i\n    \n    void normalize() {\n        // Удаляем нулевые старшие коэффициенты\n        while (!coefficients.empty() && std::fabs(coefficients.back()) < 1e-10) {\n            coefficients.pop_back();\n        }\n    }\n    \npublic:\n    Polynomial(const std::vector<double>& coeffs) : coefficients(coeffs) {\n        if (coeffs.empty()) {\n            throw std::invalid_argument(\"Polynomial must have at least one coefficient\");\n        }\n        normalize();\n        if (coefficients.empty()) {\n            coefficients.push_back(0);  // Нулевой многочлен\n        }\n    }\n    \n    int degree() const {\n        return coefficients.size() - 1;\n    }\n    \n    double evaluate(double x) const {\n        if (coefficients.empty()) {\n            return 0;\n        }\n        \n        double result = 0;\n        double power = 1;\n        \n        for (double coeff : coefficients) {\n            result += coeff * power;\n            power *= x;\n            \n            if (std::isinf(result) || std::isnan(result)) {\n                throw std::overflow_error(\"Polynomial evaluation overflow\");\n            }\n        }\n        \n        return result;\n    }\n    \n    Polynomial add(const Polynomial& other) const {\n        size_t max_size = std::max(coefficients.size(), other.coefficients.size());\n        std::vector<double> result_coeffs(max_size, 0);\n        \n        for (size_t i = 0; i < max_size; i++) {\n            double coeff1 = (i < coefficients.size()) ? coefficients[i] : 0;\n            double coeff2 = (i < other.coefficients.size()) ? other.coefficients[i] : 0;\n            result_coeffs[i] = coeff1 + coeff2;\n            \n            if (std::isinf(result_coeffs[i]) || std::isnan(result_coeffs[i])) {\n                throw std::overflow_error(\"Polynomial addition overflow\");\n            }\n        }\n        \n        return Polynomial(result_coeffs);\n    }\n    \n    Polynomial derivative() const {\n        if (coefficients.size() <= 1) {\n            return Polynomial({0});\n        }\n        \n        std::vector<double> deriv_coeffs(coefficients.size() - 1);\n        for (size_t i = 1; i < coefficients.size(); i++) {\n            deriv_coeffs[i-1] = coefficients[i] * i;\n            \n            if (std::isinf(deriv_coeffs[i-1]) || std::isnan(deriv_coeffs[i-1])) {\n                throw std::overflow_error(\"Polynomial derivative overflow\");\n            }\n        }\n        \n        return Polynomial(deriv_coeffs);\n    }\n    \n    Polynomial multiply(const Polynomial& other) const {\n        if (coefficients.empty() || other.coefficients.empty()) {\n            return Polynomial({0});\n        }\n        \n        size_t result_size = coefficients.size() + other.coefficients.size() - 1;\n        std::vector<double> result_coeffs(result_size, 0);\n        \n        for (size_t i = 0; i < coefficients.size(); i++) {\n            for (size_t j = 0; j < other.coefficients.size(); j++) {\n                result_coeffs[i + j] += coefficients[i] * other.coefficients[j];\n                \n                if (std::isinf(result_coeffs[i + j]) || std::isnan(result_coeffs[i + j])) {\n                    throw std::overflow_error(\"Polynomial multiplication overflow\");\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        \n        return Polynomial(result_coeffs);\n    }\n    \n    void print() const {\n        if (coefficients.empty()) {\n            std::cout << \"0\";\n            return;\n        }\n        \n        bool first_term = true;\n        for (int i = degree(); i >= 0; i--) {\n            double coeff = coefficients[i];\n            if (std::fabs(coeff) < 1e-10) continue;\n            \n            if (!first_term) {\n                std::cout << (coeff >= 0 ? \" + \" : \" - \");\n            }\n            \n            if (i == 0 || std::fabs(std::fabs(coeff) - 1.0) > 1e-10) {\n                std::cout << std::fabs(coeff);\n            }\n            \n            if (i > 0) {\n                std::cout << \"x\";\n                if (i > 1) {\n                    std::cout << \"^\" << i;\n                }\n            }\n            \n            first_term = false;\n        }\n        \n        if (first_term) {\n            std::cout << \"0\";\n        }\n    }\n    \n    double root_newton(double initial_guess, double tolerance = 1e-10, int max_iterations = 1000) {\n        if (coefficients.size() <= 1) {\n            throw PolynomialException(\"Cannot find root of constant polynomial\");\n        }\n        \n        Polynomial deriv = derivative();\n        double x = initial_guess;\n        \n        for (int iter = 0; iter < max_iterations; iter++) {\n            double fx = evaluate(x);\n            double fpx = deriv.evaluate(x);\n            \n            if (std::fabs(fpx) < tolerance) {\n                throw PolynomialException(\"Derivative is zero, Newton's method fails\");\n            }\n            \n            double delta = fx / fpx;\n            x = x - delta;\n            \n            if (std::isinf(x) || std::isnan(x)) {\n                throw std::overflow_error(\"Newton's method overflow\");\n            }\n            \n            if (std::fabs(delta) < tolerance) {\n                return x;\n            }\n        }\n        \n        throw PolynomialException(\"Newton's method did not converge\");\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    try {\n        Polynomial p1({1, -3, 2});  // x^2 - 3x + 2\n        Polynomial p2({0, 2, -1});  // -x^2 + 2x\n        \n        std::cout << \"P1(x) = \";\n        p1.print();\n        std::cout << std::endl;\n        \n        std::cout << \"P2(x) = \";\n        p2.print();\n        std::cout << std::endl;\n        \n        std::cout << \"P1(2) = \" << p1.evaluate(2) << std::endl;\n        \n        Polynomial sum = p1.add(p2);\n        std::cout << \"P1 + P2 = \";\n        sum.print();\n        std::cout << std::endl;\n        \n        Polynomial deriv = p1.derivative();\n        std::cout << \"P1'(x) = \";\n        deriv.print();\n        std::cout << std::endl;\n        \n        double root = p1.root_newton(1.5);\n        std::cout << \"Root near 1.5: \" << root << std::endl;\n        \n        Polynomial empty_poly({});  // This will throw\n        \n    } catch (const PolynomialException& e) {\n        std::cout << \"Polynomial error: \" << e.what() << std::endl;\n    } catch (const std::invalid_argument& e) {\n        std::cout << \"Invalid argument: \" << e.what() << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    return 0;\n}

{\n    static std::map<std::type_index, size_t> allocations;\n    static std::map<std::type_index, size_t> deallocations;\n    static std::map<std::type_index, size_t> currentCount;\n    \npublic:\n    template<typename T>\n    static void* allocate(size_t size) {\n        void* ptr = malloc(size);\n        if (ptr) {\n            std::type_index ti = typeid(T);\n            allocations[ti]++;\n            currentCount[ti]++;\n            std::cout << \"Allocated \" << size << \" bytes for type: \" << ti.name() \n                 << \" (total allocations: \" << allocations[ti] << \")\" << typeid(T);\n            deallocations[ti]++;\n            currentCount[ti]--;\n            std::cout << \"Deallocated \" << size << \" bytes for type: \" << ti.name() << std::endl;\n Currently allocated: \" << currCount << std::endl;\n            if (allocCount > deallocCount) {\n                std::cout << \"  WARNING: Potential memory leak!\" << std::endl;\n            }\n std::endl;\n    }\n};\n\nstd::map<std::type_index, size_t> TypeAwareAllocator::allocations;\nstd::map<std::type_index, size_t> TypeAwareAllocator::deallocations;\nstd::map<std::type_index, size_t> #include <iostream>\nusing namespace std;\n\nclass Counter {\nprivate:\n    int count;\n    int minValue;\n    int maxValue;\n    \npublic:\n    Counter(int initial = 0, int min = 0, int max = 100) \n        : count(initial), minValue(min), maxValue(max) {\n        if (count < minValue) count = minValue;\n        if (count > maxValue) count = maxValue;\n    }\n    \n    void increment() {\n        if (count < maxValue) {\n            count++;\n            cout << \"Увеличили до: \" << count << endl;\n        } else {\n            cout << \"Достигнут максимум (\" << maxValue << \")\" << endl;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    void decrement() {\n        if (count > minValue) {\n            count--;\n            cout << \"Уменьшили до: \" << count << endl;\n        } else {\n            cout << \"Достигнут минимум (\" << minValue << \")\" << endl;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    void reset() {\n        count = minValue;\n        cout << \"Сброшено к минимальному значению: \" << count << endl;\n    }\n    \n    void setValue(int newValue) {\n        if (newValue >= minValue && newValue <= maxValue) {\n            count = newValue;\n            cout << \"Установлено значение: \" << count << endl;\n        } else {\n            cout << \"Значение должно быть в диапазоне [\" \n                 << minValue << \", \" << maxValue << \"]\" << endl;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    void print() const {\n        cout << \"Текущее значение: \" << count \n             << \" (диапазон [\" << minValue << \", \" << maxValue << \"]) \" << endl;\n    }\n    \n    int getCount() const { return count; }\n    int getMin() const { return minValue; }\n    int getMax() const { return maxValue; }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    Counter c(5, 0, 10);\n    c.print();\n    \n    c.increment();\n    c.increment();\n    c.decrement();\n    \n    // Попытка выйти за пределы\n    for (int i = 0; #include <iostream>\n#include <string>\n#include <vector>\n#include <queue>\n#include <unordered_map>\nusing namespace std;\n\nstruct TrieNode {\n    unordered_map<char, TrieNode*> children;\n    TrieNode* fail = nullptr;\n    vector<int> output;\n};\n\nvoid insertTrie(TrieNode* root, const string& word, int index) {\n    TrieNode* node = root;\n    for (char c : word) {\n        if (!node->children[c]) {\n            node->children[c] = new TrieNode();\n        }\n        node = node->children[c];\n    }\n    node->output.push_back(index);\n}\n\nvoid buildFailureLinks(TrieNode* root) {\n    queue<TrieNode*> q;\n    for (auto& pair : root->children) {\n        pair.second->fail = root;\n        q.push(pair.second);\n    }\n    while (!q.empty()) {\n        TrieNode* current = q.front(); q.pop();\n        for (auto& pair : current->children) {\n            char ch = pair.first;\n            TrieNode* child = pair.second;\n            TrieNode* failNode = current->fail;\n            while (failNode && !failNode->children[ch]) {\n                failNode = failNode->fail;\n            }\n            child->fail = (failNode) ? failNode->children[ch] : root;\n            child->output.insert(child->output.end(), child->fail->output.begin(), child->fail->output.end());\n            q.push(child);\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nvector<pair<int, int>> ahoCorasickSearch(const string& text, TrieNode* root, const vector<string>& patterns) {\n    vector<pair<int, int>> results;\n    TrieNode* current = root;\n    for (int i = 0; i < text.length(); ++i) {\n        char c = text[i];\n        while (current && !current->children[c]) {\n            current = current->fail;\n        }\n        current = (current) ? current->children[c] : root;\n        for (int patternIndex : current->output) {\n            results.push_back({i - patterns[patternIndex].length() + 1, patternIndex});\n        }\n    }\n    return results;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    string text = \"ushers\";\n    vector<string> patterns = {\"he\", \"she\", \"his\", \"hers\"};\n    TrieNode* root = new TrieNode();\n    for (int i = 0; i < patterns.size(); ++i) {\n        insertTrie(root, patterns[i], i);\n    }\n    buildFailureLinks(root);\n    auto matches = ahoCorasickSearch(text, root, patterns);\n    cout << \"Текст: \" << text << endl;\n    cout << \"Найденные шаблоны:\" << endl;\n    for (auto& match : matches) {\n        cout << \"  Шаблон '\" << patterns[match.second] << \"' на позиции \" << match.first << endl;\n    }\n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <future>\n#include <vector>\n#include <numeric>\n#include <chrono>\n#include <algorithm>\n\nvoid process_chunk(const std::vector<int>& data, size_t start, size_t end, \n                   std::promise<int>&& prom) {\n    int sum = std::accumulate(data.begin() + start, data.begin() + end, 0);\n    prom.set_value(sum);\n}\n\nint main() {\n    std::vector<int> data(1000000);\n    std::iota(data.begin(), data.end(), 1);\n    \n    const size_t num_chunks = 4;\n    const size_t chunk_size = data.size() / num_chunks;\n    \n    std::vector<std::future<int>> futures;\n    std::vector<std::thread> threads;\n    \n    auto start = std::chrono::high_resolution_clock::now();\n    \n    for (size_t i = 0; i < num_chunks; i++) {\n        size_t start_idx = i * chunk_size;\n        size_t end_idx = (i == num_chunks - 1) ? data.size() : start_idx + chunk_size;\n        \n        std::promise<int> prom;\n        futures.push_back(prom.get_future());\n        \n        threads.emplace_back(process_chunk, std::cref(data), start_idx, end_idx, \n                            std::move(prom));\n    }\n    \n    int total_sum = 0;\n    for (auto& fut : futures) {\n        total_sum += fut.get();\n    }\n    \n    for (auto& t : threads) {\n        t.join();\n    }\n    \n    auto end = std::chrono::high_resolution_clock::now();\n    auto duration = std::chrono::duration_cast<std::chrono::milliseconds>(end - start);\n    \n    std::cout << \"Общая сумма: \" << total_sum << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"Время выполнения: \" << duration.count() << \" мс\" << std::endl;\n    \n    // Альтернатива с std::async\n    std::vector<std::future<int>> async_futures;\n    start = std::chrono::high_resolution_clock::now();\n    \n    for (size_t i = 0; i < num_chunks; i++) {\n        size_t start_idx = i * chunk_size;\n        size_t end_idx = (i == num_chunks - 1) ? data.size() : start_idx + chunk_size;\n        \n        async_futures.push_back(std::async(std::launch::async, [&data, start_idx, end_idx]() {\n            return std::accumulate(data.begin() + start_idx, data.begin() + end_idx, 0);\n        }));\n    }\n    \n    total_sum = 0;\n    for (auto& fut : async_futures) {\n        total_sum += fut.get();\n    }\n    \n    end = std::chrono::high_resolution_clock::now();\n    duration = std::chrono::duration_cast<std::chrono::milliseconds>(end - start);\n    \n    std::cout << \"Сумма через async: \" << total_sum << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"Время выполнения async: \" << duration.count() << \" мс\" << std::endl;\n    \n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n\nint main() {\n    int size = 8;\n    int* arr = new int[size] {10, 22, 9, 33, 21, 50, 41, 60};\n    int* lengths = new int[size] {};\n    int maxLength = 0;\n    for(int i = 0; i < size; i++) {\n        lengths[i] = 1;\n        for(int j = 0; j < i; j++) {\n            if(arr[i] > arr[j] && lengths[i] < lengths[j] + 1) {\n                lengths[i] = lengths[j] + 1;\n            }\n        }\n        if(lengths[i] > maxLength) maxLength = lengths[i];\n    }\n    std::cout << \"Длина самой длинной возрастающей подпоследовательности: \" << maxLength << std::endl;\n    delete[] arr;\n    delete[] lengths;\n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <string>\n\nclass Date {\n    int day, month, year;\n    \n    bool isValidDate(int d, int m, int y) const {\n        if(y < 1900 || y > 2100) return false;\n        if(m < 1 || m > 12) return false;\n        \n        int daysInMonth[] = {31, (isLeapYear(y) ? 29 : 28), 31, 30, 31, 30, 31, 31, 30, 31, 30, 31};\n        if(d < 1 || d > daysInMonth[m-1]) return false;\n        \n        return true;\n    }\n    \n    bool isLeapYear(int y) const {\n        return (y % 4 == 0 && y % 100 != 0) || (y % 400 == 0);\n    }\n    \npublic:\n    Date() : day(1), month(1), year(2000) {\n        std::cout << \"Дата по умолчанию: \" << toString() << \" создана\" << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    Date(int d, int m, int y) {\n        if(isValidDate(d, m, y)) {\n            day = d; month = m; year = y;\n        } else {\n            std::cout << \"Некорректная дата, установлена дата по умолчанию\" << std::endl;\n            day = 1; month = 1; year = 2000;\n        }\n        std::cout << \"Дата \" << toString() << \" создана\" << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    ~Date() {\n        std::cout << \"Дата \" << toString() << \" разрушена\" << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    void setDate(int d, int m, int y) {\n        if(isValidDate(d, m, y)) {\n            day = d; month = m; year = y;\n            std::cout << \"Дата установлена: \" << toString() << std::endl;\n        } else {\n            std::cout << \"Ошибка: некорректная дата\" << std::endl;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    void addDays(int days) {\n        // Упрощенная реализация\n        day += days;\n        while(day > 31) {\n            day -= 31;\n            month++;\n            if(month > 12) {\n                month = 1;\n                year++;\n            }\n        }\n        std::cout << \"После добавления \" << days << \" дней: \" << toString() << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    std::string toString() const {\n        return std::to_string(day) + \".\" + std::to_string(month) + \".\" + std::to_string(year);\n    }\n    \n    bool isLeapYear() const {\n        return isLeapYear(year);\n    }\n    \n    void display() const {\n        std::cout << \"Дата: \" << toString() << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"Високосный год: \" << (isLeapYear() ? \"Да\" : \"Нет\") << std::endl;\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    Date d1;\n    Date d2(25, 12, 2023);\n    Date d3(31, 2, 2023); // Некорректная дата\n    \n    d1.display();\n    std::cout << std::endl;\n    d2.display();\n    \n    d2.addDays(10);\n    d2.setDate(15, 6, 2024);\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <string>\n#include <memory>\n\nclass Implementor {\npublic:\n    virtual void operationImpl() = 0;\n    virtual ~Implementor() = default;\n};\n\nclass ConcreteImplementorA : public Implementor {\npublic:\n    void operationImpl() override { \n        std::cout << \"ConcreteImplementorA operation\" << std::endl; \n    }\n};\n\nclass ConcreteImplementorB : public Implementor {\npublic:\n    void operationImpl() override { \n        std::cout << \"ConcreteImplementorB operation\" << std::endl; \n    }\n};\n\nclass Abstraction {\nprotected:\n    Implementor* impl;\npublic:\n    Abstraction(Implementor* i) : impl(i) {}\n    virtual void operation() {\n        impl->operationImpl();\n    }\n    virtual ~Abstraction() = default;\n};\n\nclass RefinedAbstraction : public Abstraction {\npublic:\n    RefinedAbstraction(Implementor* i) : Abstraction(i) {}\n    \n    void operation() override {\n        std::cout << \"[RefinedAbstraction] calling: \";\n        Abstraction::operation();\n    }\n    \n    void extendedOperation() {\n        std::cout << \"[RefinedAbstraction] extended operation with: \";\n        impl->operationImpl();\n    }\n};\n\nclass AnotherAbstraction : public Abstraction {\npublic:\n    AnotherAbstraction(Implementor* i) : Abstraction(i) {}\n    \n    void operation() override {\n        std::cout << \"[AnotherAbstraction] enhanced: \";\n        for (int i = 0; i < 2; ++i) {\n            impl->operationImpl();\n        }\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    std::cout << \"=== Bridge Pattern Demonstration ===\" << std::endl;\n    \n    ConcreteImplementorA implA;\n    ConcreteImplementorB implB;\n    \n    // Разные абстракции с разными реализациями\n    std::cout << \"\\n1. RefinedAbstraction with ImplementorA:\" << std::endl;\n    RefinedAbstraction refinedA(&implA);\n    refinedA.operation();\n    refinedA.extendedOperation();\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\n2. RefinedAbstraction with ImplementorB:\" << std::endl;\n    RefinedAbstraction refinedB(&implB);\n    refinedB.operation();\n    refinedB.extendedOperation();\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\n3. AnotherAbstraction with ImplementorA:\" << std::endl;\n    AnotherAbstraction anotherA(&implA);\n    anotherA.operation();\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\n4. AnotherAbstraction with ImplementorB:\" << std::endl;\n    AnotherAbstraction anotherB(&implB);\n    anotherB.operation();\n    \n    // Демонстрация замены реализации в рантайме\n    std::cout << \"\\n5. Runtime implementation switching:\" << std::endl;\n    RefinedAbstraction dynamicAbstraction(&implA);\n    dynamicAbstraction.operation();\n    \n    // Меняем реализацию (создаем новый объект)\n    RefinedAbstraction dynamicAbstraction2(&implB);\n    dynamicAbstraction2.operation();\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <fstream>\n#include <string>\n#include <sstream>\n#include <vector>\n#include <map>\n#include <cctype>\n\nstd::string escapeJson(const std::string& s) {\n    std::ostringstream oss;\n    for (char c : s) {\n        switch (c) {\n            case '\"': oss << \"\\\\\\\"\"; break;\n            case '\\\\': oss << \"\\\\\\\\\"; break;\n            case '\\b': oss << \"\\\\b\"; break;\n            case '\\f': oss << \"\\\\f\"; break;\n            case '\\n': oss << \"\\\\n\"; break;\n            case '\\r': oss << \"\\\\r\"; break;\n            case '\\t': oss << \"\\\\t\"; break;\n            default: oss << c;\n        }\n    }\n    return oss.str();\n}\n\nint main() {\n    std::ifstream csv(\"data.csv\");\n    std::ofstream json(\"output.json\");\n    std::string line;\n    std::vector<std::string> headers;\n    \n    // Читаем заголовки\n    if (std::getline(csv, line)) {\n        std::stringstream ss(line);\n        std::string header;\n        while (std::getline(ss, header, ',')) {\n            headers.push_back(header);\n        }\n    }\n    \n    json << \"[\\n\";\n    bool first_row = true;\n    while (std::getline(csv, line)) {\n        if (!first_row) json << \",\\n\";\n        std::stringstream ss(line);\n        std::vector<std::string> values;\n        std::string value;\n        while (std::getline(ss, value, ',')) {\n            values.push_back(value);\n        }\n        \n        json << \"  {\\n\";\n        for (std::size_t i = 0; i < headers.size(); ++i) {\n            json << \"    \\\"\" << escapeJson(headers[i]) << \"\\\": \";\n            // Пытаемся определить тип значения\n            bool is_number = !values[i].empty() && \n                (std::isdigit(values[i][0]) || (values[i][0] == '-' && values[i].size() > 1 && std::isdigit(values[i][1])));\n            if (is_number) {\n                json << values[i];\n            } else {\n                json << \"\\\"\" << escapeJson(values[i]) << \"\\\"\";\n            }\n            if (i != headers.size() - 1) json << \",\";\n            json << \"\\n\";\n        }\n        json << \"  }\";\n        first_row = false;\n    }\n    json << \"\\n]\\n\";\n    \n    csv.close();\n    json.close();\n    std::cout << \"CSV to JSON conversion complete.\\n\";\n    return 0;\n}
