#include <iostream>\n#include <string>\n#include <stdexcept>\n#include <limits>\n#include <cctype>\n\nint parse_string_to_int(const std::string& str) {\n    if (str.empty()) {\n        throw std::invalid_argument(\"Input string cannot be empty\");\n    }\n    \n    // Проверяем наличие недопустимых символов\n    size_t start = 0;\n    if (str[0] == '+' || str[0] == '-') {\n        start = 1;\n    }\n    \n    for (size_t i = start; i < str.length(); i++) {\n        if (!std::isdigit(static_cast<unsigned char>(str[i]))) {\n            throw std::invalid_argument(\"String contains non-digit characters: \" + str);\n        }\n    }\n    \n    try {\n        long long result = std::stoll(str);\n        \n        // Проверка на переполнение\n        if (result < std::numeric_limits<int>::min() || result > std::numeric_limits<int>::max()) {\n            throw std::out_of_range(\"Integer value out of range for int type: \" + str);\n        }\n        \n        return static_cast<int>(result);\n    } \n    catch (const std::invalid_argument&) {\n        throw std::invalid_argument(\"Invalid integer format: \" + str);\n    }\n    catch (const std::out_of_range&) {\n        throw std::out_of_range(\"Integer value out of range: \" + str);\n    }\n}\n\nint main() {\n    try {\n        std::cout << \"Parsed: '123' -> \" << parse_string_to_int(\"123\") << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"Parsed: '-456' -> \" << parse_string_to_int(\"-456\") << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"Parsed: '+789' -> \" << parse_string_to_int(\"+789\") << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"Parsed: '' -> \" << parse_string_to_int(\"\") << std::endl;\n    } catch (const std::exception& e) {\n        std::cout << \"Error: \" << e.what() << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    try {\n        std::cout << \"Parsed: '123abc' -> \" << parse_string_to_int(\"123abc\") << std::endl;\n    } catch (const std::exception& e) {\n        std::cout << \"Error: \" << e.what() << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    try {\n        std::cout << \"Parsed: '9999999999' -> \" << parse_string_to_int(\"9999999999\") << std::endl;\n    } catch (const std::exception& e) {\n        std::cout << \"Error: \" << e.what() << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n\nclass OuterClass {\nprivate:\n    int outerValue;\n    \npublic:\n    OuterClass(int val) : outerValue(val) {}\n    \n    int getOuterValue() const { return outerValue; }\n    \n    // Декларация friend класса\n    friend class InnerClass;\n};\n\nclass InnerClass {\nprivate:\n    int& refToOuter;\n    const int& constRefToOuter;\n    int* ptrToOuter;\n    \npublic:\n    InnerClass(OuterClass& outer) \n        : refToOuter(outer.outerValue),\n          constRefToOuter(outer.getOuterValue()),\n          ptrToOuter(&outer.outerValue) {\n        \n        std::cout << \"Конструктор InnerClass\" << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"refToOuter = \" << refToOuter << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"constRefToOuter = \" << constRefToOuter << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    InnerClass(int& ref1, const int& ref2) \n        : refToOuter(ref1), constRefToOuter(ref2), ptrToOuter(nullptr) {\n        std::cout << \"Конструктор с двумя ссылками\" << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    void modifyThroughRef(int newValue) {\n        refToOuter = newValue;\n    }\n    \n    void print() const {\n        std::cout << \"refToOuter = \" << refToOuter << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"constRefToOuter = \" << constRefToOuter << std::endl;\n        if (ptrToOuter) {\n            std::cout << \"*ptrToOuter = \" << *ptrToOuter << std::endl;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    ~InnerClass() {\n        std::cout << \"Деструктор InnerClass\" << std::endl;\n    }\n};\n\nclass SelfReferential {\nprivate:\n    int value;\n    SelfReferential* selfPtr;\n    \npublic:\n    SelfReferential(int v) : value(v), selfPtr(this) {\n        std::cout << \"Создан SelfReferential со значением \" << value << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    SelfReferential& getSelf() {\n        return *this;\n    }\n    \n    void print() const {\n        std::cout << \"value = \" << value << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"selfPtr = \" << selfPtr << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"this = \" << this << std::endl;\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    OuterClass outer(42);\n    \n    std::cout << \"=== Создание InnerClass ===\" << std::endl;\n    InnerClass inner(outer);\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\nouter.getOuterValue() = \" << outer.getOuterValue() << std::endl;\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\n=== Модификация через ссылку ===\" << std::endl;\n    inner.modifyThroughRef(100);\n    \n    std::cout << \"outer.getOuterValue() после модификации = \" << outer.getOuterValue() << std::endl;\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\n=== Создание с двумя ссылками ===\" << std::endl;\n    int a = 10;\n    const int b = 20;\n    InnerClass inner2(a, b);\n    \n    inner2.modifyThroughRef(999);\n    std::cout << \"a после модификации = \" << a << std::endl;\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\n=== SelfReferential класс ===\" << std::endl;\n    SelfReferential self(777);\n    SelfReferential& selfRef = self.getSelf();\n    selfRef.print();\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\n=== Области видимости ===\" << std::endl;\n    {\n        int localVar = 123;\n        InnerClass localInner(localVar, localVar);\n    }\n    \n    return 0;\n}

Попробуйте снова.\" << endl;\n            } else {\n                cout << \"Карта заблокирована. Обратитесь в банк.\" << endl;\n                return 1;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // Главное меню\n    bool sessionActive = true;\n    while (sessionActive) {\n        cout << \"\\n===== ГЛАВНОЕ МЕНЮ =====\" << endl;\n        cout << \"1. Проверить баланс\" << endl;\n        cout << \"2. Снять наличные\" << endl;\n        cout << \"3. Внести наличные\" << endl;\n        cout << \"4. Изменить PIN-код\" << endl;\n        cout << \"5. Выход\" << endl;\n        cout << \"Выберите операцию (1-5): \";\n        \n        int choice;\n        cin >> choice;\n        \n        if (cin.fail()) {\n            cin.clear();\n            cin.ignore(numeric_limits<streamsize>::max(), '\\n');\n            cout << \"Ошибка ввода. Пожалуйста, введите число.\" << endl;\n            continue;\n        }\n        \n        switch (choice) {\n            case 1: { // Проверка баланса\n                cout << \"\\n=== Баланс ===\" << endl;\n                cout << \"Ваш текущий баланс: \" << balance << \" руб.\" << endl;\n                \n                // Условная рекомендация на основе баланса\n                if (balance < 100) {\n                    cout << \"Внимание: низкий баланс!\" << endl;\n                } else if (balance > 5000) {\n                    cout << \"Отличный баланс!\" << endl;\n                }\n                break;\n            }\n            \n            case 2: { // Снятие наличных\n                cout << \"\\n=== Снятие наличных ===\" << endl;\n                double amount;\n                cout << \"Введите сумму для снятия: \";\n                cin >> amount;\n                \n                if (amount <= 0) {\n                    cout << \"Сумма должна быть положительной.\" << endl;\n                } else if (amount > balance) {\n                    cout << \"Недостаточно средств на счете.\" << endl;\n                    cout << \"Доступно: \" << balance << \" руб.\" << endl;\n                } else {\n                    // Подтверждение через тернарный оператор\n                    char confirm;\n                    cout << \"Вы уверены, что хотите снять \" << amount << \" руб.? (y/n): \";\n                    cin >> confirm;\n                    \n                    if (confirm == 'y' || confirm == 'Y') {\n                        balance -= amount;\n                        cout << \"Операция успешна. Снято: \" << amount << \" руб.\" << endl;\n                        cout << \"Новый баланс: \" << balance << \" руб.\" << endl;\n                    } else {\n                        cout << \"Операция отменена.\" << endl;\n                    }\n                }\n                break;\n            }\n            \n            case 3: { // Внесение наличных\n                cout << \"\\n=== Внесение наличных ===\" << endl;\n                double amount;\n                cout << \"Введите сумму для внесения: \";\n                cin >> amount;\n                \n                if (amount <= 0) {\n                    cout << \"Сумма должна быть положительной.\" << endl;\n                } else if (amount > 100000) {\n                    cout << \"Сумма превышает максимальный лимит для внесения.\" << endl;\n                } else {\n                    balance += amount;\n                    cout << \"Средства успешно зачислены.\" << endl;\n                    cout << \"Новый баланс: \" << balance << \" руб.\" << endl;\n                }\n                break;\n            }\n            \n            case 4: { // Изменение PIN-кода\n                cout << \"\\n=== Изменение PIN-кода ===\" << endl;\n                string oldPin, newPin, confirmPin;\n                \n                cout << \"Введите текущий PIN-код: \";\n                cin >> oldPin;\n                \n                if (oldPin != CORRECT_PIN) {\n                    cout << \"Неверный текущий PIN-код.\" << endl;\n                    break;\n                }\n                \n                cout << \"Введите новый PIN-код (4 цифры): \";\n                cin >> newPin;\n                \n                if (newPin.length() != 4) {\n                    cout << \"PIN-код должен состоять из 4 цифр.\" << endl;\n                    break;\n                }\n                \n                // Проверка, что все символы - цифры\n                bool allDigits = true;\n                for (char c : newPin) {\n                    if (!isdigit(c)) {\n                        allDigits = false;\n                        break;\n                    }\n                }\n                \n                if (!allDigits) {\n                    cout << \"PIN-код должен содержать только цифры.\" << endl;\n                    break;\n                }\n                \n                cout << \"Подтвердите новый PIN-код: \";\n                cin >> confirmPin;\n                \n                if (newPin == confirmPin) {\n                    // В реальной системе здесь был бы код для изменения PIN\n                    cout << \"PIN-код успешно изменен!\" << endl;\n                } else {\n                    cout << \"PIN-коды не совпадают.\" << endl;\n                }\n                break;\n            }\n            \n            case 5: { // Выход\n                cout << \"\\nСпасибо за использование банкомата. До свидания!\" << endl;\n                sessionActive = false;\n                break;\n            }\n            \n            default: {\n                cout << \"Неверный выбор. Пожалуйста, выберите операцию от 1 до 5.\" << endl;\n                break;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <string>\n#include <cctype>\nusing namespace std;\n\nstring toCamelCase(const string& str) {\n    string result;\n    bool capitalizeNext = false;\n    \n    for(char c : str) {\n        if(isalpha(c)) {\n            if(result.empty()) {\n                result += tolower(c);\n            } else if(capitalizeNext) {\n                result += toupper(c);\n                capitalizeNext = false;\n            } else {\n                result += c;\n            }\n        } else if(c == ' ' || c == '_' || c == '-') {\n            capitalizeNext = true;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    return result;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    string test1 = \"hello_world_example\";\n    string test2 = \"Hello World Example\";\n    \n    cout << test1 << \" -> \" << toCamelCase(test1) << endl;\n    cout << test2 << \" -> \" << toCamelCase(test2) << endl;\n    \n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <fstream>\n#include <filesystem>\n#include <string>\n#include <vector>\n#include <ctime>\n#include <sstream>\n#include <iomanip>\n#include <cstdlib>\n#include <cstdio>\nnamespace fs = std::filesystem;\n\nclass SimpleVersionControl {\nprivate:\n    std::string repoPath;\n    \n    std::string getTimestamp() {\n        std::time_t now = std::time(nullptr);\n        std::tm* t = std::localtime(&now);\n        std::stringstream ss;\n        ss << std::put_time(t, \"%Y%m%d_%H%M%S\");\n        return ss.str();\n    }\n    \npublic:\n    SimpleVersionControl(const std::string& path) : repoPath(path) {\n        if (!fs::exists(repoPath)) {\n            fs::create_directory(repoPath);\n        }\n    }\n    \n    void commit(const std::string& filePath, const std::string& message) {\n        if (!fs::exists(filePath)) {\n            throw std::runtime_error(\"Файл не существует: \" + filePath);\n        }\n        \n        std::string timestamp = getTimestamp();\n        std::string versionDir = repoPath + \"/\" + timestamp;\n        fs::create_directory(versionDir);\n        \n        std::string destFile = versionDir + \"/\" + fs::path(filePath).filename().string();\n        fs::copy_file(filePath, destFile, fs::copy_options::overwrite_existing);\n        \n        std::ofstream infoFile(versionDir + \"/commit_info.txt\");\n        infoFile << \"Message: \" << message << std::endl;\n        infoFile << \"Timestamp: \" << timestamp << std::endl;\n        infoFile << \"Original: \" << fs::absolute(filePath).string() << std::endl;\n        infoFile.close();\n        \n        std::cout << \"Коммит создан: \" << timestamp << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"Сообщение: \" << message << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    void listVersions() {\n        std::cout << \"\\nДоступные версии:\\n\";\n        int count = 0;\n        \n        for (const auto& entry : fs::directory_iterator(repoPath)) {\n            if (fs::is_directory(entry.path())) {\n                std::string version = entry.path().filename().string();\n                \n                std::ifstream infoFile(entry.path().string() + \"/commit_info.txt\");\n                std::string line, message;\n                while (std::getline(infoFile, line)) {\n                    if (line.find(\"Message: \") == 0) {\n                        message = line.substr(9);\n                    }\n                }\n                infoFile.close();\n                \n                std::cout << ++count << \". \" << version << \" - \" << message << std::endl;\n            }\n        }\n        \n        if (count == 0) {\n            std::cout << \"Версий не найдено\" << std::endl;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    void restoreVersion(const std::string& version, const std::string& outputPath) {\n        std::string versionPath = repoPath + \"/\" + version;\n        if (!fs::exists(versionPath)) {\n            throw std::runtime_error(\"Версия не найдена: \" + version);\n        }\n        \n        for (const auto& entry : fs::directory_iterator(versionPath)) {\n            if (fs::is_regular_file(entry.path()) && \n                entry.path().extension() != \".txt\") {\n                fs::copy_file(entry.path(), outputPath, fs::copy_options::overwrite_existing);\n                std::cout << \"Версия \" << version << \" восстановлена в \" << outputPath << std::endl;\n                return;\n            }\n        }\n        \n        throw std::runtime_error(\"Файл не найден в версии\");\n    }\n    \n    void showDiff(const std::string& version1, const std::string& version2) {\n        std::string path1 = repoPath + \"/\" + version1;\n        std::string path2 = repoPath + \"/\" + version2;\n        \n        if (!fs::exists(path1) || !fs::exists(path2)) {\n            throw std::runtime_error(\"Одна из версий не найдена\");\n        }\n        \n        size_t size1 = 0, size2 = 0;\n        \n        for (const auto& entry : fs::directory_iterator(path1)) {\n            if (fs::is_regular_file(entry.path()) && \n                entry.path().extension() != \".txt\") {\n                size1 = fs::file_size(entry.path());\n                break;\n            }\n        }\n        \n        for (const auto& entry : fs::directory_iterator(path2)) {\n            if (fs::is_regular_file(entry.path()) && \n                entry.path().extension() != \".txt\") {\n                size2 = fs::file_size(entry.path());\n                break;\n            }\n        }\n        \n        std::cout << \"\\nСравнение версий:\";\n        std::cout << \"\\nВерсия \" << version1 << \": \" << size1 << \" байт\";\n        std::cout << \"\\nВерсия \" << version2 << \": \" << size2 << \" байт\";\n        \n        if (size1 == size2) {\n            std::cout << \"\\nФайлы имеют одинаковый размер\" << std::endl;\n        } else {\n            std::cout << \"\\nРазница в размере: \" << std::abs((long long)size1 - (long long)size2) \n                      << \" байт\" << std::endl;\n        }\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    SimpleVersionControl vc(\"./test_repo\");\n    \n    // Удаляем старый репозиторий если существует\n    if (fs::exists(\"./test_repo\")) {\n        fs::remove_all(\"./test_repo\");\n    }\n    \n    // Создаем тестовый файл\n    std::ofstream testFile(\"test_document.txt\");\n    testFile << \"Это тестовый документ.\\n\";\n    testFile << \"Первая версия файла.\\n\";\n    testFile.close();\n    \n    std::cout << \"=== Демонстрация системы контроля версий ===\\n\";\n    \n    // Коммит первой версии\n    vc.commit(\"test_document.txt\", \"Первая версия документа\");\n    \n    // Модифицируем файл\n    testFile.open(\"test_document.txt\", std::ios::app);\n    testFile << \"Добавлена новая строка.\\n\";\n    testFile << \"Вторая версия.\\n\";\n    testFile.close();\n    \n    // Коммит второй версии\n    vc.commit(\"test_document.txt\", \"Вторая версия с дополнениями\");\n    \n    // Показываем версии\n    vc.listVersions();\n    \n    // Сравниваем версии\n    std::cout << \"\\n=== Сравнение версий ===\";\n    \n    // Получаем список версий для сравнения\n    std::vector<std::string> versions;\n    for (const auto& entry : fs::directory_iterator(\"./test_repo\")) {\n        if (fs::is_directory(entry.path())) {\n            versions.push_back(entry.path().filename().string());\n        }\n    }\n    \n    if (versions.size() >= 2) {\n        vc.showDiff(versions[0], versions[1]);\n    }\n    \n    // Восстанавливаем первую версию\n    std::cout << \"\\n=== Восстановление версии ===\\n\";\n    if (!versions.empty()) {\n        vc.restoreVersion(versions[0], \"restored_version.txt\");\n        \n        // Показываем содержимое восстановленного файла\n        std::ifstream restored(\"restored_version.txt\");\n        std::cout << \"\\nСодержимое восстановленного файла:\\n\";\n        std::string line;\n        while (std::getline(restored, line)) {\n            std::cout << line << std::endl;\n        }\n        restored.close();\n        \n        // Убираем тестовые файлы\n        std::remove(\"restored_version.txt\");\n        std::remove(\"test_document.txt\");\n        fs::remove_all(\"./test_repo\");\n    }\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\n=== Демонстрация завершена ===\" << std::endl;\n    \n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <stack>\n\nclass MinStack {\n    std::stack<int> mainStack;\n    std::stack<int> minStack;\npublic:\n    void push(int x) {\n        mainStack.push(x);\n        if (minStack.empty() || x <= minStack.top()) {\n            minStack.push(x);\n        }\n    }\n    void pop() {\n        if (mainStack.empty()) return;\n        if (mainStack.top() == minStack.top()) {\n            minStack.pop();\n        }\n        mainStack.pop();\n    }\n    int top() {\n        return mainStack.top();\n    }\n    int getMin() {\n        return minStack.top();\n    }\n    bool empty() {\n        return mainStack.empty();\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    MinStack s;\n    s.push(3);\n    s.push(5);\n    std::cout << \"Минимальный: \" << s.getMin() << std::endl;\n    s.push(2);\n    s.push(1);\n    std::cout << \"Минимальный: \" << s.getMin() << std::endl;\n    s.pop();\n    std::cout << \"Минимальный после pop: \" << s.getMin() << std::endl;\n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <string>\n#include <unordered_map>\nusing namespace std;\n\nvoid countSubstringsOfLengthK(const string& str, int k) {\n    if(k <= 0 || k > str.length()) {\n        cout << \"Некорректная длина подстроки\" << endl;\n        return;\n    }\n    \n    unordered_map<string, int> substringCount;\n    \n    for(int i = 0; i <= str.length() - k; i++) {\n        string substring = str.substr(i, k);\n        substringCount[substring]++;\n    }\n    \n    cout << \"Подстроки длины \" << k << \" и их количество:\" << endl;\n    for(const auto& pair : substringCount) {\n        cout << pair.first << \": \" << pair.second << endl;\n    }\n}\n\nint main() {\n    string text = \"abababab\";\n    int k = 2;\n    \n    countSubstringsOfLengthK(text, k);\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <string>\nusing namespace std;\n\nbool isSubstring(const string& text, const string& pattern) {\n    if (pattern.empty()) return true;\n    if (text.length() < pattern.length()) return false;\n    for (size_t i = 0; i <= text.length() - pattern.length(); ++i) {\n        bool found = true;\n        for (size_t j = 0; j < pattern.length(); ++j) {\n            if (text[i + j] != pattern[j]) {\n                found = false;\n                break;\n            }\n        }\n        if (found) return true;\n    }\n    return false;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    string main = \"Hello, world!\";\n    string sub1 = \"world\";\n    string sub2 = \"planet\";\n    cout << sub1 << (isSubstring(main, sub1) ? \" является \" : \" не является \") << \"подстрокой\" << endl;\n    cout << sub2 << (isSubstring(main, sub2) ? \" является \" : \" не является \") << \"подстрокой\" << endl;\n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n\nint main() {\n    int num, minDigit = 9;\n    \n    std::cout << \"Введите число: \";\n    std::cin >> num;\n    \n    int temp = (num < 0) ? -num : num;\n    \n    if (temp == 0) minDigit = 0;\n    \n    while (temp != 0) {\n        int digit = temp % 10;\n        if (digit < minDigit) {\n            minDigit = digit;\n        }\n        temp /= 10;\n    }\n    \n    std::cout << \"Наименьшая цифра: \" << minDigit << std::endl;\n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <stdexcept>\n\nclass LibraryAPI { // Имитация библиотеки\npublic:\n    static bool initialized;\n    static void init() { \n        if (initialized) throw std::runtime_error(\"Already initialized\");\n        initialized = true; \n        std::cout << \"Library initialized\" << std::endl; \n    }\n    static void cleanup() { \n        if (initialized) {\n            initialized = false; \n            std::cout << \"Library cleaned up\" << std::endl; \n        }\n    }\n    static void doWork() {\n        if (!initialized) throw std::runtime_error(\"Library not initialized\");\n        std::cout << \"Library working\" << std::endl;\n    }\n};\nbool LibraryAPI::initialized = false;\n\nclass LibraryGuard {\npublic:\n    LibraryGuard() { LibraryAPI::init(); }\n    ~LibraryGuard() { LibraryAPI::cleanup(); }\n    LibraryGuard(const LibraryGuard&) = delete;\n    LibraryGuard& operator=(const LibraryGuard&) = delete;\n    void work() { LibraryAPI::doWork(); }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    try {\n        LibraryGuard lib;\n        lib.work();\n        lib.work();\n    } catch (const std::exception& e) {\n        std::cout << \"Error: \" << e.what() << std::endl;\n    }\n    std::cout << \"Library is now deinitialized\" << std::endl;\n    return 0;\n}

#include <sys/prctl.h>\n#include <unistd.h>\n#include <iostream>\n#include <cstring>\n#include <signal.h>\nusing namespace std;\n\nint main() {\n    char process_name[16];\n    strcpy(process_name, \"myprogram\");\n    if(prctl(PR_SET_NAME, process_name) == -1) {\n        perror(\"prctl PR_SET_NAME\");\n        return 1;\n    }\n    cout << \"Process name set to: \" << process_name << endl;\n    \n    char read_name[16];\n    if(prctl(PR_GET_NAME, read_name) == -1) {\n        perror(\"prctl PR_GET_NAME\");\n        return 1;\n    }\n    cout << \"Read process name: \" << read_name << endl;\n    \n    pid_t pid = fork();\n    if(pid == 0) {\n        prctl(PR_SET_PDEATHSIG, SIGKILL);\n        cout << \"Child will die when parent dies\" << endl;\n        sleep(5);\n    } else {\n        sleep(2);\n        cout << \"Parent exiting now\" << endl;\n    }\n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <climits>\n\nint main() {\n    const int V = 4;\n    int graph[V][V] = {{0, 4, 0, 0},\n                       {4, 0, 8, 0},\n                       {0, 8, 0, 7},\n                       {0, 0, 7, 0}};\n    \n    int dist[V];\n    bool visited[V];\n    \n    for (int i = 0; i < V; i++) {\n        dist[i] = INT_MAX;\n        visited[i] = false;\n    }\n    dist[0] = 0;\n    \n    for (int count = 0; count < V - 1; count++) {\n        int min = INT_MAX, u;\n        \n        for (int v = 0; v < V; v++) {\n            if (!visited[v] && dist[v] <= min) {\n                min = dist[v];\n                u = v;\n            }\n        }\n        \n        visited[u] = true;\n        \n        for (int v = 0; v < V; v++) {\n            if (!visited[v] && graph[u][v] && dist[u] != INT_MAX &&\n                dist[u] + graph[u][v] < dist[v]) {\n                dist[v] = dist[u] + graph[u][v];\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    std::cout << \"Кратчайшие расстояния от вершины 0:\" << std::endl;\n    for (int i = 0; i < V; i++) {\n        std::cout << \"До вершины \" << i << \": \" << dist[i] << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <string>\nusing namespace std;\n\nstring reverse_string_iterative(const string& str) {\n    string reversed = str;\n    int left = 0;\n    int right = reversed.length() - 1;\n    \n    while (left < right) {\n        swap(reversed[left], reversed[right]);\n        left++;\n        right--;\n    }\n    \n    return reversed;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    string str = \"hello\";\n    cout << \"Исходная строка: \" << str << endl;\n    string reversed = reverse_string_iterative(str);\n    cout << \"Реверс: \" << reversed << endl;\n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <string>\n#include <iomanip>\n\nint main() {\n    std::string clientType; // \"regular\", \"premium\", \"vip\"\n    double amount;\n    std::string currency; // \"RUB\", \"USD\", \"EUR\"\n    \n    std::cout << \"Введите тип клиента (regular/premium/vip): \";\n    std::cin >> clientType;\n    std::cout << \"Введите сумму операции: \";\n    std::cin >> amount;\n    std::cout << \"Введите валюту (RUB/USD/EUR): \";\n    std::cin >> currency;\n    \n    if (amount <= 0) {\n        std::cout << \"Сумма должна быть положительной!\" << std::endl;\n        return 1;\n    }\n    \n    double commissionRate = 0.0;\n    double fixedFee = 0.0;\n    \n    // Базовая комиссия в зависимости от типа клиента\n    if (clientType == \"regular\") {\n        commissionRate = 0.05; // 5%\n        fixedFee = 50.0;\n    } else if (clientType == \"premium\") {\n        commissionRate = 0.02; // 2%\n        fixedFee = 20.0;\n    } else if (clientType == \"vip\") {\n        commissionRate = 0.005; // 0.5%\n        fixedFee = 0.0;\n    } else {\n        std::cout << \"Неверный тип клиента!\" << std::endl;\n        return 1;\n    }\n    \n    // Дополнительные условия в зависимости от суммы\n    if (amount > 1000000) {\n        commissionRate *= 0.5; // Скидка 50% на комиссию для крупных сумм\n    } else if (amount < 1000) {\n        fixedFee += 10; // Дополнительный сбор для мелких сумм\n    }\n    \n    // Корректировка в зависимости от валюты\n    if (currency == \"USD\" || currency == \"EUR\") {\n        fixedFee *= 1.1; // На 10% выше для иностранных валют\n    } else if (currency != \"RUB\") {\n        std::cout << \"Валюта не поддерживается!\" << std::endl;\n        return 1;\n    }\n    \n    double commission = amount * commissionRate + fixedFee;\n    \n    // Ограничение максимальной комиссии\n    if (commission > amount * 0.1) {\n        commission = amount * 0.1;\n        std::cout << \"Внимание: комиссия ограничена 10% от суммы.\" << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    // Минимальная комиссия\n    if (commission < 10) {\n        commission = 10.0;\n    }\n    \n    double total = amount + commission;\n    \n    std::cout << std::fixed << std::setprecision(2);\n    std::cout << \"\\nРезультат расчета:\\n\";\n    std::cout << \"Сумма операции: \" << amount << \" \" << currency << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"Комиссия: \" << commission << \" \" << currency << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"Итого к оплате: \" << total << \" \" << currency << std::endl;\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\nusing namespace std;\n\nint main() {\n    int x = 10, y = 20;\n    \n    const int *ptr1 = &x;\n    cout << \"1. const int *ptr1 (указатель на константу):\" << endl;\n    cout << \"   *ptr1 = \" << *ptr1 << endl;\n    \n    ptr1 = &y;\n    cout << \"   После ptr1 = &y: *ptr1 = \" << *ptr1 << endl;\n    \n    int *const ptr2 = &x;\n    cout << \"\\n2. int *const ptr2 (константный указатель):\" << endl;\n    cout << \"   *ptr2 = \" << *ptr2 << endl;\n    \n    *ptr2 = 30;\n    cout << \"   После *ptr2 = 30: x = \" << x << endl;\n    \n    const int *const ptr3 = &x;\n    cout << \"\\n3. const int *const ptr3 (константный указатель на константу):\" << endl;\n    cout << \"   *ptr3 = \" << *ptr3 << endl;\n    cout << \"   Ни указатель, ни значение нельзя изменить через ptr3.\" << endl;\n    \n    x = 40;\n    cout << \"   После x = 40 (напрямую): x = \" << x << endl;\n    cout << \"   *ptr3 теперь = \" << *ptr3 << \" (отражает изменение x)\" << endl;\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <cmath>\nusing namespace std;\n\nint main() {\n    double x, y, r, x0 = 0, y0 = 0;\n    cout << \"Введите координаты точки и радиус: \";\n    cin >> x >> y >> r;\n    double dist = sqrt((x - x0) * (x - x0) + (y - y0) * (y - y0));\n    if (dist <= r) {\n        cout << \"Точка внутри круга\";\n    } else {\n        cout << \"Точка вне круга\";\n    }\n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n\ntemplate<typename T>\nclass Container {\n    T value;\npublic:\n    Container(T v) : value(v) {}\n    \n    template<typename U>\n    bool isEqual(const Container<U>& other) const {\n        return value == other.getValue();\n    }\n    \n    T getValue() const { return value; }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    Container<int> c1(42);\n    Container<double> c2(42.0);\n    Container<int> c3(100);\n    \n    std::cout << std::boolalpha;\n    std::cout << \"c1 == c2: \" << c1.isEqual(c2) << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"c1 == c3: \" << c1.isEqual(c3) << std::endl;\n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <cmath>\n\nunion Matrix2x2 {\n    struct {\n        double a11, a12;\n        double a21, a22;\n    } elements;\n    \n    struct {\n        double m[2][2];\n    } array;\n    \n    struct {\n        double trace;\n        double determinant;\n        double angle;\n        double scale;\n    } properties;\n    \n    Matrix2x2(double a = 1, double b = 0, double c = 0, double d = 1) {\n        elements.a11 = a;\n        elements.a12 = b;\n        elements.a21 = c;\n        elements.a22 = d;\n        update_properties();\n    }\n    \n    void update_properties() {\n        properties.trace = elements.a11 + elements.a22;\n        properties.determinant = elements.a11 * elements.a22 - elements.a12 * elements.a21;\n        \n        properties.scale = std::sqrt(elements.a11 * elements.a11 + elements.a21 * elements.a21);\n        properties.angle = std::atan2(elements.a21, elements.a11);\n    }\n    \n    void set_from_rotation(double angle) {\n        elements.a11 = std::cos(angle);\n        elements.a12 = -std::sin(angle);\n        elements.a21 = std::sin(angle);\n        elements.a22 = std::cos(angle);\n        update_properties();\n    }\n    \n    void set_from_scale(double sx, double sy) {\n        elements.a11 = sx;\n        elements.a12 = 0;\n        elements.a21 = 0;\n        elements.a22 = sy;\n        update_properties();\n    }\n    \n    Matrix2x2 multiply(const Matrix2x2& other) const {\n        Matrix2x2 result;\n        result.elements.a11 = elements.a11 * other.elements.a11 + elements.a12 * other.elements.a21;\n        result.elements.a12 = elements.a11 * other.elements.a12 + elements.a12 * other.elements.a22;\n        result.elements.a21 = elements.a21 * other.elements.a11 + elements.a22 * other.elements.a21;\n        result.elements.a22 = elements.a21 * other.elements.a12 + elements.a22 * other.elements.a22;\n        result.update_properties();\n        return result;\n    }\n    \n    void print(const char* name) const {\n        std::cout << name << \":\" << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"  Элементы: [[\" << elements.a11 << \", \" << elements.a12 << \"],\" << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"              [\" << elements.a21 << \", \" << elements.a22 << \"]]\" << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"  След: \" << properties.trace << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"  Определитель: \" << properties.determinant << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"  Масштаб: \" << properties.scale << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"  Угол: \" << properties.angle << \" радиан\" << std::endl;\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    Matrix2x2 A(1, 2, 3, 4);\n    Matrix2x2 B;\n    B.set_from_rotation(M_PI / 4);\n    Matrix2x2 C;\n #include <iostream>\n#include <string>\n#include <vector>\nusing namespace std;\n\nvector<int> computeLPS(const string& pattern) {\n    int m = pattern.length();\n    vector<int> lps(m, 0);\n    \n    int len = 0;\n    int i = 1;\n    \n    while(i < m) {\n        if(pattern[i] == pattern[len]) {\n            len++;\n            lps[i] = len;\n            i++;\n        } else {\n            if(len != 0) {\n                len = lps[len - 1];\n            } else {\n                lps[i] = 0;\n                i++;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    return lps;\n}\n\nvector<int> kmpSearch(const string& text, const string& pattern) {\n    vector<int> positions;\n    int n = text.length();\n    int m = pattern.length();\n    \n    if(m == 0) return positions;\n    \n    vector<int> lps = computeLPS(pattern);\n    \n    int i = 0; // индекс для текста\n    int j = 0; // индекс для паттерна\n    \n    while(i < n) {\n        if(pattern[j] == text[i]) {\n            i++;\n            j++;\n        }\n        \n        if(j == m) {\n            positions.push_back(i - j);\n            j = lps[j - 1];\n        } else if(i < n && pattern[j] != text[i]) {\n            if(j != 0) {\n                j = lps[j - 1];\n            } else {\n                i++;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    return positions;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    string text = \"ABABDABACDABABCABAB\";\n    string pattern = \"ABABCABAB\";\n    \n    vector<int> positions = kmpSearch(text, pattern);\n    \n    cout << \"KMP поиск: подстрока найдена на позициях: \";\n    for(int pos : positions) {\n        cout << pos << \" \";\n    }\n    cout << endl;\n    \n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <fstream>\n#include <string>\n#include <vector>\n#include <mutex>\n#include <thread>\n#include <chrono>\n#include <atomic>\n#include <queue>\n#include <condition_variable>\n#include <random>\n\nclass DistributedLogger {\nprivate:\n    struct LogEntry {\n        std::chrono::system_clock::time_point timestamp;\n        std::string source;\n        std::string message;\n        int severity;\n    };\n    \n    std::vector<std::string> logFiles;\n    std::queue<LogEntry> logQueue;\n    std::mutex mtx;\n    std::condition_variable cv;\n    std::atomic<bool> running{true};\n    std::thread loggerThread;\n    \n    std::string getCurrentTimestamp() {\n        auto now = std::chrono::system_clock::now();\n        std::time_t now_time = std::chrono::system_clock::to_time_t(now);\n        char buffer[80];\n        std::strftime(buffer, sizeof(buffer), \"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S\", std::localtime(&now_time));\n        return std::string(buffer);\n    }\n    \n    std::string severityToString(int severity) {\n        switch (severity) {\n            case 0: return \"INFO\";\n            case 1: return \"WARN\";\n            case 2: return \"ERROR\";\n            default: return \"UNKNOWN\";\n        }\n    }\n    \n    void loggerWorker() {\n        std::random_device rd;\n        std::mt19937 gen(rd());\n        \n        while (running || !logQueue.empty()) {\n            LogEntry entry;\n            {\n                std::unique_lock<std::mutex> lock(mtx);\n                cv.wait_for(lock, std::chrono::milliseconds(100), \n                           [this] { return !logQueue.empty() || !running; });\n                \n                if (!running && logQueue.empty()) {\n                    break;\n                }\n                \n                if (!logQueue.empty()) {\n                    entry = logQueue.front();\n                    logQueue.pop();\n                } else {\n                    continue;\n                }\n            }\n            \n            if (!logFiles.empty()) {\n                std::uniform_int_distribution<> dist(0, logFiles.size() - 1);\n                int fileIndex = dist(gen);\n                \n                std::ofstream file(logFiles[fileIndex], std::ios::app);\n                if (file.is_open()) {\n                    file << \"[\" << getCurrentTimestamp() << \"] \"\n                         << \"[\" << severityToString(entry.severity) << \"] \"\n                         << \"[\" << entry.source << \"] \"\n                         << entry.message << std::endl;\n                    file.close();\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \npublic:\n    DistributedLogger(const std::vector<std::string>& files) : logFiles(files) {\n        loggerThread = std::thread(&DistributedLogger::loggerWorker, this);\n    }\n    \n    ~DistributedLogger() {\n        running = false;\n        cv.notify_all();\n        if (loggerThread.joinable()) {\n            loggerThread.join();\n        }\n        \n        syncLogs();\n    }\n    \n    void log(const std::string& source, const std::string& message, int severity = 0) {\n        LogEntry entry{std::chrono::system_clock::now(), source, message, severity};\n        {\n            std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mtx);\n            logQueue.push(entry);\n        }\n        cv.notify_one();\n    }\n    \n    void syncLogs() {\n        std::ofstream masterLog(\"master.log\", std::ios::app);\n        if (!masterLog.is_open()) return;\n        \n        for (const auto& filename : logFiles) {\n            std::ifstream file(filename);\n            if (file.is_open()) {\n                std::string line;\n                while (std::getline(file, line)) {\n                    masterLog << \"[FROM \" << filename << \"] \" << line << std::endl;\n                }\n                file.close();\n            }\n        }\n        masterLog << \"\\n=== LOG SYNCHRONIZATION COMPLETE ===\\n\" << std::endl;\n        masterLog.close();\n        \n        std::cout << \"Логи синхронизированы в master.log\" << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    void showStats() {\n        std::cout << \"\\nСтатистика логов:\";\n        for (const auto& filename : logFiles) {\n            std::ifstream file(filename);\n            if (file.is_open()) {\n                file.seekg(0, std::ios::end);\n                std::streamsize size = file.tellg();\n                file.close();\n                std::cout << \"\\n  \" << filename << \": \" << size << \" байт\";\n            }\n        }\n        std::cout << std::endl;\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    std::vector<std::string> logFiles = {\"node1.log\", \"node2.log\", \"node3.log\"};\n    DistributedLogger logger(logFiles);\n    \n    std::vector<std::thread> workers;\n    for (int i = 0; i < 5; i++) {\n        workers.emplace_back([i, &logger]() {\n            for (int j = 0; j < 10; j++) {\n                logger.log(\"Worker\" + std::to_string(i), \n                          \"Сообщение \" + std::to_string(j) + \" от воркера \" + std::to_string(i),\n                          j % 3);\n                std::this_thread::sleep_for(std::chrono::milliseconds(rand() % 100));\n            }\n        });\n    }\n    \n    for (auto& worker : workers) {\n        worker.join();\n    }\n    \n    std::this_thread::sleep_for(std::chrono::seconds(1));\n    \n    logger.showStats();\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\nРаспределенный логгер завершил работу\" << std::endl;\n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <stdexcept>\nusing namespace std;\n\nclass LinkedList {\n    struct Node {\n        int data;\n        Node* next;\n        Node(int value) : data(value), next(nullptr) {}\n    };\n    \n    Node* head;\n    Node* tail;\n    size_t size;\n    \n    void copyList(const LinkedList& other) {\n        Node* current = other.head;\n        while(current) {\n            append(current->data);\n            current = current->next;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    void clearList() {\n        Node* current = head;\n        while(current) {\n            Node* next = current->next;\n            delete current;\n            current = next;\n        }\n        head = tail = nullptr;\n        size = 0;\n    }\n    \npublic:\n    LinkedList() : head(nullptr), tail(nullptr), size(0) {\n        cout << \"Пустой список создан\" << endl;\n    }\n    \n    LinkedList(const LinkedList& other) : head(nullptr), tail(nullptr), size(0) {\n        copyList(other);\n        cout << \"Список скопирован, размер: \" << size << endl;\n    }\n    \n    ~LinkedList() {\n        clearList();\n        cout << \"Список разрушен\" << endl;\n    }\n    \n    LinkedList& operator=(const LinkedList& other) {\n        if(this != &other) {\n            clearList();\n            copyList(other);\n        }\n        cout << \"Список присвоен\" << endl;\n        return *this;\n    }\n    \n    void append(int value) {\n        Node* newNode = new Node(value);\n        if(!head) {\n            head = tail = newNode;\n        } else {\n            tail->next = newNode;\n            tail = newNode;\n        }\n        size++;\n        cout << \"Добавлен элемент: \" << value << endl;\n    }\n    \n    void prepend(int value) {\n        Node* newNode = new Node(value);\n        if(!head) {\n            head = tail = newNode;\n        } else {\n            newNode->next = head;\n            head = newNode;\n        }\n        size++;\n        cout << \"Добавлен элемент в начало: \" << value << endl;\n    }\n    \n    void insert(int index, int value) {\n        if(index < 0 || index > size) {\n            throw out_of_range(\"Индекс вне диапазона\");\n        }\n        \n        if(index == 0) {\n            prepend(value);\n            return;\n        }\n        \n        if(index == size) {\n            append(value);\n            return;\n        }\n        \n        Node* newNode = new Node(value);\n        Node* current = head;\n        for(int i = 0; i < index - 1; i++) {\n            current = current->next;\n        }\n        newNode->next = current->next;\n        current->next = newNode;\n        size++;\n        cout << \"Вставлен элемент \" << value << \" на позицию \" << index << endl;\n    }\n    \n    void remove(int index) {\n        if(index < 0 || index >= size) {\n            throw out_of_range(\"Индекс вне диапазона\");\n        }\n        \n        Node* toDelete;\n        if(index == 0) {\n            toDelete = head;\n            head = head->next;\n            if(!head) tail = nullptr;\n        } else {\n            Node* current = head;\n            for(int i = 0; i < index - 1; i++) {\n                current = current->next;\n            }\n            toDelete = current->next;\n            current->next = toDelete->next;\n            if(toDelete == tail) {\n                tail = current;\n            }\n        }\n        \n        cout << \"Удален элемент: \" << toDelete->data << \" с позиции \" << index << endl;\n        delete toDelete;\n        size--;\n    }\n    \n    int get(int index) const {\n        if(index < 0 || index >= size) {\n            throw out_of_range(\"Индекс вне диапазона\");\n        }\n        \n        Node* current = head;\n        for(int i = 0; i < index; i++) {\n            current = current->next;\n        }\n        return current->data;\n    }\n    \n    void set(int index, int value) {\n        if(index < 0 || index >= size) {\n            throw out_of_range(\"Индекс вне диапазона\");\n        }\n        \n        Node* current = head;\n        for(int i = 0; i < index; i++) {\n            current = current->next;\n        }\n        current->data = value;\n        cout << \"Элемент на позиции \" << index << \" установлен в \" << value << endl;\n    }\n    \n    bool contains(int value) const {\n        Node* current = head;\n        while(current) {\n            if(current->data == value) return true;\n            current = current->next;\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n    \n    size_t getSize() const {\n        return size;\n    }\n    \n    bool isEmpty() const {\n        return size == 0;\n    }\n    \n    void reverse() {\n        if(!head || !head->next) return;\n        \n        Node* prev = nullptr;\n        Node* current = head;\n        Node* next = nullptr;\n        \n        tail = head;\n        while(current) {\n            next = current->next;\n            current->next = prev;\n            prev = current;\n            current = next;\n        }\n        head = prev;\n        cout << \"Список развернут\" << endl;\n    }\n    \n    void print() const {\n        cout << \"Список: \";\n        Node* current = head;\n        while(current) {\n            cout << current->data << \" \";\n            current = current->next;\n        }\n        cout << \"(размер: \" << size << \")\" << endl;\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    try {\n        LinkedList list;\n        list.append(10);\n        list.append(20);\n        list.append(30);\n        list.prepend(5);\n        \n        list.print();\n        \n        list.insert(2, 15);\n        list.print();\n        \n        cout << \"Элемент на позиции 2: \" << list.get(2) << endl;\n        \n        list.set(2, 25);\n        list.print();\n        \n        list.remove(1);\n        list.print();\n        \n        cout << \"Содержит 25? \" << (list.contains(25) ? \"Да\" : \"Нет\") << endl;\n        \n        list.reverse();\n        list.print();\n        \n        LinkedList list2 = list; // Конструктор копирования\n        list2.print();\n        \n        list2.append(100);\n        list = list2; // Оператор присваивания\n        list.print();\n        \n    } catch(const exception& e) {\n        cerr << \"Ошибка: \" << e.what() << endl;\n    }\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <queue>\nusing namespace std;\n\nclass BinaryTree {\n    struct TreeNode {\n        int data;\n        TreeNode* left;\n        TreeNode* right;\n        TreeNode(int val) : data(val), left(nullptr), right(nullptr) {}\n    };\n    \n    TreeNode* root;\n    \n    TreeNode* copyTree(TreeNode* node) {\n        if(!node) return nullptr;\n        TreeNode* newNode = new TreeNode(node->data);\n        newNode->left = copyTree(node->left);\n        newNode->right = copyTree(node->right);\n        return newNode;\n    }\n    \n    void deleteTree(TreeNode* node) {\n        if(node) {\n            deleteTree(node->left);\n            deleteTree(node->right);\n            delete node;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    void inorder(TreeNode* node) const {\n        if(node) {\n            inorder(node->left);\n            cout << node->data << \" \";\n            inorder(node->right);\n        }\n    }\n    \n    void preorder(TreeNode* node) const {\n        if(node) {\n            cout << node->data << \" \";\n            preorder(node->left);\n            preorder(node->right);\n        }\n    }\n    \n    void postorder(TreeNode* node) const {\n        if(node) {\n            postorder(node->left);\n            postorder(node->right);\n            cout << node->data << \" \";\n        }\n    }\n    \npublic:\n    BinaryTree() : root(nullptr) {\n        cout << \"Бинарное дерево создано\" << endl;\n    }\n    \n    BinaryTree(const BinaryTree& other) {\n        root = copyTree(other.root);\n        cout << \"Бинарное дерево скопировано\" << endl;\n    }\n    \n    ~BinaryTree() {\n        deleteTree(root);\n        cout << \"Бинарное дерево разрушено\" << endl;\n    }\n    \n    BinaryTree& operator=(const BinaryTree& other) {\n        if(this != &other) {\n            deleteTree(root);\n            root = copyTree(other.root);\n        }\n        cout << \"Бинарное дерево присвоено\" << endl;\n        return *this;\n    }\n    \n    void insert(int value) {\n        TreeNode* newNode = new TreeNode(value);\n        if(!root) {\n            root = newNode;\n            cout << \"Вставлен корень: \" << value << endl;\n            return;\n        }\n        \n        queue<TreeNode*> q;\n        q.push(root);\n        \n        while(!q.empty()) {\n            TreeNode* current = q.front();\n            q.pop();\n            \n            if(!current->left) {\n                current->left = newNode;\n                cout << \"Вставлен узел слева: \" << value << endl;\n                return;\n            } else {\n                q.push(current->left);\n            }\n            \n            if(!current->right) {\n                current->right = newNode;\n                cout << \"Вставлен узел справа: \" << value << endl;\n                return;\n            } else {\n                q.push(current->right);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    bool search(int value) const {\n        if(!root) return false;\n        \n        queue<TreeNode*> q;\n        q.push(root);\n        \n        while(!q.empty()) {\n            TreeNode* current = q.front();\n            q.pop();\n            \n            if(current->data == value) {\n                return true;\n            }\n            \n            if(current->left) q.push(current->left);\n            if(current->right) q.push(current->right);\n        }\n        \n        return false;\n    }\n    \n    void inorderTraversal() const {\n        cout << \"Inorder обход: \";\n        inorder(root);\n        cout << endl;\n    }\n    \n    void preorderTraversal() const {\n        cout << \"Preorder обход: \";\n        preorder(root);\n        cout << endl;\n    }\n    \n    void postorderTraversal() const {\n        cout << \"Postorder обход: \";\n        postorder(root);\n        cout << endl;\n    }\n    \n    void levelOrderTraversal() const {\n        if(!root) return;\n        \n        cout << \"Level-order обход: \";\n        queue<TreeNode*> q;\n        q.push(root);\n        \n        while(!q.empty()) {\n            TreeNode* current = q.front();\n            q.pop();\n            cout << current->data << \" \";\n            \n            if(current->left) q.push(current->left);\n            if(current->right) q.push(current->right);\n        }\n        cout << endl;\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    BinaryTree tree;\n #include <iostream>\n#include <vector>\n#include <algorithm>\n#include <climits>\n\nint findMaximumGap(std::vector<int>& nums) {\n    if (nums.size() < 2) return 0;\n    \n    int minVal = INT_MAX, maxVal = INT_MIN;\n    for (int num : nums) {\n        minVal = std::min(minVal, num);\n        maxVal = std::max(maxVal, num);\n    }\n    \n    int bucketSize = std::max(1, (maxVal - minVal) / ((int)nums.size() - 1));\n    int bucketCount = (maxVal - minVal) / bucketSize + 1;\n    \n    std::vector<std::pair<int, int>> buckets(bucketCount, {INT_MAX, INT_MIN});\n    \n    for (int num : nums) {\n        int bucketIndex = (num - minVal) / bucketSize;\n        buckets[bucketIndex].first = std::min(buckets[bucketIndex].first, num);\n        buckets[bucketIndex].second = std::max(buckets[bucketIndex].second, num);\n    }\n    \n    int maxGap = 0;\n    int prevMax = minVal;\n    \n    for (auto& bucket : buckets) {\n        if (bucket.first == INT_MAX) continue;\n        maxGap = std::max(maxGap, bucket.first - prevMax);\n        prevMax = bucket.second;\n    }\n    \n    return maxGap;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    std::vector<int> nums = {3,6,9,1};\n    std::cout << findMaximumGap(nums) << std::endl;\n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <thread>\n#include <atomic>\n#include <vector>\n#include <chrono>\n\nclass LockFreeStack {\nprivate:\n    struct Node {\n        int value;\n        Node* next;\n        Node(int val) : value(val), next(nullptr) {}\n    };\n    \n    std::atomic<Node*> head;\n    \npublic:\n    LockFreeStack() : head(nullptr) {}\n    \n    void push(int value) {\n        Node* new_node = new Node(value);\n        new_node->next = head.load();\n        \n        while (!head.compare_exchange_strong(new_node->next, new_node)) {\n            // Продолжаем попытки, пока не удастся обновить head\n        }\n        std::cout << \"Добавлен элемент: \" << value << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    bool pop(int& result) {\n        Node* old_head = head.load();\n        \n        while (old_head && \n               !head.compare_exchange_strong(old_head, old_head->next)) {\n            // Продолжаем попытки, пока не удастся обновить head\n        }\n        \n        if (old_head) {\n            result = old_head->value;\n            delete old_head;\n            std::cout << \"Извлечен элемент: \" << result << std::endl;\n            return true;\n        }\n        \n        return false;\n    }\n    \n    bool empty() const {\n        return head.load() == nullptr;\n    }\n};\n\nvoid pusher(LockFreeStack& stack, int id, int items) {\n    for (int i = 0; i < items; i++) {\n        int value = id * 100 + i;\n        stack.push(value);\n        std::this_thread::sleep_for(std::chrono::microseconds(10));\n    }\n}\n\nvoid popper(LockFreeStack& stack, int id, int items) {\n    for (int i = 0; i < items; i++) {\n        int value;\n        if (stack.pop(value)) {\n            // Успешно извлекли элемент\n        } else {\n            std::cout << \"Поток \" << id << \" не смог извлечь элемент\" << std::endl;\n        }\n        std::this_thread::sleep_for(std::chrono::microseconds(15));\n    }\n}\n\nvoid test_compare_exchange() {\n    std::atomic<int> counter(0);\n    std::vector<std::thread> threads;\n    \n    for (int i = 0; i < 5; i++) {\n        threads.emplace_back([&counter, i]() {\n            for (int j = 0; j < 100; j++) {\n                int expected = counter.load();\n                int desired = expected + 1;\n                \n                // compare_exchange_strong гарантирует успех или неудачу\n                while (!counter.compare_exchange_strong(expected, desired)) {\n                    desired = expected + 1;\n                }\n            }\n        });\n    }\n    \n    for (auto& t : threads) {\n        t.join();\n    }\n    \n    std::cout << \"Результат compare_exchange_strong: \" << counter << std::endl;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    std::cout << \"Тест Lock-Free Stack:\" << std::endl;\n    LockFreeStack stack;\n    \n    std::vector<std::thread> pushers;\n    std::vector<std::thread> poppers;\n    \n    for (int i = 0; i < 3; i++) {\n        pushers.emplace_back(pusher, std::ref(stack), i + 1, 5);\n    }\n    \n    std::this_thread::sleep_for(std::chrono::milliseconds(10));\n    \n    for (int i = 0; i < 2; i++) {\n        poppers.emplace_back(popper, std::ref(stack), i + 1, 7);\n    }\n    \n    for (auto& t : pushers) {\n        t.join();\n    }\n    \n    for (auto& t : poppers) {\n        t.join();\n    }\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\nТест compare_exchange_strong:\" << std::endl;\n    test_compare_exchange();\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <vector>\n#include <string>\n#include <unordered_set>\n#include <algorithm>\nusing namespace std;\n\nbool canForm(string& word, unordered_set<string>& dict) {\n    if (word.empty()) return false;\n    \n    vector<bool> dp(word.length() + 1, false);\n    dp[0] = true;\n    \n    for (int i = 1; i <= word.length(); i++) {\n        for (int j = 0; j < i; j++) {\n            if (dp[j] && dict.count(word.substr(j, i - j))) {\n                dp[i] = true;\n                break;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    return dp[word.length()];\n}\n\nvector<string> findConcatenatedWords(vector<string>& words) {\n    unordered_set<string> dict(words.begin(), words.end());\n    vector<string> result;\n    \n    for (string& word : words) {\n        dict.erase(word);\n        if (canForm(word, dict)) {\n            result.push_back(word);\n        }\n        dict.insert(word);\n    }\n    \n    return result;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    vector<string> words = {\"cat\",\"cats\",\"catsdogcats\",\"dog\",\"dogcatsdog\",\"hippopotamuses\",\"rat\",\"ratcatdogcat\"};\n    vector<string> concatenated = findConcatenatedWords(words);\n    for (string& word : concatenated) {\n        cout << word << \" \";\n    }\n    cout << endl;\n    return 0;\n}
#include <sys/socket.h>\n#include <netinet/in.h>\n#include <unistd.h>\n#include <iostream>\n#include <cstring>\n#include <sstream>\n#include <csignal>\n#include <ctime>\n\nvolatile sig_atomic_t keep_running = 1;\n\nvoid signal_handler(int sig) {\n    keep_running = 0;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    // Обработка сигналов для graceful shutdown\n    std::signal(SIGINT, signal_handler);\n    \n    int server_fd = socket(AF_INET, SOCK_STREAM, 0);\n    if(server_fd == -1) {\n        std::perror(\"socket\");\n        return 1;\n    }\n    \n    int opt = 1;\n    setsockopt(server_fd, SOL_SOCKET, SO_REUSEADDR, &opt, sizeof(opt));\n    \n    struct sockaddr_in address;\n    address.sin_family = AF_INET;\n    address.sin_addr.s_addr = INADDR_ANY;\n    address.sin_port = htons(8080);\n    \n    if(bind(server_fd, (struct sockaddr*)&address, sizeof(address)) < 0) {\n        std::perror(\"bind\");\n        close(server_fd);\n        return 1;\n    }\n    \n    if(listen(server_fd, 3) < 0) {\n        std::perror(\"listen\");\n        close(server_fd);\n        return 1;\n    }\n    \n    std::cout << \"Server listening on port 8080...\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"Press Ctrl+C to stop the server.\" << std::endl;\n    \n    int request_count = 0;\n    const int MAX_REQUESTS = 10; // Ограничение для тестирования\n    \n    while(keep_running && request_count < MAX_REQUESTS) {\n        struct sockaddr_in client_addr;\n        socklen_t client_len = sizeof(client_addr);\n        \n        int client_fd = accept(server_fd, (struct sockaddr*)&client_addr, &client_len);\n        if(client_fd < 0) {\n            std::perror(\"accept\");\n            continue;\n        }\n        \n        char buffer[1024] = {0};\n        ssize_t bytes_read = read(client_fd, buffer, sizeof(buffer) - 1);\n        \n        if(bytes_read > 0) {\n            buffer[bytes_read] = '\\0';\n            std::cout << \"\\n=== Received request (\" << ++request_count << \") ===\" << std::endl;\n            std::cout << buffer << std::endl;\n            \n            // Простой парсинг запроса\n            std::string request(buffer);\n            std::string response;\n            \n            if(request.find(\"GET /hello\") != std::string::npos) {\n                response = \"HTTP/1.1 200 OK\\r\\nContent-Type: text/html\\r\\n\\r\\n<h1>Hello World!</h1><p>Welcome to C++ HTTP Server</p>\";\n            }\n            else if(request.find(\"GET /time\") != std::string::npos) {\n                std::time_t now = std::time(nullptr);\n                std::string time_str = std::ctime(&now);\n                response = \"HTTP/1.1 200 OK\\r\\nContent-Type: text/html\\r\\n\\r\\n<h1>Current Time:</h1><p>\" + time_str + \"</p>\";\n            }\n            else if(request.find(\"GET /\") != std::string::npos) {\n                response = \"HTTP/1.1 200 OK\\r\\nContent-Type: text/html\\r\\n\\r\\n<h1>C++ HTTP Server</h1><p>Available endpoints:</p><ul><li><a href='/hello'>/hello</a></li><li><a href='/time'>/time</a></li></ul>\";\n            }\n            else {\n                response = \"HTTP/1.1 404 Not Found\\r\\nContent-Type: text/html\\r\\n\\r\\n<h1>404 Not Found</h1>\";\n            }\n            \n            write(client_fd, response.c_str(), response.length());\n            std::cout << \"Response sent.\" << std::endl;\n        }\n        \n        close(client_fd);\n    }\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\nServer shutting down...\" << std::endl;\n    close(server_fd);\n    \n    if(request_count >= MAX_REQUESTS) {\n        std::cout << \"Maximum request limit (\" << MAX_REQUESTS << \") reached.\" << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <vector>\n#include <algorithm>\nusing namespace std;\n\nclass Set {\n    vector<int> elements;\n    void sortUnique() {\n        sort(elements.begin(), elements.end());\n        elements.erase(unique(elements.begin(), elements.end()), elements.end());\n    }\npublic:\n    Set() = default; // конструктор по умолчанию\n    Set(initializer_list<int> il) : elements(il) { sortUnique(); }\n    \n    void add(int x) {\n        if (find(elements.begin(), elements.end(), x) == elements.end()) {\n            elements.push_back(x);\n            sortUnique();\n        }\n    }\n    \n    void remove(int x) {\n        auto it = find(elements.begin(), elements.end(), x);\n        if (it != elements.end()) {\n            elements.erase(it);\n        }\n    }\n    \n    bool contains(int x) const {\n        return find(elements.begin(), elements.end(), x) != elements.end();\n    }\n    \n    size_t size() const { return elements.size(); }\n    bool empty() const { return elements.empty(); }\n    \n    Set operator+(const Set& other) const { // объединение\n        Set result = *this;\n        for (int x : other.elements) {\n            result.add(x);\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n    \n    Set operator-(const Set& other) const { // разность\n        Set result;\n        for (int x : elements) {\n            if (!other.contains(x)) {\n                result.add(x);\n            }\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n    \n    Set operator*(const Set& other) const { // пересечение\n        Set result;\n        for (int x : elements) {\n            if (other.contains(x)) {\n                result.add(x);\n            }\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n    \n    bool operator==(const Set& other) const {\n        if (elements.size() != other.elements.size()) return false;\n        for (size_t i = 0; i < elements.size(); i++) {\n            if (elements[i] != other.elements[i]) return false;\n        }\n        return true;\n    }\n    \n    bool operator!=(const Set& other) const {\n        return !(*this == other);\n    }\n    \n    friend ostream& operator<<(ostream& os, const Set& s) {\n        os << \"{\";\n        for (size_t i = 0; i < s.elements.size(); i++) {\n            os << s.elements[i];\n            if (i < s.elements.size() - 1) os << \", \";\n        }\n        return os << \"}\";\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    Set A = {1, 2, 3, 4, 4, 2}; // дубликаты будут удалены\n    Set B = {3, 4, 5, 6, 6};\n    \n    cout << \"A: \" << A << endl;\n    cout << \"B: \" << B << endl;\n    cout << \"Size of A: \" << A.size() << endl;\n    cout << \"Size of B: \" << B.size() << endl;\n    \n    cout << \"\\nSet Operations:\" << endl;\n    cout << \"A + B (union): \" << (A + B) << endl;\n    cout << \"A - B (difference): \" << (A - B) << endl;\n    cout << \"B - A (difference): \" << (B - A) << endl;\n    cout << \"A * B (intersection): \" << (A * B) << endl;\n    \n    cout << \"\\nEquality Tests:\" << endl;\n    cout << \"A == B: \" << (A == B ? \"true\" : \"false\") << endl;\n    cout << \"A != B: \" << (A != B ? \"true\" : \"false\") << endl;\n    \n    Set C = {1, 2, 3, 4};\n    cout << \"\\nC = \" << C << endl;\n    cout << \"A == C: \" << (A == C ? \"true\" : \"false\") << endl;\n    \n    // Дополнительные операции\n    cout << \"\\nAdditional operations:\" << endl;\n    A.add(7);\n    cout << \"After A.add(7): \" << A << endl;\n    \n    B.remove(4);\n    cout << \"After B.remove(4): \" << B << endl;\n    \n    cout << \"\\nMembership tests:\" << endl;\n    cout << \"A.contains(3): \" << (A.contains(3) ? \"true\" : \"false\") << endl;\n    cout << \"A.contains(10): \" << (A.contains(10) ? \"true\" : \"false\") << endl;\n    \n    // Работа с пустым множеством\n    Set emptySet;\n    cout << \"\\nEmpty set: \" << emptySet << endl;\n    cout << \"Is empty? \" << (emptySet.empty() ? \"true\" : \"false\") << endl;\n    cout << \"Size: \" << emptySet.size() << endl;\n    \n    // Комбинированные операции\n    Set D = {2, 4, 6, 8};\n    Set E = {1, 3, 5, 7};\n    Set F = (A + D) * E;\n    cout << \"\\nCombined operation (A + D) * E:\" << endl;\n    cout << \"A: \" << A << endl;\n    cout << \"D: \" << D << endl;\n    cout << \"E: \" << E << endl;\n    cout << \"Result: \" << F << endl;\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <cstdlib>\nusing namespace std;\n\nclass PoolAllocator {\n    static const size_t POOL_SIZE = 1000;\n    static char memoryPool[POOL_SIZE];\n    static bool initialized;\n    static size_t nextFree;\n    int data;\npublic:\n    PoolAllocator(int val) : data(val) {\n        cout << \"Constructed PoolAllocator with data: \" << data << endl;\n    }\n    ~PoolAllocator() {\n        cout << \"Destructor called for data: \" << data << endl;\n    }\n    static void initializePool() {\n        if(!initialized) {\n            nextFree = 0;\n            initialized = true;\n            cout << \"Memory pool initialized (\" << POOL_SIZE << \" bytes)\" << endl;\n        }\n    }\n    static void cleanupPool() {\n        cout << \"Pool cleanup called (simple example).\" << endl;\n        initialized = false;\n        nextFree = 0;\n    }\n    void* operator new(size_t size) {\n        if(!initialized) initializePool();\n        if(nextFree + size <= POOL_SIZE) {\n            void* ptr = &memoryPool[nextFree];\n            nextFree += size;\n            cout << \"Allocated \" << size << \" bytes from pool. Next free at: \" << nextFree << endl;\n            return ptr;\n        }\n        throw bad_alloc();\n    }\n    void operator delete(void* ptr) noexcept {\n        cout << \"Custom delete - memory block returned to pool (logically).\" << endl;\n    }\n    void display() const { cout << \"PoolAllocator data: \" << data << endl; }\n};\n\nchar PoolAllocator::memoryPool[POOL_SIZE];\nbool PoolAllocator::initialized = false;\nsize_t PoolAllocator::nextFree = 0;\n\nint main() {\n    PoolAllocator* obj1 = new PoolAllocator(10);\n    PoolAllocator* obj2 = new PoolAllocator(20);\n    obj1->display();\n    obj2->display();\n    delete obj1;\n    delete obj2;\n    PoolAllocator::cleanupPool();\n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <string>\n#include <unordered_set>\n#include <vector>\n#include <algorithm>\n#include <chrono>\nusing namespace std;\n\nvector<string> getAllUniqueSubstrings(const string& str) {\n    unordered_set<string> unique_substrings;\n    int n = str.length();\n    \n    // Генерируем все подстроки\n    for(int i = 0; i < n; i++) {\n        for(int length = 1; length <= n - i; length++) {\n            string substring = str.substr(i, length);\n            unique_substrings.insert(substring);\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // Конвертируем в вектор и сортируем\n    vector<string> result(unique_substrings.begin(), unique_substrings.end());\n    sort(result.begin(), result.end());\n    \n    return result;\n}\n\n// Более эффективная версия с использованием хеширования\nvector<string> getUniqueSubstringsEfficient(const string& str) {\n    unordered_set<string> unique_substrings;\n    int n = str.length();\n    \n    // Используем скользящее хеширование для эффективности\n    for(int length = 1; length <= n; length++) {\n        unordered_set<string> current_length_substrings;\n        \n        for(int i = 0; i <= n - length; i++) {\n            string substring = str.substr(i, length);\n            current_length_substrings.insert(substring);\n        }\n        \n        // Добавляем в общий набор\n        unique_substrings.insert(current_length_substrings.begin(), \n                                current_length_substrings.end());\n    }\n    \n    vector<string> result(unique_substrings.begin(), unique_substrings.end());\n    sort(result.begin(), result.end());\n    \n    return result;\n}\n\n// Версия с использованием суффиксного массива (оптимизированная)\nvector<string> getUniqueSubstringsOptimized(const string& str) {\n    unordered_set<string> unique_substrings;\n    int n = str.length();\n    \n    // Строим все суффиксы\n    vector<string> suffixes;\n    for(int i = 0; i < n; i++) {\n        suffixes.push_back(str.substr(i));\n    }\n    \n    // Сортируем суффиксы\n    sort(suffixes.begin(), suffixes.end());\n    \n    // Извлекаем уникальные подстроки из суффиксов\n    for(const string& suffix : suffixes) {\n        int len = suffix.length();\n        for(int length = 1; length <= len; length++) {\n            string substring = suffix.substr(0, length);\n            unique_substrings.insert(substring);\n        }\n    }\n    \n    vector<string> result(unique_substrings.begin(), unique_substrings.end());\n    sort(result.begin(), result.end());\n    \n    return result;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    vector<string> test_cases = {\n        \"abc\",\n        \"aaaa\",\n        \"ababa\",\n        \"\",\n        \"abcd\",\n        \"test\",\n        \"banana\"\n    };\n    \n    cout << \"Unique Substrings Finder:\\n\";\n    cout << \"==========================\\n\";\n    \n    for(const string& test : test_cases) {\n        cout << \"\\nString: \\\"\" << test << \"\\\"\" << endl;\n        cout << \"Length: \" << test.length() << endl;\n        \n        // Тестируем разные методы\n        auto start1 = chrono::high_resolution_clock::now();\n        vector<string> result1 = getAllUniqueSubstrings(test);\n        auto end1 = chrono::high_resolution_clock::now();\n        auto duration1 = chrono::duration_cast<chrono::microseconds>(end1 - start1);\n        \n        auto start2 = chrono::high_resolution_clock::now();\n        vector<string> result2 = getUniqueSubstringsOptimized(test);\n        auto end2 = chrono::high_resolution_clock::now();\n        auto duration2 = chrono::duration_cast<chrono::microseconds>(end2 - start2);\n        \n        cout << \"Total unique substrings: \" << result1.size() << endl;\n        cout << \"Naive method time: \" << duration1.count() << \" µs\" << endl;\n        cout << \"Optimized method time: \" << duration2.count() << \" µs\" << endl;\n        \n        // Проверяем совпадение результатов\n        bool results_match = (result1.size() == result2.size());\n        if(results_match) {\n            sort(result1.begin(), result1.end());\n            sort(result2.begin(), result2.end());\n            results_match = (result1 == result2);\n        }\n        \n        cout << \"Results match: \" << (results_match ? \"YES\" : \"NO\") << endl;\n        \n        // Показываем несколько подстрок (если не слишком много)\n        if(result1.size() <= 20 && !result1.empty()) {\n            cout << \"Substrings: \";\n            for(const string& s : result1) {\n                cout << s << \" \";\n            }\n            cout << endl;\n        } else if(!result1.empty()) {\n            cout << \"First 10 substrings: \";\n            for(int i = 0; i < min(10, (int)result1.size()); i++) {\n                cout << result1[i] << \" \";\n            }\n            cout << \"...\" << endl;\n        }\n        \n        // Вычисляем теоретическое максимальное количество подстрок\n        long long max_possible = (test.length() * (test.length() + 1)) / 2;\n        cout << \"Maximum possible substrings: \" << max_possible << endl;\n        cout << \"Uniqueness ratio: \" << (test.empty() ? 0.0 : result1.size() * 100.0 / max_possible) << \"%\" << endl;\n    }\n    \n    // Тест производительности для длинной строки\n    cout << \"\\n\\nPerformance test for longer string:\\n\";\n    string long_str = \"abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz\";\n    cout << \"String length: \" << long_str.length() << endl;\n    \n    auto start = chrono::high_resolution_clock::now();\n    auto result = getUniqueSubstringsOptimized(long_str);\n    auto end = chrono::high_resolution_clock::now();\n    auto duration = chrono::duration_cast<chrono::milliseconds>(end - start);\n    \n    cout << \"Time: \" << duration.count() << \" ms\" << endl;\n    cout << \"Unique substrings: \" << result.size() << endl;\n    \n    // Теоретический максимум\n    long long n = long_str.length();\n    long long max_possible = (n * (n + 1)) / 2;\n    cout << \"Theoretical maximum: \" << max_possible << endl;\n    cout << \"All substrings are unique: \" << (result.size() == max_possible ? \"YES\" : \"NO\") << endl;\n    \n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <vector>\n#include <algorithm>\n\nvoid findBridgesUtil(int u, const std::vector<std::vector<int>>& graph, std::vector<bool>& visited, \n                    std::vector<int>& disc, std::vector<int>& low, int parent, \n                    std::vector<std::pair<int, int>>& bridges, int& time) {\n    visited[u] = true;\n    disc[u] = low[u] = ++time;\n    \n    for (int v : graph[u]) {\n        if (!visited[v]) {\n            findBridgesUtil(v, graph, visited, disc, low, u, bridges, time);\n            \n            low[u] = std::min(low[u], low[v]);\n            \n            if (low[v] > disc[u]) {\n                bridges.push_back({u, v});\n            }\n        } else if (v != parent) {\n            low[u] = std::min(low[u], disc[v]);\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nstd::vector<std::pair<int, int>> findBridges(const std::vector<std::vector<int>>& graph) {\n    int n = graph.size();\n    std::vector<bool> visited(n, false);\n    std::vector<int> disc(n, -1);\n    std::vector<int> low(n, -1);\n    std::vector<std::pair<int, int>> bridges;\n    int time = 0;\n    \n    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {\n        if (!visited[i]) {\n            findBridgesUtil(i, graph, visited, disc, low, -1, bridges, time);\n        }\n    }\n    \n    return bridges;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    int n = 5;\n    std::vector<std::vector<int>> graph(n);\n    \n    graph[0] = {1, 2};\n    graph[1] = {0, 2};\n    graph[2] = {0, 1, 3, 4};\n    graph[3] = {2, 4};\n    graph[4] = {2, 3};\n    \n    std::vector<std::pair<int, int>> bridges = findBridges(graph);\n    \n    std::cout << \"Мосты в графе:\" << std::endl;\n    for (auto& bridge : bridges) {\n        std::cout << bridge.first << \" - \" << bridge.second << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    return 0;\n}

Финальный баланс: \" << balance << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    void deposit(double amount) {\n        if(amount <= 0) {\n            std::cout << \"Ошибка: сумма депозита должна быть положительной\" << std::endl;\n            return;\n        }\n        balance += amount;\n        std::cout << \"Внесено \" << amount << \". Новый баланс: \" << balance << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    bool withdraw(double amount) {\n        if(amount <= 0) {\n            std::cout << \"Ошибка: сумма снятия должна быть положительной\" << std::endl;\n            return false;\n        }\n        if(amount > balance) {\n            std::cout << \"Ошибка: недостаточно средств. Баланс: \" << balance << std::endl;\n            return false;\n        }\n        balance -= amount;\n        std::cout << \"Снято \" << amount << \". Новый баланс: \" << balance << std::endl;\n        return true;\n    }\n    \n    double getBalance() const {\n        return balance;\n    }\n    \n    void displayInfo() const {\n        std::cout << \"Номер счета: \" << accountNumber << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"Владелец: \" << ownerName << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"Баланс: \" << balance << std::endl;\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    BankAccount acc1;\n    BankAccount acc2(\"123456\", \"Иван Иванов\", 1000.0);\n    \n    acc1.displayInfo();\n    std::cout << std::endl;\n    acc2.displayInfo();\n    \n    acc2.deposit(500.0);\n    acc2.withdraw(200.0);\n    acc2.withdraw(2000.0); // Недостаточно средств\n    \n    std::cout << \"Финальный баланс acc2: \" << acc2.getBalance() << std::endl;\n    \n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <algorithm>\nusing namespace std;\n\nstruct Node {\n    int data;\n    Node* left;\n    Node* right;\n    Node(int val) : data(val), left(nullptr), right(nullptr) {}\n};\n\nint height(Node* root, int& diameter) {\n    if (root == nullptr) return 0;\n    int leftHeight = height(root->left, diameter);\n    int rightHeight = height(root->right, diameter);\n    diameter = max(diameter, leftHeight + rightHeight);\n    return 1 + max(leftHeight, rightHeight);\n}\n\nint diameterOfTree(Node* root) {\n    int diameter = 0;\n    height(root, diameter);\n    return diameter;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    Node* root = new Node(1);\n    root->left = new Node(2);\n    root->right = new Node(3);\n    root->left->left = new Node(4);\n    root->left->right = new Node(5);\n    root->left->right->right = new Node(6);\n    cout << \"Диаметр дерева: \" << diameterOfTree(root) << endl;\n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <string>\n#include <cctype>\nusing namespace std;\n\nenum class DataType { INTEGER, FLOAT, STRING, BOOLEAN };\n\nbool validateData(const string& input, DataType expectedType) {\n switch(expectedType) {\n case DataType::INTEGER: {\n if (input.empty()) return false;\n for (size_t i = 0; i < input.length(); i++) {\n if (!isdigit(input[i])) {\n if (i == 0 && input[i] == '-') continue;\n return false;\n }\n }\n return true;\n }\n \n case DataType::FLOAT: {\n if (input.empty()) return false;\n bool hasDot = false;\n for (size_t i = 0; i < input.length(); i++) {\n if (!isdigit(input[i])) {\n if (i == 0 && input[i] == '-') continue;\n if (input[i] == '.' && !hasDot) {\n hasDot = true;\n continue;\n }\n return false;\n }\n }\n return hasDot;\n }\n \n case DataType::BOOLEAN: {\n return (input == "true" || input == "false" || \n input == "1" || input == "0");\n }\n \n case DataType::STRING: {\n return true;\n }\n }\n return false;\n}\n\nint main() {\n cout << boolalpha;\n cout << "Валидация '123' как INTEGER: " << validateData("123", DataType::INTEGER) << endl;\n cout << "Валидация '-456' как INTEGER: " << validateData("-456", DataType::INTEGER) << endl;\n cout << "Валидация '12.3' как FLOAT: " << validateData("12.3", DataType::FLOAT) << endl;\n cout << "Валидация '-45.67' как FLOAT: " << validateData("-45.67", DataType::FLOAT) << endl;\n cout << "Валидация 'abc' как STRING: " << validateData("abc", DataType::STRING) << endl;\n cout << "Валидация 'true' как BOOLEAN: " << validateData("true", DataType::BOOLEAN) << endl;\n cout << "Валидация '12a' как INTEGER: " << validateData("12a", DataType::INTEGER) << endl;\n cout << "Валидация '12.3.4' как FLOAT: " << validateData("12.3.4", DataType::FLOAT) << endl;\n \n return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <vector>\n#include <queue>\n\nint findKthLargest(std::vector<int>& nums, int k) {\n    std::priority_queue<int, std::vector<int>, std::greater<int>> min_heap;\n    for (int num : nums) {\n        min_heap.push(num);\n        if (min_heap.size() > k) {\n            min_heap.pop();\n        }\n    }\n    return min_heap.top();\n}\n\nint main() {\n    std::vector<int> nums = {3,2,1,5,6,4};\n    int k = 2;\n    std::cout << \"K-th largest: \" << findKthLargest(nums, k) << std::endl;\n    return 0;\n}
