#include <iostream>\n#include <type_traits>\nusing namespace std;\n\n#define SELECT_IMPLEMENTATION(T) \\\n    template<typename U = T> \\\n    typename enable_if<sizeof(U) <= 4>::type \\\n    processImplementation(U value) { \\\n        cout << \"Small type processing: \" << value << endl; \\\n    } \\\n    template<typename U = T> \\\n    typename enable_if<(sizeof(U) > 4)>::type \\\n    processImplementation(U value) { \\\n        cout << \"Large type processing: \" << value << endl; \\\n    }\n\ntemplate<typename T>\nstruct Processor {\n    SELECT_IMPLEMENTATION(T)\n    \n    void process(T value) {\n        processImplementation(value);\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    Processor<int> p1;\n    Processor<double> p2;\n    Processor<long long> p3;\n    \n    p1.process(42);          // Маленький тип\n    p2.process(3.14159);     // Маленький тип\n    p3.process(123456789012345LL); // Большой тип\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n\nclass PrimeChecker {\npublic:\n    bool isPrime(int number) {\n        if(number <= 1) return false;\n        for(int i = 2; i * i <= number; i++) {\n            if(number % i == 0) return false;\n        }\n        return true;\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    PrimeChecker checker;\n    std::cout << \"7 is prime: \" << (checker.isPrime(7) ? \"Yes\" : \"No\") << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"8 is prime: \" << (checker.isPrime(8) ? \"Yes\" : \"No\") << std::endl;\n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <stdexcept>\n#include <utility>\nusing namespace std;\n\ntemplate<typename T>\nclass SmartPointer {\n    T* ptr;\n    int* refCount;\n    \n    void release() {\n        if(refCount) {\n            (*refCount)--;\n            if(*refCount == 0) {\n                delete ptr;\n                delete refCount;\n                cout << \"Memory freed\" << endl;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \npublic:\n    SmartPointer() : ptr(nullptr), refCount(nullptr) {\n        cout << \"Empty SmartPointer created\" << endl;\n    }\n    \n    explicit SmartPointer(T* p) : ptr(p) {\n        if(p) {\n            refCount = new int(1);\n            cout << \"SmartPointer created, reference count: 1\" << endl;\n        } else {\n            refCount = nullptr;\n            cout << \"SmartPointer created with null pointer\" << endl;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    SmartPointer(const SmartPointer& other) : ptr(other.ptr), refCount(other.refCount) {\n        if(refCount) {\n            (*refCount)++;\n            cout << \"SmartPointer copied, reference count: \" << *refCount << endl;\n        } else {\n            cout << \"SmartPointer copied (null pointer)\" << endl;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    ~SmartPointer() {\n        release();\n        cout << \"SmartPointer destroyed\" << endl;\n    }\n    \n    SmartPointer& operator=(const SmartPointer& other) {\n        if(this != &other) {\n            release();\n            \n            ptr = other.ptr;\n            refCount = other.refCount;\n            \n            if(refCount) {\n                (*refCount)++;\n                cout << \"SmartPointer assigned, reference count: \" << *refCount << endl;\n            }\n        }\n        return *this;\n    }\n    \n    T& operator*() const {\n        if(!ptr) {\n            throw runtime_error(\"Attempt to dereference null pointer\");\n        }\n        return *ptr;\n    }\n    \n    T* operator->() const {\n        if(!ptr) {\n            throw runtime_error(\"Attempt to access through null pointer\");\n        }\n        return ptr;\n    }\n    \n    T* get() const {\n        return ptr;\n    }\n    \n    int use_count() const {\n        return refCount ? *refCount : 0;\n    }\n    \n    explicit operator bool() const {\n        return ptr != nullptr;\n    }\n    \n    void reset(T* p = nullptr) {\n        release();\n        ptr = p;\n        if(p) {\n            refCount = new int(1);\n            cout << \"SmartPointer reset, reference count: 1\" << endl;\n        } else {\n            refCount = nullptr;\n            cout << \"SmartPointer reset to nullptr\" << endl;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    void swap(SmartPointer& other) {\n        swap(ptr, other.ptr);\n        swap(refCount, other.refCount);\n        cout << \"SmartPointer swapped\" << endl;\n    }\n};\n\nclass TestClass {\n    int value;\npublic:\n    TestClass(int v) : value(v) {\n        cout << \"TestClass created with value \" << value << endl;\n    }\n    \n    ~TestClass() {\n        cout << \"TestClass destroyed, value was \" << value << endl;\n    }\n    \n    void print() const {\n        cout << \"Value: \" << value << endl;\n    }\n    \n    void setValue(int v) {\n        value = v;\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    try {\n        SmartPointer<TestClass> sp1(new TestClass(10));\n        sp1->print();\n        \n        SmartPointer<TestClass> sp2 = sp1; // Copy constructor\n        cout << \"Reference count sp1: \" << sp1.use_count() << endl;\n        \n        {\n            SmartPointer<TestClass> sp3;\n            sp3 = sp2; // Assignment operator\n            cout << \"Reference count after assignment: \" << sp1.use_count() << endl;\n            \n            (*sp3).setValue(20);\n            sp1->print();\n        } // sp3 goes out of scope\n        \n        cout << \"Reference count after sp3 destruction: \" << sp1.use_count() << endl;\n        \n        SmartPointer<TestClass> sp4(new TestClass(30));\n        sp1.swap(sp4);\n        \n        sp1->print();\n        sp4->print();\n        \n        sp4.reset();\n        cout << \"Is sp4 empty? \" << (sp4 ? \"No\" : \"Yes\") << endl;\n        \n    } catch(const exception& e) {\n        cerr << \"Error: \" << e.what() << endl;\n    }\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <vector>\n#include <map>\n#include <algorithm>\nusing namespace std;\n\nint main() {\n    vector<int> vec = {1, 3, 2, 3, 4, 3, 2, 2, 2};\n    \n    map<int, int> freq;\n    for (int x : vec) {\n        freq[x]++;\n    }\n    \n    auto mostFrequent = max_element(freq.begin(), freq.end(),\n                                   [](const pair<int, int>& a, const pair<int, int>& b) {\n                                       return a.second < b.second;\n                                   });\n    \n    cout << \"Наиболее частый элемент: \" << mostFrequent->first << endl;\n    cout << \"Количество повторений: \" << mostFrequent->second << endl;\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\nusing namespace std;\n\nint binarySearch(int* arr, int size, int target) {\n    int left = 0, right = size - 1;\n    while(left <= right) {\n        int mid = left + (right - left) / 2;\n        if(arr[mid] == target) return mid;\n        else if(arr[mid] < target) left = mid + 1;\n        else right = mid - 1;\n    }\n    return -1;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    int size = 9;\n    int* arr = new int[size] {2, 5, 8, 12, 16, 23, 38, 45, 56};\n    int target = 23;\n    int index = binarySearch(arr, size, target);\n    if(index != -1) {\n        cout << \"Элемент \" << target << \" найден на позиции \" << index << endl;\n    } else {\n        cout << \"Элемент \" << target << \" не найден\" << endl;\n    }\n    delete[] arr;\n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <string>\nusing namespace std;\n\nclass NetworkProtocol {\nprotected:\n    string name;\n    int defaultPort;\npublic:\n    NetworkProtocol(string protoName, int port) \n        : name(protoName), defaultPort(port) {}\n    virtual string sendRequest(string request) const {\n        cout << \"Sending request via \" << name \n             << \" on port \" << defaultPort << \": \" << request << endl;\n        return \"Generic response\";\n    }\n    virtual void showInfo() const {\n        cout << \"Protocol: \" << name << \" (port \" << defaultPort << \")\" << endl;\n    }\n    virtual ~NetworkProtocol() = default;\n};\n\nclass HTTP : public NetworkProtocol {\n    string version;\npublic:\n    HTTP(string protoName, int port, string ver = \"1.1\") \n        : NetworkProtocol(protoName, port), version(ver) {}\n    string sendRequest(string request) const override {\n        cout << \"HTTP/\" << version << \" request to port \" << defaultPort \n             << \": \" << request << endl;\n        return \"HTTP/\" + version + \" 200 OK\";\n    }\n    void showInfo() const override {\n        cout << \"HTTP Protocol: \" << name \n             << \" (port \" << defaultPort << \", version \" << version << \")\" << endl;\n    }\n};\n\nclass FTP : public NetworkProtocol {\n    bool passiveMode;\npublic:\n    FTP(string protoName, int port, bool passive = true) \n        : NetworkProtocol(protoName, port), passiveMode(passive) {}\n    string sendRequest(string request) const override {\n        cout << \"FTP \" << (passiveMode ? \"passive\" : \"active\") \n             << \" mode request on port \" << defaultPort \n             << \": \" << request << endl;\n        return \"FTP 226 Transfer complete\";\n    }\n    void showInfo() const override {\n        cout << \"FTP Protocol: \" << name \n             << \" (port \" << defaultPort \n             << \", mode \" << (passiveMode ? \"passive\" : \"active\") << \")\" << endl;\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    NetworkProtocol* protocols[3];\n    protocols[0] = new NetworkProtocol(\"Generic\", 0);\n    protocols[1] = new HTTP(\"HTTP\", 80, \"2.0\");\n    protocols[2] = new FTP(\"FTP\", 21, true);\n    \n    for (int i = 0; i < 3; i++) {\n        protocols[i]->showInfo();\n        string response = protocols[i]->sendRequest(\"GET /index.html\");\n        cout << \"Response: \" << response << endl;\n        delete protocols[i];\n        cout << endl;\n    }\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <string>\n#include <memory>\nusing namespace std;\n\n// Макросы для Builder pattern\n#define DECLARE_BUILDER(classname) \\\n    class classname; \\\n    class classname##Builder\n\n#define BEGIN_CLASS(classname) \\\n    class classname { \\\n        friend class classname##Builder; \\\n    private: \\\n        classname() = default;\n\n#define CLASS_FIELD(type, name) \\\n        type name##_;\n\n#define END_CLASS(classname) \\\n    public: \\\n        void print() const; \\\n    };\n\n#define BEGIN_BUILDER(classname) \\\n    class classname##Builder { \\\n        classname object; \\\n    public: \\\n        classname##Builder() = default; \\\n        classname##Builder& operator=(const classname##Builder&) = delete;\n\n#define BUILDER_FIELD(classname, type, name) \\\n        classname##Builder& name(type value) { \\\n            object.name##_ = value; \\\n            return *this; \\\n        }\n\n#define END_BUILDER(classname) \\\n        classname build() { \\\n            return move(object); \\\n        } \\\n        unique_ptr<classname> buildPtr() { \\\n            return make_unique<classname>(move(object)); \\\n        } \\\n    };\n\n// Определение класса Computer\nDECLARE_BUILDER(Computer);\n\nBEGIN_CLASS(Computer)\n    CLASS_FIELD(string, cpu)\n    CLASS_FIELD(int, ram)\n    CLASS_FIELD(int, storage)\n    CLASS_FIELD(bool, hasGPU)\n    CLASS_FIELD(double, price)\nEND_CLASS(Computer)\n\nBEGIN_BUILDER(Computer)\n    BUILDER_FIELD(Computer, string, cpu)\n    BUILDER_FIELD(Computer, int, ram)\n    BUILDER_FIELD(Computer, int, storage)\n    BUILDER_FIELD(Computer, bool, hasGPU)\n    BUILDER_FIELD(Computer, double, price)\nEND_BUILDER(Computer)\n\nvoid Computer::print() const {\n    cout << \"Computer Configuration:\" << endl;\n    cout << \"  CPU: \" << cpu_ << endl;\n    cout << \"  RAM: \" << ram_ << \" GB\" << endl;\n    cout << \"  Storage: \" << storage_ << \" GB\" << endl;\n    cout << \"  GPU: \" << (hasGPU_ ? \"Yes\" : \"No\") << endl;\n    cout << \"  Price: $\" << price_ << endl;\n}\n\n// Определение класса House\nDECLARE_BUILDER(House);\n\nBEGIN_CLASS(House)\n    CLASS_FIELD(int, rooms)\n    CLASS_FIELD(double, area)\n    CLASS_FIELD(string, address)\n    CLASS_FIELD(bool, hasGarage)\nEND_CLASS(House)\n\nBEGIN_BUILDER(House)\n    BUILDER_FIELD(House, int, rooms)\n    BUILDER_FIELD(House, double, area)\n    BUILDER_FIELD(House, string, address)\n    BUILDER_FIELD(House, bool, hasGarage)\nEND_BUILDER(House)\n\nvoid House::print() const {\n    cout << \"\\nHouse Details:\" << endl;\n    cout << \"  Rooms: \" << rooms_ << endl;\n    cout << \"  Area: \" << area_ << \" sqm\" << endl;\n    cout << \"  Address: \" << address_ << endl;\n    cout << \"  Garage: \" << (hasGarage_ ? \"Yes\" : \"No\") << endl;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    cout << \"Builder Pattern Example:\\n\" << endl;\n    \n    // Создание компьютера через билдер\n    Computer computer = ComputerBuilder()\n        .cpu(\"Intel i7\")\n        .ram(16)\n        .storage(512)\n        .hasGPU(true)\n        .price(999.99)\n        .build();\n    \n    computer.print();\n    \n    // Создание дома через билдер с unique_ptr\n    auto house = HouseBuilder()\n        .rooms(3)\n        .area(120.5)\n        .address(\"123 Main St\")\n        .hasGarage(true)\n        .buildPtr();\n    \n    house->print();\n    \n    // Цепочка вызовов\n    cout << \"\\nChained builder usage:\" << endl;\n    ComputerBuilder()\n        .cpu(\"AMD Ryzen 5\")\n        .ram(8)\n        .storage(256)\n        .build()\n        .print();\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n\nclass Fraction {\nprivate:\n    int numerator;\n    int denominator;\npublic:\n    Fraction(int num, int den) : numerator(num), denominator(den) {}\n    friend std::ostream& operator<<(std::ostream& os, const Fraction& f);\n};\n\nstd::ostream& operator<<(std::ostream& os, const Fraction& f) {\n    os << f.numerator << '/' << f.denominator;\n    return os;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    Fraction f1(3, 4);\n    Fraction f2(7, 8);\n    std::cout << \"Дробь 1: \" << f1 << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"Дробь 2: \" << f2 << std::endl;\n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <string>\nusing namespace std;\n\nstring toLowerCaseManual(const string& str) {\n    string result = str;\n    \n    for(size_t i = 0; i < result.length(); i++) {\n        if(result[i] >= 'A' && result[i] <= 'Z') {\n            result[i] = result[i] + ('a' - 'A');\n        }\n    }\n    \n    return result;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    string text = \"Hello WORLD 123\";\n    string lower = toLowerCaseManual(text);\n    \n    cout << \"Оригинал: \" << text << endl;\n    cout << \"Нижний регистр: \" << lower << endl;\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <climits>\n\nint main() {\n    const int V = 5;\n    int graph[V][V] = {{0, 2, 0, 6, 0},\n                       {2, 0, 3, 8, 5},\n                       {0, 3, 0, 0, 7},\n                       {6, 8, 0, 0, 9},\n                       {0, 5, 7, 9, 0}};\n    \n    bool inMST[V] = {false};\n    int key[V];\n    int parent[V];\n    \n    for (int i = 0; i < V; i++) {\n        key[i] = INT_MAX;\n    }\n    \n    key[0] = 0;\n    parent[0] = -1;\n    \n    for (int count = 0; count < V - 1; count++) {\n        int minKey = INT_MAX, u;\n        \n        for (int v = 0; v < V; v++) {\n            if (!inMST[v] && key[v] < minKey) {\n                minKey = key[v];\n                u = v;\n            }\n        }\n        \n        inMST[u] = true;\n        \n        for (int v = 0; v < V; v++) {\n            if (graph[u][v] && !inMST[v] && graph[u][v] < key[v]) {\n                parent[v] = u;\n                key[v] = graph[u][v];\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    std::cout << \"Ребра минимального остовного дерева:\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"Ребро \\tВес\" << std::endl;\n    int totalWeight = 0;\n    for (int i = 1; i < V; i++) {\n        std::cout << parent[i] << \" - \" << i << \" \\t\" << graph[i][parent[i]] << std::endl;\n        totalWeight += graph[i][parent[i]];\n    }\n    std::cout << \"Общий вес: \" << totalWeight << std::endl;\n    \n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <type_traits>\n#include <cstdint>\n#include <limits>\nusing namespace std;\n\n// Шаблонная функция для проверки вхождения значения в диапазон типа\ntemplate<typename To, typename From>\nconstexpr bool in_range_type(From value) {\n    return value >= numeric_limits<To>::min() && \n           value <= numeric_limits<To>::max();\n}\n\n// Функция для проверки вхождения в заданный диапазон\ntemplate<typename T>\nconstexpr bool in_range(T value, T min_val, T max_val) {\n    return value >= min_val && value <= max_val;\n}\n\n// Проверка безопасного преобразования между целыми типами\ntemplate<typename To, typename From>\nconstexpr bool safe_integer_cast(From value) {\n    static_assert(is_integral_v<From> && is_integral_v<To>, \n                  \"Both types must be integral\");\n    \n    if constexpr (is_signed_v<From> == is_signed_v<To>) {\n        return in_range_type<To>(value);\n    } else if constexpr (is_signed_v<From> && !is_signed_v<To>) {\n        return value >= 0 && static_cast<uintmax_t>(value) <= \n               static_cast<uintmax_t>(numeric_limits<To>::max());\n    } else { // !is_signed_v<From> && is_signed_v<To>\n        return static_cast<uintmax_t>(value) <= \n               static_cast<uintmax_t>(numeric_limits<To>::max());\n    }\n}\n\nint main() {\n    int value = 150;\n    \n    cout << \"Value 150 in range 0..255 (uint8_t): \" \n         << in_range_type<uint8_t>(value) << endl;\n    cout << \"Value 300 in range 0..255 (uint8_t): \" \n         << in_range_type<uint8_t>(300) << endl;\n    \n    cout << \"Value -5 in range 0..100: \" \n         << in_range<int>(-5, 0, 100) << endl;\n    cout << \"Value 50 in range 0..100: \" \n         << in_range<int>(50, 0, 100) << endl;\n    \n    // Дополнительные примеры\n    cout << \"\\nДополнительные проверки:\" << endl;\n    cout << \"int8_t диапазон: [\" << int(numeric_limits<int8_t>::min()) \n         << \", \" << int(numeric_limits<int8_t>::max()) << \"]\" << endl;\n    \n    int8_t small = 127;\n    cout << \"127 в диапазоне int8_t: \" << safe_integer_cast<int8_t>(small) << endl;\n    cout << \"128 в диапазоне int8_t: \" << safe_integer_cast<int8_t>(128) << endl;\n    cout << \"-129 в диапазоне int8_t: \" << safe_integer_cast<int8_t>(-129) << endl;\n    \n    // Проверка с отрицательными числами\n    cout << \"\\nПроверка с отрицательными числами:\" << endl;\n    cout << \"-10 в диапазоне 0..100: \" << in_range(-10, 0, 100) << endl;\n    cout << \"-10 в диапазоне -100..0: \" << in_range(-10, -100, 0) << endl;\n    \n    // Проверка разных типов\n    cout << \"\\nПроверка безопасного преобразования:\" << endl;\n    int16_t medium = 32000;\n    cout << \"32000 (int16_t) в int8_t: \" << safe_integer_cast<int8_t>(medium) << endl;\n    cout << \"32000 (int16_t) в uint16_t: \" << safe_integer_cast<uint16_t>(medium) << endl;\n    \n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <cmath>\nusing namespace std;\n\nstruct Point {\n    double x, y;\n    \n    // Конструктор\n    Point(double x_val = 0, double y_val = 0) : x(x_val), y(y_val) {}\n    \n    // Методы\n    double distanceToOrigin() const {\n        return sqrt(x * x + y * y);\n    }\n    \n    double distanceTo(const Point& other) const {\n        return sqrt((x - other.x) * (x - other.x) + (y - other.y) * (y - other.y));\n    }\n    \n    void move(double dx, double dy) {\n        x += dx;\n        y += dy;\n    }\n    \n    void print() const {\n        cout << \"(\" << x << \", \" << y << \")\" << endl;\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    Point p1(3, 4);\n    Point p2(6, 8);\n    \n    cout << \"Точка 1: \";\n    p1.print();\n    cout << \"Расстояние до начала координат: \" << p1.distanceToOrigin() << endl;\n    \n    cout << \"Точка 2: \";\n    p2.print();\n    cout << \"Расстояние между точками: \" << p1.distanceTo(p2) << endl;\n    \n    p1.move(1, 1);\n    cout << \"Точка 1 после перемещения: \";\n    p1.print();\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <cmath>\n\nstruct Date {\n    int day, month, year;\n    \n    int daysSinceEpoch() const {\n        int m = month;\n        int y = year;\n        if (m < 3) {\n            m += 12;\n            y -= 1;\n        }\n        return day + (153 * m - 457) / 5 + 365 * y + y / 4 - y / 100 + y / 400 - 306;\n    }\n    \n    int daysDifference(const Date& other) const {\n        return std::abs(daysSinceEpoch() - other.daysSinceEpoch());\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    Date date1 = {15, 10, 2023};\n    Date date2 = {25, 10, 2023};\n    \n    std::cout << \"Разница между датами: \" << date1.daysDifference(date2) << \" дней\" << std::endl;\n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <vector>\n#include <queue>\n#include <climits>\nusing namespace std;\n\ntypedef pair<int, int> pii;\n\nvoid dijkstra(vector<vector<pii>>& graph, int src) {\n    int V = graph.size();\n    vector<int> dist(V, INT_MAX);\n    priority_queue<pii, vector<pii>, greater<pii>> pq;\n    dist[src] = 0;\n    pq.push({0, src});\n    while (!pq.empty()) {\n        int u = pq.top().second;\n        int d = pq.top().first;\n        pq.pop();\n        if (d > dist[u]) continue;\n        for (auto& edge : graph[u]) {\n            int v = edge.first;\n            int weight = edge.second;\n            if (dist[u] + weight < dist[v]) {\n                dist[v] = dist[u] + weight;\n                pq.push({dist[v], v});\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    cout << \"Расстояния от вершины \" << src << \":\\n\";\n    for (int i = 0; i < V; i++) {\n        cout << i << \": \" << dist[i] << endl;\n    }\n}\n\nint main() {\n    int V = 5;\n    vector<vector<pii>> graph(V);\n    graph[0].push_back({1, 10});\n    graph[0].push_back({2, 5});\n    graph[1].push_back({2, 2});\n    graph[1].push_back({3, 1});\n    graph[2].push_back({1, 3});\n    graph[2].push_back({3, 9});\n    graph[2].push_back({4, 2});\n    graph[3].push_back({4, 4});\n    graph[4].push_back({3, 6});\n    dijkstra(graph, 0);\n    return 0;\n}

#include <iterator>\n#include <vector>\n#include <string>\n#include <iostream>\nusing namespace std;\n\nclass DataMover {\n    vector<string> data;\npublic:\n    void addData(string value) {\n        data.push_back(move(value));\n    }\n    \n    vector<string> extractData() {\n        vector<string> result;\n        result.insert(result.end(),\n                     make_move_iterator(data.begin()),\n                     make_move_iterator(data.end()));\n        data.clear();\n        return result;\n    }\n    \n    template<typename InputIt>\n    void moveData(InputIt first, InputIt last) {\n        data.insert(data.end(),\n                   make_move_iterator(first),\n                   make_move_iterator(last));\n    }\n    \n    void display() const {\n        cout << \"DataMover содержит \" << data.size() << \" элементов:\" << endl;\n        for(const auto& item : data) {\n            cout << \"  '\" << item << \"'\" << endl;\n        }\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    DataMover mover;\n    mover.addData(\"first\");\n    mover.addData(\"second\");\n    mover.addData(\"third\");\n    \n    mover.display();\n    \n    vector<string> extracted = mover.extractData();\n    cout << \"\\nИзвлечено \" << extracted.size() << \" элементов\" << endl;\n    \n    mover.display();\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <vector>\n#include <memory>\n#include <stdexcept>\n\ntemplate<typename T>\nclass ObjectPool {\n    struct PoolItem {\n        T object;\n        bool inUse;\n        PoolItem() : inUse(false) {}\n    };\n    \n    std::vector<PoolItem> pool;\n    std::size_t maxSize;\n    \npublic:\n    ObjectPool(std::size_t size) : maxSize(size) {\n        pool.reserve(size);\n        for(std::size_t i = 0; i < size; ++i) {\n            pool.emplace_back();\n        }\n        std::cout << \"Пул объектов размером \" << size << \" создан\" << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    ~ObjectPool() {\n        std::cout << \"Пул объектов размером \" << pool.size() << \" разрушен\" << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    ObjectPool(const ObjectPool&) = delete;\n    ObjectPool& operator=(const ObjectPool&) = delete;\n    \n    T* acquire() {\n        for(auto& item : pool) {\n            if(!item.inUse) {\n                item.inUse = true;\n                std::cout << \"Объект получен из пула\" << std::endl;\n                return &item.object;\n            }\n        }\n        throw std::runtime_error(\"Нет свободных объектов в пуле\");\n    }\n    \n    void release(T* obj) {\n        for(auto& item : pool) {\n            if(&item.object == obj) {\n                item.inUse = false;\n                std::cout << \"Объект возвращен в пул\" << std::endl;\n                return;\n            }\n        }\n        throw std::invalid_argument(\"Объект не принадлежит этому пулу\");\n    }\n    \n    std::size_t availableCount() const {\n        std::size_t count = 0;\n        for(const auto& item : pool) {\n            if(!item.inUse) ++count;\n        }\n        return count;\n    }\n};\n\nclass Connection {\n    int id;\npublic:\n    Connection() : id(0) {\n        std::cout << \"Соединение создано\" << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    ~Connection() {\n        std::cout << \"Соединение разрушено\" << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    void connect(int connId) {\n        id = connId;\n        std::cout << \"Соединение \" << id << \" установлено\" << std::endl;\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    ObjectPool<Connection> pool(3);\n    \n    Connection* conn1 = pool.acquire();\n    conn1->connect(1);\n    \n    Connection* conn2 = pool.acquire();\n    conn2->connect(2);\n    \n    std::cout << \"Доступно объектов: \" << pool.availableCount() << std::endl;\n    \n    pool.release(conn1);\n    \n    Connection* conn3 = pool.acquire();\n    conn3->connect(3);\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <memory>\n#include <vector>\n#include <string>\n#include <ctime>\n#include <iomanip>\nusing namespace std;\n\nclass Vehicle {\nprotected:\n    string licensePlate;\n    string model;\n    double dailyRate;\n    bool isAvailable;\n    time_t nextAvailableDate;\n    \npublic:\n    Vehicle(string plate, string mdl, double rate) \n        : licensePlate(move(plate)), model(move(mdl)), dailyRate(rate), \n          isAvailable(true), nextAvailableDate(0) {}\n    \n    virtual ~Vehicle() = default;\n    \n    virtual double calculateRentalCost(int days) const {\n        return days * dailyRate;\n    }\n    \n    virtual bool rentVehicle(int days) {\n        if (isAvailable) {\n            isAvailable = false;\n            time_t now = time(nullptr);\n            nextAvailableDate = now + (days * 24 * 60 * 60);\n            cout << model << \" rented for \" << days << \" days. Cost: $\" \n                 << fixed << setprecision(2) << calculateRentalCost(days) << endl;\n            return true;\n        }\n        cout << model << \" is not available until \" << ctime(&nextAvailableDate);\n        return false;\n    }\n    \n    virtual void returnVehicle() {\n        isAvailable = true;\n        nextAvailableDate = 0;\n        cout << model << \" has been returned.\" << endl;\n    }\n    \n    virtual void displayInfo() const = 0;\n    virtual string getVehicleType() const = 0;\n    \n    bool getIsAvailable() const { return isAvailable; }\n    string getLicensePlate() const { return licensePlate; }\n    string getModel() const { return model; }\n    double getDailyRate() const { return dailyRate; }\n};\n\nclass Car : public Vehicle {\n    int passengerCapacity;\n    bool hasAC;\n    \npublic:\n    Car(string plate, string mdl, double rate, int capacity, bool ac)\n        : Vehicle(move(plate), move(mdl), rate), \n          passengerCapacity(capacity), hasAC(ac) {}\n    \n    void displayInfo() const override {\n        cout << \"[CAR] \" << model << \" (\" << licensePlate << \")\" << endl;\n        cout << \"  Daily rate: $\" << fixed << setprecision(2) << dailyRate << endl;\n        cout << \"  Passengers: \" << passengerCapacity << endl;\n        cout << \"  AC: \" << (hasAC ? \"Yes\" : \"No\") << endl;\n        cout << \"  Available: \" << (isAvailable ? \"Yes\" : \"No\") << endl;\n    }\n    \n    string getVehicleType() const override { return \"Car\"; }\n    \n    int getPassengerCapacity() const { return passengerCapacity; }\n    bool getHasAC() const { return hasAC; }\n};\n\nclass Motorcycle : public Vehicle {\n    string engineType;\n    bool hasHelmet;\n    \npublic:\n    Motorcycle(string plate, string mdl, double rate, string engine, bool helmet)\n        : Vehicle(move(plate), move(mdl), rate), \n          engineType(move(engine)), hasHelmet(helmet) {}\n    \n    void displayInfo() const override {\n        cout << \"[MOTORCYCLE] \" << model << \" (\" << licensePlate << \")\" << endl;\n        cout << \"  Daily rate: $\" << fixed << setprecision(2) << dailyRate << endl;\n        cout << \"  Engine: \" << engineType << endl;\n        cout << \"  Helmet included: \" << (hasHelmet ? \"Yes\" : \"No\") << endl;\n        cout << \"  Available: \" << (isAvailable ? \"Yes\" : \"No\") << endl;\n    }\n    \n    string getVehicleType() const override { return \"Motorcycle\"; }\n    \n    string getEngineType() const { return engineType; }\n    bool getHasHelmet() const { return hasHelmet; }\n};\n\nclass Truck : public Vehicle {\n    double cargoCapacity;\n    bool hasTrailer;\n    \npublic:\n    Truck(string plate, string mdl, double rate, double capacity, bool trailer)\n        : Vehicle(move(plate), move(mdl), rate), \n          cargoCapacity(capacity), hasTrailer(trailer) {}\n    \n    double calculateRentalCost(int days) const override {\n        double baseCost = days * dailyRate;\n        if (hasTrailer) {\n            baseCost += 50 * days; // Extra for trailer\n        }\n        return baseCost;\n    }\n    \n    void displayInfo() const override {\n        cout << \"[TRUCK] \" << model << \" (\" << licensePlate << \")\" << endl;\n        cout << \"  Daily rate: $\" << fixed << setprecision(2) << dailyRate << endl;\n        cout << \"  Cargo capacity: \" << cargoCapacity << \" tons\" << endl;\n        cout << \"  Trailer: \" << (hasTrailer ? \"Yes\" : \"No\") << endl;\n        cout << \"  Available: \" << (isAvailable ? \"Yes\" : \"No\") << endl;\n    }\n    \n    string getVehicleType() const override { return \"Truck\"; }\n    \n    double getCargoCapacity() const { return cargoCapacity; }\n    bool getHasTrailer() const { return hasTrailer; }\n};\n\nclass RentalAgency {\n    vector<unique_ptr<Vehicle>> vehicles;\n    double totalRevenue;\n    \npublic:\n    RentalAgency() : totalRevenue(0) {}\n    \n    void addVehicle(unique_ptr<Vehicle> vehicle) {\n        vehicles.push_back(move(vehicle));\n    }\n    \n    Vehicle* findAvailableVehicle(const string& type) {\n        for (const auto& vehicle : vehicles) {\n            if (vehicle->getVehicleType() == type && vehicle->getIsAvailable()) {\n                return vehicle.get();\n            }\n        }\n        return nullptr;\n    }\n    \n    bool rentVehicle(const string& licensePlate, int days) {\n        for (const auto& vehicle : vehicles) {\n            if (vehicle->getLicensePlate() == licensePlate) {\n                if (vehicle->rentVehicle(days)) {\n                    totalRevenue += vehicle->calculateRentalCost(days);\n                    return true;\n                }\n                return false;\n            }\n        }\n        cout << \"Vehicle not found.\" << endl;\n        return false;\n    }\n    \n    void returnVehicle(const string& licensePlate) {\n        for (const auto& vehicle : vehicles) {\n            if (vehicle->getLicensePlate() == licensePlate) {\n                vehicle->returnVehicle();\n                return;\n            }\n        }\n        cout << \"Vehicle not found.\" << endl;\n    }\n    \n    void displayAllVehicles() const {\n        cout << \"\\n=== ALL VEHICLES ===\" << endl;\n        for (const auto& vehicle : vehicles) {\n            vehicle->displayInfo();\n            cout << endl;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    void displayAvailableVehicles() const {\n        cout << \"\\n=== AVAILABLE VEHICLES ===\" << endl;\n        for (const auto& vehicle : vehicles) {\n            if (vehicle->getIsAvailable()) {\n                vehicle->displayInfo();\n                cout << endl;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    void displayStatistics() const {\n        cout << \"\\n=== AGENCY STATISTICS ===\" << endl;\n        cout << \"Total vehicles: \" << vehicles.size() << endl;\n        \n        int cars = 0, motorcycles = 0, trucks = 0;\n        int available = 0;\n        \n        for (const auto& vehicle : vehicles) {\n            if (vehicle->getIsAvailable()) available++;\n            \n            if (vehicle->getVehicleType() == \"Car\") cars++;\n            else if (vehicle->getVehicleType() == \"Motorcycle\") motorcycles++;\n            else if (vehicle->getVehicleType() == \"Truck\") trucks++;\n        }\n        \n        cout << \"Cars: \" << cars << endl;\n        cout << \"Motorcycles: \" << motorcycles << endl;\n        cout << \"Trucks: \" << trucks << endl;\n        cout << \"Available: \" << available << endl;\n        cout << \"Rented: \" << (vehicles.size() - available) << endl;\n        cout << \"Total revenue: $\" << fixed << setprecision(2) << totalRevenue << endl;\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    RentalAgency agency;\n    \n    agency.addVehicle(make_unique<Car>(\"ABC123\", \"Toyota Camry\", 45.99, 5, true));\n agency.addVehicle(make_unique<Truck>(\"TRUCK1\", \"Ford F-150\", 79.99, 1.5, false));\n    agency.addVehicle(make_unique<Truck>(\"TRUCK2\", \"Freightliner\", 149.99, 10.0, true));\n    \n    agency.displayAllVehicles();\n    agency.displayStatistics();\n    \n    cout << \"\\n=== RENTING VEHICLES ===\" << endl;\n    agency.rentVehicle(\"ABC123\", 3);\n    agency.rentVehicle(\"MOTO1\", 7);\n    \n    agency.displayAvailableVehicles();\n    \n    cout << \"\\n=== TRYING TO RENT UNAVAILABLE VEHICLE ===\" << endl;\n    agency.rentVehicle(\"ABC123\", 2);\n    \n    cout << \"\\n=== #include <iostream>\n#include <string>\n#include <stack>\n#include <unordered_map>\n#include <vector>\nusing namespace std;\n\nbool checkBracketsBalance(const string& expr) {\n    stack<char> s;\n    unordered_map<char, char> brackets = {\n        {')', '('},\n        {']', '['},\n        {'}', '{'},\n        {'>', '<'}\n    };\n    \n    for(char c : expr) {\n        if(c == '(' || c == '[' || c == '{' || c == '<') {\n            s.push(c);\n        } else if(c == ')' || c == ']' || c == '}' || c == '>') {\n            if(s.empty() || s.top() != brackets[c]) {\n                return false;\n            }\n            s.pop();\n        }\n    }\n    \n    return s.empty();\n}\n\nint main() {\n    vector<string> tests = {\n        \"(a + b) * (c - d)\",\n        \"{[()]}\",\n        \"{[()()]}\",\n        \"{[(()]}\",\n        \"\",\n        \"a + b\",\n        \"<html><body></body></html>\",\n        \"{[}]\",\n        \"((())){{{}}}[[[]]]\",\n        \")(\"\n    };\n    \n    cout << \"Bracket Balance Check:\\n\";\n    for(const string& test : tests) {\n        bool balanced = checkBracketsBalance(test);\n        cout << \"\\\"\" << test << \"\\\" : \" << (balanced ? \"BALANCED\" : \"UNBALANCED\") << endl;\n    }\n    \n    // Дополнительно: найти позицию первой ошибки\n    string complex = \"{(a + b) * [c - d]} / (e + f)\";\n    cout << \"\\nComplex test: \" << complex << endl;\n    cout << \"Result: \" << (checkBracketsBalance(complex) ? \"OK\" : \"ERROR\") << endl;\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\nusing namespace std;\n\nclass SimpleDate {\n    int day, month, year;\npublic:\n    SimpleDate(int d, int m, int y) : day(d), month(m), year(y) {}\n    void print() const { cout << day << \".\" << month << \".\" << year << endl; }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    SimpleDate date(20, 10, 2023);\n    date.print();\n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <vector>\n#include <cmath>\n#include <iomanip>\n#include <limits>\n#include <utility>\n\nconst double EPS = 1e-10;\nconst int MAX_ITER = 50;\n\n// Функция f1(x,y) = x² + y² - 4\ndouble f1(double x, double y) {\n    return x * x + y * y - 4;\n}\n\n// Функция f2(x,y) = x² - y - 1\ndouble f2(double x, double y) {\n    return x * x - y - 1;\n}\n\n// Производные для якобиана\ndouble df1_dx(double x, double y) { return 2 * x; }\ndouble df1_dy(double x, double y) { return 2 * y; }\ndouble df2_dx(double x, double y) { return 2 * x; }\ndouble df2_dy(double x, double y) { return -1; }\n\n// Вычисление якобиана\nvoid computeJacobian(double x, double y, std::vector<std::vector<double>>& J) {\n    J[0][0] = df1_dx(x, y);\n    J[0][1] = df1_dy(x, y);\n    J[1][0] = df2_dx(x, y);\n    J[1][1] = df2_dy(x, y);\n}\n\n// Вычисление определителя матрицы 2x2\ndouble det2x2(const std::vector<std::vector<double>>& A) {\n    return A[0][0] * A[1][1] - A[0][1] * A[1][0];\n}\n\n// Решение системы линейных уравнений 2x2\nstd::vector<double> solveLinear2x2(const std::vector<std::vector<double>>& A, const std::vector<double>& b) {\n    double det = det2x2(A);\n    \n    if (std::fabs(det) < EPS) {\n        return {0, 0};\n    }\n    \n    std::vector<double> x(2);\n    x[0] = (b[0] * A[1][1] - b[1] * A[0][1]) / det;\n    x[1] = (A[0][0] * b[1] - A[1][0] * b[0]) / det;\n    \n    return x;\n}\n\n// Метод Ньютона для системы 2 уравнений\nstd::vector<double> newtonMethod(double x0, double y0, double epsilon, int maxIter) {\n    double x = x0;\n    double y = y0;\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\n=== МЕТОД НЬЮТОНА ДЛЯ СИСТЕМЫ УРАВНЕНИЙ ===\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"f1(x,y) = x² + y² - 4 = 0\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"f2(x,y) = x² - y - 1 = 0\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"Начальное приближение: (\" << x0 << \", \" << y0 << \")\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"Точность: \" << epsilon << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"Максимальное число итераций: \" << maxIter << std::endl;\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\n=== ПРОЦЕСС ИТЕРАЦИЙ ===\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"Итер.\\tx\\t\\ty\\t\\tf1(x,y)\\tf2(x,y)\\tНорма\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"--------------------------------------------------------\" << std::endl;\n    \n    std::vector<std::vector<double>> J(2, std::vector<double>(2));\n    std::vector<double> F(2);\n    \n    for (int iter = 0; iter < maxIter; iter++) {\n        // Вычисляем функции\n        F[0] = f1(x, y);\n        F[1] = f2(x, y);\n        \n        // Вычисляем норму невязки\n        double norm = std::sqrt(F[0] * F[0] + F[1] * F[1]);\n        \n        // Вывод текущего состояния\n        std::cout << std::setw(3) << iter << \"\\t\"\n                  << std::fixed << std::setprecision(8) << x << \"\\t\" << y << \"\\t\"\n                  << F[0] << \"\\t\" << F[1] << \"\\t\" << norm << std::endl;\n        \n        // Проверка сходимости\n        if (norm < epsilon) {\n            std::cout << \"\\n✓ Сходимость достигнута на итерации \" << iter << std::endl;\n            std::cout << \"Норма невязки: \" << norm << \" < \" << epsilon << std::endl;\n            return {x, y};\n        }\n        \n        // Вычисляем якобиан\n        computeJacobian(x, y, J);\n        \n        // Проверяем, что якобиан не вырожден\n        double detJ = det2x2(J);\n        if (std::fabs(detJ) < EPS) {\n            std::cout << \"\\n✗ Якобиан вырожден! det(J) = \" << detJ << std::endl;\n            std::cout << \"Метод не может быть продолжен.\" << std::endl;\n            return {x, y};\n        }\n        \n        // Решаем линейную систему J * Δ = -F\n        std::vector<double> delta = solveLinear2x2(J, {-F[0], -F[1]});\n        \n        // Обновляем переменные\n        x += delta[0];\n        y += delta[1];\n        \n        // Проверка на расходимость\n        if (std::isnan(x) || std::isnan(y) || std::isinf(x) || std::isinf(y)) {\n            std::cout << \"\\n✗ Метод расходится!\" << std::endl;\n            return {x, y};\n        }\n    }\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\n✗ Достигнуто максимальное количество итераций!\" << std::endl;\n    return {x, y};\n}\n\n// Функция для проверки решения\nvoid checkSolution(double x, double y) {\n    std::cout << \"\\n=== ПРОВЕРКА РЕШЕНИЯ ===\" << std::endl;\n    \n    double f1_val = f1(x, y);\n    double f2_val = f2(x, y);\n    \n    std::cout << \"f1(\" << x << \", \" << y << \") = \" << f1_val << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"f2(\" << x << \", \" << y << \") = \" << f2_val << std::endl;\n    \n    if (std::fabs(f1_val) < EPS && std::fabs(f2_val) < EPS) {\n        std::cout << \"✓ Решение удовлетворяет уравнениям с точностью \" << EPS << std::endl;\n    } else {\n        std::cout << \"✗ Решение не удовлетворяет уравнениям с требуемой точностью\" << std::endl;\n    }\n}\n\n// Функция для анализа сходимости из разных начальных точек\nvoid convergenceAnalysis() {\n    std::cout << \"\\n=== АНАЛИЗ СХОДИМОСТИ ИЗ РАЗНЫХ НАЧАЛЬНЫХ ТОЧЕК ===\" << std::endl;\n    \n    std::vector<std::pair<double, double>> initialPoints = {\n        {1.0, 1.0}, {2.0, 0.0}, {-1.0, 1.0}, {-2.0, 0.0},\n        {0.0, 2.0}, {0.0, -2.0}, {1.5, 1.5}, {-1.5, -1.5}\n    };\n    \n    std::cout << \"Нач. точка\\tРешение\\t\\tИтер.\\tНорма\\tСходимость\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"----------------------------------------------------------------\" << std::endl;\n    \n    for (const auto& point : initialPoints) {\n        double x0 = point.first;\n        double y0 = point.second;\n        \n        // Запускаем метод Ньютона\n        double x = x0, y = y0;\n        std::vector<std::vector<double>> J(2, std::vector<double>(2));\n        std::vector<double> F(2);\n        \n        int iter;\n        double norm = 0.0;\n        bool converged = false;\n        \n        for (iter = 0; iter < MAX_ITER; iter++) {\n            F[0] = f1(x, y);\n            F[1] = f2(x, y);\n            norm = std::sqrt(F[0] * F[0] + F[1] * F[1]);\n            \n            if (norm < EPS) {\n                converged = true;\n                break;\n            }\n            \n            computeJacobian(x, y, J);\n            double detJ = det2x2(J);\n            \n            if (std::fabs(detJ) < EPS) {\n                break;\n            }\n            \n            std::vector<double> delta = solveLinear2x2(J, {-F[0], -F[1]});\n            x += delta[0];\n            y += delta[1];\n            \n            if (std::isnan(x) || std::isnan(y) || std::isinf(x) || std::isinf(y)) {\n                break;\n            }\n        }\n        \n        std::cout << std::fixed << std::setprecision(2) << \"(\" << x0 << \",\" << y0 << \")\\t\"\n                  << std::setprecision(6) << \"(\" << x << \",\" << y << \")\\t\"\n                  << iter << \"\\t\" << norm << \"\\t\"\n                  << (converged ? \"✓\" : \"✗\") << std::endl;\n    }\n}\n\nint main() {\n    std::cout << \"=== РЕШЕНИЕ СИСТЕМЫ НЕЛИНЕЙНЫХ УРАВНЕНИЙ МЕТОДОМ НЬЮТОНА ===\" << std::endl;\n    \n    // Вывод информации о системе\n    std::cout << \"\\nСистема уравнений:\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"1) x² + y² - 4 = 0\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"2) x² - y - 1 = 0\" << std::endl;\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\nЯкобиан системы:\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"J = [ ∂f1/∂x  ∂f1/∂y ] = [ 2x   2y ]\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"    [ ∂f2/∂x  ∂f2/∂y ]   [ 2x   -1 ]\" << std::endl;\n    \n    // Аналитическое решение для сравнения\n    std::cout << \"\\nАналитическое решение:\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"Из второго уравнения: y = x² - 1\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"Подставляем в первое: x² + (x² - 1)² - 4 = 0\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"x⁴ - x² - 3 = 0\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"Корни: x² = (1 ± √13)/2\" << std::endl;\n    \n    double sqrt13 = std::sqrt(13);\n    double x1_sq = (1 + sqrt13) / 2;\n    double x2_sq = (1 - sqrt13) / 2;\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\nВозможные решения:\" << std::endl;\n    if (x1_sq >= 0) {\n        double x1 = std::sqrt(x1_sq);\n        double y1 = x1_sq - 1;\n        std::cout << \"1) (\" << x1 << \", \" << y1 << \")\" << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"2) (\" << -x1 << \", \" << y1 << \")\" << std::endl;\n    }\n    if (x2_sq >= 0) {\n        double x2 = std::sqrt(x2_sq);\n        double y2 = x2_sq - 1;\n        std::cout << \"3) (\" << x2 << \", \" << y2 << \")\" << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"4) (\" << -x2 << \", \" << y2 << \")\" << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    // Ввод начального приближения\n    double x0, y0;\n    std::cout << \"\\nВведите начальное приближение (x0 y0): \";\n    std::cin >> x0 >> y0;\n    \n    double epsilon;\n    std::cout << \"Введите точность вычислений (например, 1e-8): \";\n    std::cin >> epsilon;\n    \n    // Запуск метода Ньютона\n    std::vector<double> solution = newtonMethod(x0, y0, epsilon, MAX_ITER);\n    \n    // Проверка решения\n    checkSolution(solution[0], solution[1]);\n    \n    // Анализ сходимости\n    convergenceAnalysis();\n    \n    // Визуализация\n    std::cout << \"\\n=== ВИЗУАЛИЗАЦИЯ ===\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"Уравнение 1: x² + y² = 4 (окружность радиусом 2)\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"Уравнение 2: y = x² - 1 (парабола)\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"Точки пересечения - решения системы.\" << std::endl;\n    \n    // Построение простой текстовой визуализации\n    std::cout << \"\\nТекстовая визуализация (масштаб 21x21):\" << std::endl;\n    int size = 21;\n    double scale = 0.3;\n    \n    for (int i = -size/2; i <= size/2; i++) {\n        for (int j = -size/2; j <= size/2; j++) {\n            double x = j * scale;\n            double y = -i * scale; // Инвертируем y для корректного отображения\n            \n            // Проверяем принадлежность к уравнениям\n            bool onCircle = std::fabs(x*x + y*y - 4) < 0.2;\n            bool onParabola = std::fabs(y - (x*x - 1)) < 0.2;\n            \n            if (onCircle && onParabola) {\n                std::cout << \"X\"; // Точка пересечения\n            } else if (onCircle) {\n                std::cout << \"O\"; // Окружность\n            } else if (onParabola) {\n                std::cout << \"*\"; // Парабола\n            } else if (std::fabs(x) < 0.1 && std::fabs(y) < 0.1) {\n                std::cout << \"+\"; // Центр координат\n            } else if (std::fabs(x) < 0.1) {\n                std::cout << \"|\"; // Ось Y\n            } else if (std::fabs(y) < 0.1) {\n                std::cout << \"-\"; // Ось X\n            } else {\n                std::cout << \" \";\n            }\n            std::cout << \" \";\n        }\n        std::cout << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\nЛегенда:\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"O - окружность x² + y² = 4\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"* - парабола y = x² - 1\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"X - точки пересечения (решения)\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"+ - центр координат\" << std::endl;\n    \n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <string>\n#include <algorithm>\n\nint levenshteinDistance(const std::string& s1, const std::string& s2) {\n    int m = s1.length(), n = s2.length();\n    int dist[m+1][n+1];\n    \n    for(int i = 0; i <= m; i++) dist[i][0] = i;\n    for(int j = 0; j <= n; j++) dist[0][j] = j;\n    \n    for(int i = 1; i <= m; i++) {\n        for(int j = 1; j <= n; j++) {\n            int cost = (s1[i-1] == s2[j-1]) ? 0 : 1;\n            dist[i][j] = std::min({dist[i-1][j] + 1, dist[i][j-1] + 1, dist[i-1][j-1] + cost});\n        }\n    }\n    \n    return dist[m][n];\n}\n\nint main() {\n    std::string s1 = \"кот\", s2 = \"скат\";\n    std::cout << \"Расстояние Левенштейна между \\\"\" << s1 << \"\\\" и \\\"\" << s2 << \"\\\": \" << levenshteinDistance(s1, s2) << std::endl;\n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <string>\n#include <vector>\n#include <algorithm>\n#include <stdexcept>\nusing namespace std;\n\nclass BookException : public runtime_error {\npublic:\n    BookException(const string& msg) : runtime_error(msg) {}\n};\n\nclass Book {\nprivate:\n    string isbn;\n    string title;\n    string author;\n    bool available;\n    \npublic:\n    Book(const string& i, const string& t, const string& a) \n        : isbn(i), title(t), author(a), available(true) {\n        if (isbn.empty() || title.empty() || author.empty()) {\n            throw invalid_argument(\"Book fields cannot be empty\");\n        }\n        if (isbn.length() != 13) {\n            throw invalid_argument(\"ISBN must be 13 characters long\");\n        }\n    }\n    \n    const string& get_isbn() const { return isbn; }\n    const string& get_title() const { return title; }\n    bool is_available() const { return available; }\n    \n    void borrow() {\n        if (!available) {\n            throw BookException(\"Book is already borrowed\");\n        }\n        available = false;\n    }\n    \n    void return_book() {\n        if (available) {\n            throw BookException(\"Book is not borrowed\");\n        }\n        available = true;\n    }\n    \n    void display() const {\n        cout << \"ISBN: \" << isbn \n             << \", Title: \" << title \n             << \", Author: \" << author\n             << \", Available: \" << (available ? \"Yes\" : \"No\") << endl;\n    }\n};\n\nclass Library {\nprivate:\n    vector<Book> books;\n    \npublic:\n    void add_book(const Book& book) {\n        for (const auto& b : books) {\n            if (b.get_isbn() == book.get_isbn()) {\n                throw BookException(\"Book with same ISBN already exists\");\n            }\n        }\n        books.push_back(book);\n    }\n    \n    Book& find_book(const string& isbn) {\n        auto it = find_if(books.begin(), books.end(), \n            [&](const Book& b) { return b.get_isbn() == isbn; });\n        \n        if (it == books.end()) {\n            throw BookException(\"Book not found: \" + isbn);\n        }\n        \n        return *it;\n    }\n    \n    void borrow_book(const string& isbn) {\n        Book& book = find_book(isbn);\n        book.borrow();\n        cout << \"Book borrowed successfully: \" << book.get_title() << endl;\n    }\n    \n    void return_book(const string& isbn) {\n        Book& book = find_book(isbn);\n        book.return_book();\n        cout << \"Book returned successfully: \" << book.get_title() << endl;\n    }\n    \n    void display_all_books() const {\n        if (books.empty()) {\n            cout << \"Library is empty\" << endl;\n            return;\n        }\n        \n        for (const auto& book : books) {\n            book.display();\n        }\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    Library library;\n    \n    try {\n        Book b1(\"1234567890123\", \"The Great Gatsby\", \"F. Scott Fitzgerald\");\n        Book b2(\"9876543210987\", \"1984\", \"George Orwell\");\n        Book b3(\"1234567890123\", \"Duplicate\", \"Author\");  // This will throw\n        \n        library.add_book(b1);\n        library.add_book(b2);\n        \n        library.display_all_books();\n        \n        library.borrow_book(\"1234567890123\");\n        library.borrow_book(\"1234567890123\");  // This will throw\n        \n    } catch (const BookException& e) {\n        cout << \"Library error: \" << e.what() << endl;\n    } catch (const invalid_argument& e) {\n        cout << \"Invalid argument: \" << e.what() << endl;\n    }\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n\nint main() {\n    int rows = 3, cols = 4;\n    int nnz = 4;\n    double* values = new double[nnz] {5.0, 8.0, 3.0, 6.0};\n    int* colIndices = new int[nnz] {1, 2, 0, 3};\n    int* rowPtr = new int[rows + 1] {0, 1, 2, 4};\n    double* vec = new double[cols] {1.0, 2.0, 3.0, 4.0};\n    double* result = new double[rows]();\n    for(int i = 0; i < rows; i++) {\n        for(int j = rowPtr[i]; j < rowPtr[i+1]; j++) {\n            result[i] += values[j] * vec[colIndices[j]];\n        }\n    }\n    std::cout << \"Результат умножения разреженной матрицы на вектор:\" << std::endl;\n    for(int i = 0; i < rows; i++) {\n        std::cout << result[i] << \" \";\n    }\n    std::cout << std::endl;\n    delete[] values;\n    delete[] colIndices;\n    delete[] rowPtr;\n    delete[] vec;\n    delete[] result;\n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <vector>\n#include <cmath>\nusing namespace std;\n\nint sumOfDivisors(int num) {\n    if (num <= 1) return 0;\n    int sum = 1; // 1 всегда является делителем\n    int limit = sqrt(num);\n    \n    for (int i = 2; i <= limit; ++i) {\n        if (num % i == 0) {\n            sum += i;\n            if (i != num / i) {\n                sum += num / i;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    return sum;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    int N;\n    cout << \"Введите верхнюю границу диапазона (N >= 10): \";\n    cin >> N;\n    \n    if (N < 10) {\n        cout << \"Для поиска дружественных чисел нужен диапазон от 10.\" << endl;\n        return 1;\n    }\n    \n    vector<int> divisorSums(N + 1);\n    \n    // Вычисляем суммы делителей для всех чисел\n    cout << \"\\nВычисление сумм делителей:\\n\";\n    for (int i = 1; i <= N; ++i) {\n        divisorSums[i] = sumOfDivisors(i);\n        if (i <= 20) { // Показываем только первые 20 для наглядности\n            cout << \"σ(\" << i << \") = \" << divisorSums[i] << endl;\n        }\n    }\n    if (N > 20) {\n        cout << \"... (пропущены числа 21..\" << N << \")\\n\";\n    }\n    \n    // Поиск дружественных пар\n    cout << \"\\nПоиск дружественных чисел в диапазоне 1..\" << N << \":\\n\";\n    vector<bool> paired(N + 1, false);\n    int pairCount = 0;\n    \n    for (int a = 2; a <= N; ++a) {\n        int b = divisorSums[a];\n        \n        if (b > N || b <= a || paired[a]) {\n            continue;\n        }\n        \n        if (divisorSums[b] == a) {\n            cout << \"Найдена дружественная пара: \" << a << \" и \" << b << endl;\n            cout << \"  σ(\" << a << \") = \" << divisorSums[a] << \" = \" << b << endl;\n            cout << \"  σ(\" << b << \") = \" << divisorSums[b] << \" = \" << a << endl;\n            \n            // Вывод делителей для наглядности\n            cout << \"  Делители \" << a << \": 1\";\n            for (int i = 2; i <= a/2; ++i) {\n                if (a % i == 0) cout << \" + \" << i;\n            }\n            cout << \" = \" << divisorSums[a] << endl;\n            \n            cout << \"  Делители \" << b << \": 1\";\n            for (int i = 2; i <= b/2; ++i) {\n                if (b % i == 0) cout << \" + \" << i;\n            }\n            cout << \" = \" << divisorSums[b] << \"\\n\\n\";\n            \n            paired[a] = paired[b] = true;\n            pairCount++;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    if (pairCount == 0) {\n        cout << \"Дружественные числа не найдены в данном диапазоне.\\n\";\n    } else {\n        cout << \"Всего найдено пар: \" << pairCount << endl;\n    }\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <string>\nusing namespace std;\n\nclass Route {\npublic:\n    string start, finish;\n    Route(string s, string f) : start(s), finish(f) {}\n};\n\nint main() {\n    Route trip(\"Moscow\", \"Saint Petersburg\");\n    cout << \"Route: \" << trip.start << \" -> \" << trip.finish << endl;\n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <string>\n#include <memory>\n#include <vector>\n#include <type_traits>\n#include <utility>\n#include <tuple>\nusing namespace std;\n\n// Базовый класс для всех миксинов\ntemplate<typename Derived>\nclass Cloneable {\npublic:\n    virtual ~Cloneable() = default;\n    \n    unique_ptr<Derived> clone() const {\n        return unique_ptr<Derived>(static_cast<Derived*>(cloneImpl()));\n    }\n    \nprotected:\n    virtual Cloneable* cloneImpl() const = 0;\n};\n\n// Миксин для добавления идентификатора\ntemplate<typename Derived>\nclass Identifiable {\n    static int nextId;\n    int id;\nprotected:\n    Identifiable() : id(nextId++) {}\n    \npublic:\n    int getId() const { return id; }\n    \n    void printId() const {\n        cout << \"ID: \" << id << endl;\n    }\n};\n\ntemplate<typename Derived>\nint Identifiable<Derived>::nextId = 1;\n\n// Миксин для добавления имени\ntemplate<typename Derived>\nclass Nameable {\n    string name;\nprotected:\n    Nameable(const string& n = \"\") : name(n) {}\n    \npublic:\n    void setName(const string& n) { name = n; }\n    string getName() const { return name; }\n    \n    void printName() const {\n        cout << \"Name: \" << name << endl;\n    }\n};\n\n// Миксин для добавления стоимости\ntemplate<typename Derived>\nclass Pricable {\n    double price;\nprotected:\n    Pricable(double p = 0.0) : price(p) {}\n    \npublic:\n    void setPrice(double p) { price = p; }\n    double getPrice() const { return price; }\n    \n    void printPrice() const {\n        cout << \"Price: $\" << price << endl;\n    }\n};\n\n// Миксин для добавления сериализации\ntemplate<typename Derived>\nclass Serializable {\nprotected:\n    Serializable() = default;\n    \npublic:\n    virtual string serialize() const {\n        return \"Serialized object\";\n    }\n    \n    void printSerialized() const {\n        cout << \"Serialized: \" << serialize() << endl;\n    }\n};\n\n// Дополнительный миксин с другим конструктором\ntemplate<typename Derived>\nclass Describable {\n    string description;\nprotected:\n    Describable(const string& desc = \"\") : description(desc) {}\n    \npublic:\n    void setDescription(const string& desc) { description = desc; }\n    string getDescription() const { return description; }\n    \n    void printDescription() const {\n        cout << \"Description: \" << description << endl;\n    }\n};\n\n// Базовый класс для всех продуктов с поддержкой клонирования\nclass ProductBase : public Cloneable<ProductBase> {\nprotected:\n    virtual ProductBase* cloneImpl() const override {\n        return nullptr; // Абстрактный класс\n    }\n};\n\n// Вспомогательная метафункция для проверки наличия миксина\ntemplate<typename T, template<typename> class Mixin>\nstruct has_mixin {\nprivate:\n    template<typename U>\n    static true_type test(const Mixin<U>*);\n    \n    static false_type test(...);\n    \npublic:\n    static constexpr bool value = decltype(test(static_cast<T*>(nullptr)))::value;\n};\n\ntemplate<typename T, template<typename> class Mixin>\nconstexpr bool has_mixin_v = has_mixin<T, Mixin>::value;\n\n// Конкретный класс, использующий миксины\ntemplate<typename... Mixins>\nclass Product : public ProductBase, public Mixins... {\npublic:\n    // Конструктор с perfect forwarding для аргументов миксинов\n    template<typename... Args>\n    Product(Args&&... args) : Mixins(forward<Args>(args))... {\n        cout << \"Product created with \" << sizeof...(Args) << \" arguments\" << endl;\n    }\n    \n    void printAll() const {\n        // Fold expressions для вызова методов всех миксинов\n        (static_cast<void>(Mixins::printId()), ...);\n        (static_cast<void>(Mixins::printName()), ...);\n        (static_cast<void>(Mixins::printPrice()), ...);\n    }\n    \n    // Проверка наличия функциональности с помощью SFINAE и if constexpr\n    template<typename T = Product>\n    auto serializeIfAvailable() const -> string {\n        if constexpr (has_mixin_v<T, Serializable>) {\n            return static_cast<const Serializable<T>*>(this)->serialize();\n        } else {\n            return \"No serialization available\";\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // Проверка наличия метода getPrice\n    template<typename T = Product>\n    auto getPriceIfAvailable() const -> double {\n        if constexpr (has_mixin_v<T, Pricable>) {\n            return static_cast<const Pricable<T>*>(this)->getPrice();\n        } else {\n            return 0.0;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // Проверка наличия метода getName\n    template<typename T = Product>\n    auto getNameIfAvailable() const -> string {\n        if constexpr (has_mixin_v<T, Nameable>) {\n            return static_cast<const Nameable<T>*>(this)->getName();\n        } else {\n            return \"No name available\";\n        }\n    }\n    \nprotected:\n    ProductBase* cloneImpl() const override {\n        return new Product(*this);\n    }\n};\n\n// Определение конкретных типов продуктов\nstruct SimpleProduct : Product<Identifiable<SimpleProduct>, Nameable<SimpleProduct>, Pricable<SimpleProduct>> {\n    using Base = Product<Identifiable<SimpleProduct>, Nameable<SimpleProduct>, Pricable<SimpleProduct>>;\n    using Base::Base; // Наследуем конструкторы\n};\n\nstruct MyProduct : Product<Identifiable<MyProduct>, Nameable<MyProduct>, Pricable<MyProduct>>, \n                   Serializable<MyProduct> {\n    using Base = Product<Identifiable<MyProduct>, Nameable<MyProduct>, Pricable<MyProduct>>;\n    \n    template<typename... Args>\n    MyProduct(Args&&... args) : Base(forward<Args>(args)...) {}\n    \n    string serialize() const override {\n        return \"MyProduct: \" + getName() + \" (ID: \" + to_string(getId()) + \"), Price: $\" + to_string(getPrice());\n    }\n};\n\nstruct BasicProduct : Product<Identifiable<BasicProduct>, Nameable<BasicProduct>> {\n    using Base = Product<Identifiable<BasicProduct>, Nameable<BasicProduct>>;\n    using Base::Base;\n};\n\n// Продукт с дополнительным миксином\nstruct DetailedProduct : Product<Identifiable<DetailedProduct>, \n                                 Nameable<DetailedProduct>, \n                                 Pricable<DetailedProduct>,\n                                 Describable<DetailedProduct>> {\n    using Base = Product<Identifiable<DetailedProduct>, \n                        Nameable<DetailedProduct>,\n                        Pricable<DetailedProduct>,\n                        Describable<DetailedProduct>>;\n    using Base::Base;\n};\n\n// Фабрика для создания продуктов\ntemplate<typename ProductType, typename... Args>\nunique_ptr<ProductType> makeProduct(Args&&... args) {\n    return make_unique<ProductType>(forward<Args>(args)...);\n}\n\n// Классы, объявленные вне функции main\nstruct MinimalProduct : Product<Identifiable<MinimalProduct>> {\n    using Base = Product<Identifiable<MinimalProduct>>;\n    using Base::Base;\n};\n\nstruct FullFeaturedProduct : Product<Identifiable<FullFeaturedProduct>,\n                                     Nameable<FullFeaturedProduct>,\n                                     Pricable<FullFeaturedProduct>,\n                                     Describable<FullFeaturedProduct>>,\n                            Serializable<FullFeaturedProduct> {\n    using Base = Product<Identifiable<FullFeaturedProduct>,\n                        Nameable<FullFeaturedProduct>,\n                        Pricable<FullFeaturedProduct>,\n                        Describable<FullFeaturedProduct>>;\n    \n    FullFeaturedProduct(const string& name, double price, const string& desc) \n        : Base(name, price, desc) {}\n    \n    string serialize() const override {\n        return \"Full product: \" + getName() + \", $\" + to_string(getPrice()) + \", \" + getDescription();\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    cout << \"=== Пример 1: Простой продукт с тремя миксинами ===\" << endl;\n    SimpleProduct laptop(\"Laptop\", 999.99);\n    laptop.printAll();\n    cout << \"Serialization check: \" << laptop.serializeIfAvailable() << endl;\n    \n    cout << \"\\n=== Пример 2: Клонирование продукта ===\" << endl;\n    auto laptopClone = laptop.clone();\n    cout << \"Cloned product:\" << endl;\n    laptopClone->printAll();\n    \n    cout << \"\\n=== Пример 3: Продукт с сериализацией ===\" << endl;\n    MyProduct smartphone(\"Smartphone\", 799.99);\n    smartphone.printAll();\n    cout << \"Serialized: \" << smartphone.serialize() << endl;\n    \n    cout << \"\\n=== Пример 4: Базовый продукт без цены ===\" << endl;\n    BasicProduct book(\"Book\");\n    book.printAll();\n    cout << \"Price if available: $\" << book.getPriceIfAvailable() << endl;\n    \n    cout << \"\\n=== Пример 5: Фабричное создание продуктов ===\" << endl;\n    auto tablet = makeProduct<SimpleProduct>(\"Tablet\", 499.99);\n    auto monitor = makeProduct<SimpleProduct>(\"Monitor\", 299.99);\n    auto headphones = makeProduct<MyProduct>(\"Headphones\", 199.99);\n    \n    cout << \"\\nTablet:\" << endl;\n    tablet->printAll();\n    \n    cout << \"\\nMonitor:\" << endl;\n    monitor->printAll();\n    \n    cout << \"\\nHeadphones:\" << endl;\n    headphones->printAll();\n    cout << \"Headphones serialized: \" << headphones->serialize() << endl;\n    \n    cout << \"\\n=== Пример 6: Гетерогенная коллекция ===\" << endl;\n    vector<unique_ptr<ProductBase>> products;\n    products.push_back(move(tablet));\n    products.push_back(move(monitor));\n    products.push_back(move(headphones));\n    \n    for (size_t i = 0; i < products.size(); ++i) {\n        cout << \"\\nProduct \" << i + 1 << \" in collection:\" << endl;\n        \n        // Динамическое приведение типов\n        if (auto simple = dynamic_cast<SimpleProduct*>(products[i].get())) {\n            cout << \"Type: SimpleProduct\" << endl;\n            simple->printAll();\n        } else if (auto my = dynamic_cast<MyProduct*>(products[i].get())) {\n            cout << \"Type: MyProduct with serialization\" << endl;\n            my->printAll();\n            cout << \"Serialized: \" << my->serialize() << endl;\n        } else if (auto basic = dynamic_cast<BasicProduct*>(products[i].get())) {\n            cout << \"Type: BasicProduct\" << endl;\n            basic->printAll();\n        }\n    }\n    \n    cout << \"\\n=== Пример 7: Продукт с дополнительным миксином ===\" << endl;\n    DetailedProduct camera(\"Camera\", 599.99, \"High-quality digital camera\");\n    camera.printAll();\n    camera.printDescription();\n    \n    cout << \"\\n=== Пример 8: Создание собственного миксина ===\" << endl;\n    \n    // Создание продукта с минимальным набором миксинов\n    MinimalProduct minimal;\n    minimal.printAll();\n    cout << \"Minimal product ID: \" << minimal.getId() << endl;\n    \n    // Создание продукта с максимальным набором миксинов\n    FullFeaturedProduct fullProduct(\"Gaming PC\", 1999.99, \"High-end gaming computer\");\n    fullProduct.printAll();\n    fullProduct.printDescription();\n    cout << \"Serialized: \" << fullProduct.serialize() << endl;\n    \n    cout << \"\\n=== Преимущества системы миксинов ===\" << endl;\n    cout << \"1. Композиция вместо наследования\" << endl;\n    cout << \"2. Повторное использование кода\" << endl;\n    cout << \"3. Компиляция времени проверка типов\" << endl;\n    cout << \"4. Гибкость в комбинировании функциональности\" << endl;\n    cout << \"5. Отсутствие накладных расходов на виртуальные функции (кроме клонирования)\" << endl;\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <vector>\n#include <algorithm>\n#include <iterator>\n\nint main() {\n    std::vector<std::vector<int>> vectors = {{1, 4, 7}, {2, 5, 8}, {3, 6, 9}};\n    std::vector<int> result;\n    for (const auto& vec : vectors) {\n        std::vector<int> temp;\n        std::merge(result.begin(), result.end(), vec.begin(), vec.end(), std::back_inserter(temp));\n        result = std::move(temp);\n    }\n    std::cout << \"Объединенный отсортированный вектор: \";\n    for (int x : result) std::cout << x << \" \";\n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <cstring>\n#include <cstdint>\n\nunion BufferReader {\n    char buffer[16];\n    \n    struct {\n        uint32_t magic_number;\n        uint16_t version;\n        uint16_t flags;\n        uint64_t timestamp;\n    } header;\n    \n    struct {\n        float x, y, z;\n        float w;\n    } quaternion;\n    \n    struct {\n        uint8_t r, g, b, a;\n        uint8_t pixels[12];\n    } pixel_data;\n};\n\nint main() {\n    BufferReader reader;\n    std::memset(reader.buffer, 0, sizeof(reader.buffer));\n    \n    reader.header.magic_number = 0xDEADBEEF;\n    reader.header.version = 0x0102;\n    reader.header.flags = 0x000F;\n    reader.header.timestamp = 0x123456789ABCDEF0;\n    \n    std::cout << \"Чтение как заголовок:\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"Magic: 0x\" << std::hex << reader.header.magic_number << std::dec << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"Version: 0x\" << std::hex << reader.header.version << std::dec << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"Timestamp: 0x\" << std::hex << reader.header.timestamp << std::dec << std::endl;\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\nПереинтерпретация как quaternion:\" << std::endl;\n    reader.quaternion.x = 1.0f;\n    reader.quaternion.y = 0.5f;\n    reader.quaternion.z = 0.3f;\n    reader.quaternion.w = 0.8f;\n    \n    std::cout << \"Quaternion: [\" << reader.quaternion.x << \", \" \n              << reader.quaternion.y << \", \" << reader.quaternion.z \n              << \", \" << reader.quaternion.w << \"]\" << std::endl;\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\nЗаголовок после изменения (испорчен):\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"Magic теперь: 0x\" << std::hex << reader.header.magic_number << std::dec << std::endl;\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <vector>\n#include <algorithm>\n\nint main() {\n    std::vector<int> vec = {10, 20, 30, 40, 50};\n    int target = 30;\n    auto it = std::find(vec.begin(), vec.end(), target);\n    if (it != vec.end()) {\n        std::cout << \"Элемент \" << target << \" найден на позиции \" << std::distance(vec.begin(), it) << std::endl;\n    } else {\n        std::cout << \"Элемент не найден\" << std::endl;\n    }\n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n\nclass Base {\nprotected:\n    int val;\npublic:\n    Base(int v = 0) : val(v) {}\n    operator int() const { return val; }\n};\n\nclass Derived : public Base {\npublic:\n    Derived(int v = 0) : Base(v) {}\n    operator double() const { return val * 1.5; }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    Derived d(10);\n    int i = d;\n    double f = d;\n    std::cout << \"int: \" << i << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"double: \" << f << std::endl;\n    return 0;\n}

#include <sys/types.h>\n#include <sys/socket.h>\n#include <netinet/in.h>\n#include <netinet/ip_icmp.h>\n#include <arpa/inet.h>\n#include <unistd.h>\n#include <iostream>\n#include <cstring>\nusing namespace std;\nunsigned short checksum(void* b, int len) {\n    unsigned short* buf = (unsigned short*)b;\n    unsigned int sum = 0;\n    for(; len > 1; len -= 2) sum += *buf++;\n    if(len == 1) sum += *(unsigned char*)buf;\n    sum = (sum >> 16) + (sum & 0xFFFF);\n    sum += (sum >> 16);\n    return ~sum;\n}\nint main() {\n    int sock = socket(AF_INET, SOCK_RAW, IPPROTO_ICMP);\n    sockaddr_in addr;\n    addr.sin_family = AF_INET;\n    inet_pton(AF_INET, \"8.8.8.8\", &addr.sin_addr);\n    struct icmphdr icmp;\n    memset(&icmp, 0, sizeof(icmp));\n    icmp.type = ICMP_ECHO;\n    icmp.code = 0;\n    icmp.un.echo.id = getpid();\n    icmp.un.echo.sequence = 1;\n    icmp.checksum = checksum(&icmp, sizeof(icmp));\n    sendto(sock, &icmp, sizeof(icmp), 0, (struct sockaddr*)&addr, sizeof(addr));\n    cout << \"ICMP echo request sent to 8.8.8.8\" << endl;\n    close(sock);\n    return 0;\n}
