#include <iostream>\n#include <string>\n#include <memory>\nusing namespace std;\n\n// Интерфейс\nclass Image {\npublic:\n    virtual void display() = 0;\n    virtual ~Image() {}\n};\n\n// Реальный объект\nclass RealImage : public Image {\n    string filename;\n    void loadFromDisk() {\n        cout << \"Loading image from disk: \" << filename << \" (expensive operation)\" << endl;\n    }\npublic:\n    RealImage(const string& file) : filename(file) {\n        loadFromDisk();\n    }\n    void display() override {\n        cout << \"Displaying image: \" << filename << endl;\n    }\n};\n\n// Заместитель\nclass ProxyImage : public Image {\n    unique_ptr<RealImage> realImage;\n    string filename;\npublic:\n    ProxyImage(const string& file) : filename(file) {}\n    void display() override {\n        if(!realImage) {\n            cout << \"Proxy: Creating real image on demand\" << endl;\n            realImage = make_unique<RealImage>(filename);\n        }\n        realImage->display();\n    }\n    void reset() {\n        realImage.reset();\n        cout << \"Proxy: Image cache cleared\" << endl;\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    cout << \"=== Using Proxy Pattern ===\" << endl;\n    ProxyImage image(\"photo.jpg\");\n    // Первый вызов - создание реального объекта\n    cout << \"\\nFirst display call:\" << endl;\n    image.display();\n    // Второй вызов - использование уже созданного объекта\n    cout << \"\\nSecond display call:\" << endl;\n    image.display();\n    // Сброс кэша\n    cout << \"\\nResetting proxy:\" << endl;\n    image.reset();\n    // Снова создание объекта\n    cout << \"\\nThird display call:\" << endl;\n    image.display();\n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <vector>\n#include <string>\n#include <algorithm>\n#include <ctime>\n#include <iomanip>\n#include <map>\n#include <set>\n#include <memory>\n#include <sstream>\nusing namespace std;\n\nclass Date {\nprivate:\n    int year, month, day;\npublic:\n    Date(int y = 2024, int m = 1, int d = 1) : year(y), month(m), day(d) {}\n    \n    static Date today() {\n        time_t now = time(0);\n        tm* ltm = localtime(&now);\n        return Date(1900 + ltm->tm_year, 1 + ltm->tm_mon, ltm->tm_mday);\n    }\n    \n    bool operator<(const Date& other) const {\n        if(year != other.year) return year < other.year;\n        if(month != other.month) return month < other.month;\n        return day < other.day;\n    }\n    \n    bool operator<=(const Date& other) const {\n        return *this < other || (year == other.year && month == other.month && day == other.day);\n    }\n    \n    bool operator>(const Date& other) const {\n        return other < *this;\n    }\n    \n    bool operator>=(const Date& other) const {\n        return other <= *this;\n    }\n    \n    int days_between(const Date& other) const {\n        return (other.year - year) * 365 + (other.month - month) * 30 + (other.day - day);\n    }\n    \n    Date add_days(int days) const {\n        Date result = *this;\n        result.day += days;\n        while(result.day > 30) {\n            result.day -= 30;\n            result.month++;\n        }\n        while(result.month > 12) {\n            result.month -= 12;\n            result.year++;\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n    \n    string str() const {\n        return to_string(year) + \"-\" + \n               (month < 10 ? \"0\" : \"\") + to_string(month) + \"-\" + \n               (day < 10 ? \"0\" : \"\") + to_string(day);\n    }\n};\n\nenum class TaskStatus { NOT_STARTED, IN_PROGRESS, COMPLETED, BLOCKED };\nenum class Priority { LOW, MEDIUM, HIGH, CRITICAL };\n\nclass Task {\nprivate:\n    static int next_id;\n    int id;\n    string name;\n    string description;\n    TaskStatus status;\n    Priority priority;\n    Date start_date;\n    Date end_date;\n    int duration_days;\n    double progress;\n    string assigned_to;\n    vector<int> dependencies;\n    vector<int> subtasks;\n    \npublic:\n    Task(const string& n, const string& desc, Priority pri, Date start, int duration) \n        : name(n), description(desc), status(TaskStatus::NOT_STARTED), priority(pri),\n          start_date(start), duration_days(duration), progress(0.0), assigned_to(\"\") {\n        id = next_id++;\n        end_date = start_date.add_days(duration_days);\n    }\n    \n    void update_progress(double new_progress) {\n        progress = max(0.0, min(100.0, new_progress));\n        if(progress == 0.0) {\n            status = TaskStatus::NOT_STARTED;\n        } else if(progress < 100.0) {\n            status = TaskStatus::IN_PROGRESS;\n        } else {\n            status = TaskStatus::COMPLETED;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    void add_dependency(int task_id) {\n        if(find(dependencies.begin(), dependencies.end(), task_id) == dependencies.end()) {\n            dependencies.push_back(task_id);\n        }\n    }\n    \n    void remove_dependency(int task_id) {\n        dependencies.erase(remove(dependencies.begin(), dependencies.end(), task_id), dependencies.end());\n    }\n    \n    void add_subtask(int task_id) {\n        if(find(subtasks.begin(), subtasks.end(), task_id) == subtasks.end()) {\n            subtasks.push_back(task_id);\n        }\n    }\n    \n    void remove_subtask(int task_id) {\n        subtasks.erase(remove(subtasks.begin(), subtasks.end(), task_id), subtasks.end());\n    }\n    \n    void assign_to(const string& person) {\n        assigned_to = person;\n    }\n    \n    bool can_start(const set<int>& completed_tasks) const {\n        for(int dep : dependencies) {\n            if(completed_tasks.find(dep) == completed_tasks.end()) {\n                return false;\n            }\n        }\n        return true;\n    }\n    \n    bool is_overdue(Date current_date) const {\n        return status != TaskStatus::COMPLETED && current_date > end_date;\n    }\n    \n    void display() const {\n        cout << left << setw(6) << id \n             << setw(25) << (name.length() > 24 ? name.substr(0, 21) + \"...\" : name)\n             << setw(15) << get_status_string() \n             << setw(12) << get_priority_string() \n             << setw(12) << start_date.str() \n             << setw(12) << end_date.str() \n             << setw(10) << duration_days \n             << setw(10) << fixed << setprecision(1) << progress << \"%\"\n             << setw(15) << (assigned_to.empty() ? \"Unassigned\" : assigned_to) \n             << setw(10) << dependencies.size() \n             << setw(10) << subtasks.size() << endl;\n    }\n    \n    string get_status_string() const {\n        switch(status) {\n            case TaskStatus::NOT_STARTED: return \"Not Started\";\n            case TaskStatus::IN_PROGRESS: return \"In Progress\";\n            case TaskStatus::COMPLETED: return \"Completed\";\n            case TaskStatus::BLOCKED: return \"Blocked\";\n            default: return \"Unknown\";\n        }\n    }\n    \n    string get_priority_string() const {\n        switch(priority) {\n            case Priority::LOW: return \"Low\";\n            case Priority::MEDIUM: return \"Medium\";\n            case Priority::HIGH: return \"High\";\n            case Priority::CRITICAL: return \"Critical\";\n            default: return \"Unknown\";\n        }\n    }\n    \n    int get_id() const { return id; }\n    string get_name() const { return name; }\n    TaskStatus get_status() const { return status; }\n    Priority get_priority() const { return priority; }\n    Date get_start_date() const { return start_date; }\n    Date get_end_date() const { return end_date; }\n    int get_duration() const { return duration_days; }\n    double get_progress() const { return progress; }\n    string get_assigned_to() const { return assigned_to; }\n    vector<int> get_dependencies() const { return dependencies; }\n    vector<int> get_subtasks() const { return subtasks; }\n    \n    void set_status(TaskStatus new_status) { status = new_status; }\n    void set_dates(Date start, Date end) { \n        start_date = start; \n        end_date = end;\n        duration_days = start_date.days_between(end_date);\n    }\n};\n\nint Task::next_id = 1;\n\nclass Project {\nprivate:\n    string name;\n    string description;\n    Date start_date;\n    Date end_date;\n    map<int, unique_ptr<Task>> tasks;\n    vector<int> task_order;\n    \n    vector<int> topological_sort() {\n        map<int, vector<int>> graph;\n        map<int, int> in_degree;\n        \n        for(const auto& [id, task] : tasks) {\n            graph[id] = task->get_dependencies();\n            in_degree[id] = 0;\n        }\n        \n        for(const auto& [id, deps] : graph) {\n            for(int dep : deps) {\n                in_degree[id]++;\n            }\n        }\n        \n        vector<int> result;\n        vector<int> queue;\n        \n        for(const auto& [id, degree] : in_degree) {\n            if(degree == 0) {\n                queue.push_back(id);\n            }\n        }\n        \n        while(!queue.empty()) {\n            int current = queue.back();\n            queue.pop_back();\n            result.push_back(current);\n            \n            for(const auto& [id, deps] : graph) {\n                if(find(deps.begin(), deps.end(), current) != deps.end()) {\n                    in_degree[id]--;\n                    if(in_degree[id] == 0) {\n                        queue.push_back(id);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        \n        return result;\n    }\n    \npublic:\n    Project(const string& n, const string& desc, Date start) \n        : name(n), description(desc), start_date(start) {\n        end_date = start;\n    }\n    \n    Task* add_task(const string& task_name, const string& desc, Priority pri, \n                   Date start, int duration) {\n        auto task = make_unique<Task>(task_name, desc, pri, start, duration);\n        Task* task_ptr = task.get();\n        tasks[task->get_id()] = move(task);\n        \n        if(task_ptr->get_end_date() > end_date) {\n            end_date = task_ptr->get_end_date();\n        }\n        \n        task_order = topological_sort();\n        return task_ptr;\n    }\n    \n    bool remove_task(int task_id) {\n        if(tasks.find(task_id) == tasks.end()) {\n            return false;\n        }\n        \n        for(auto& [id, task] : tasks) {\n            task->remove_dependency(task_id);\n            task->remove_subtask(task_id);\n        }\n        \n        tasks.erase(task_id);\n        task_order = topological_sort();\n        return true;\n    }\n    \n    Task* get_task(int task_id) {\n        auto it = tasks.find(task_id);\n        return it != tasks.end() ? it->second.get() : nullptr;\n    }\n    \n    void add_dependency(int task_id, int dependency_id) {\n        Task* task = get_task(task_id);\n        Task* dependency = get_task(dependency_id);\n        \n        if(task && dependency) {\n            task->add_dependency(dependency_id);\n            task_order = topological_sort();\n        }\n    }\n    \n    void remove_dependency(int task_id, int dependency_id) {\n        Task* task = get_task(task_id);\n        if(task) {\n            task->remove_dependency(dependency_id);\n            task_order = topological_sort();\n        }\n    }\n    \n    void display_gantt_chart(Date view_start, Date view_end) {\n        cout << \"\\n=== Gantt Chart: \" << name << \" ===\" << endl;\n        cout << \"Period: \" << view_start.str() << \" to \" << view_end.str() << endl;\n        cout << endl;\n        \n        int total_days = view_start.days_between(view_end);\n        if(total_days <= 0) total_days = 1;\n        \n        cout << left << setw(30) << \"Task\";\n        for(int i = 0; i <= min(total_days, 60); i += 5) {\n            cout << setw(5) << i;\n        }\n        cout << endl;\n        \n        cout << string(30 + min(total_days, 60) * 5, '-') << endl;\n        \n        for(int task_id : task_order) {\n            Task* task = get_task(task_id);\n            if(!task) continue;\n            \n            Date task_start = task->get_start_date();\n            Date task_end = task->get_end_date();\n            \n            if(task_end < view_start || task_start > view_end) continue;\n            \n            int start_offset = max(0, view_start.days_between(task_start));\n            int task_length = task->get_duration();\n            \n            string display_name = task->get_name();\n            if(display_name.length() > 28) {\n                display_name = display_name.substr(0, 25) + \"...\";\n            }\n            \n            cout << left << setw(30) << display_name;\n            \n            for(int i = 0; i <= min(total_days, 60); i++) {\n                if(i % 5 == 0) {\n                    if(i >= start_offset && i < start_offset + task_length) {\n                        char symbol = ' ';\n                        switch(task->get_status()) {\n                            case TaskStatus::NOT_STARTED: symbol = '-'; break;\n                            case TaskStatus::IN_PROGRESS: symbol = '='; break;\n                            case TaskStatus::COMPLETED: symbol = '#'; break;\n                            case TaskStatus::BLOCKED: symbol = 'X'; break;\n                        }\n                        cout << symbol;\n                    } else {\n                        cout << ' ';\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n            cout << endl;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    void display_critical_path() {\n        cout << \"\\n=== Critical Path ===\" << endl;\n        \n        if(task_order.empty()) {\n            cout << \"No tasks in project\" << endl;\n            return;\n        }\n        \n        map<int, Date> earliest_start;\n        map<int, Date> latest_start;\n        \n        for(int task_id : task_order) {\n            Task* task = get_task(task_id);\n            if(!task) continue;\n            \n            Date earliest = task->get_start_date();\n            for(int dep_id : task->get_dependencies()) {\n                Task* dep = get_task(dep_id);\n                if(dep) {\n                    Date dep_end = earliest_start[dep_id].add_days(dep->get_duration());\n                    if(dep_end > earliest) {\n                        earliest = dep_end;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n            earliest_start[task_id] = earliest;\n        }\n        \n        Date project_end = end_date;\n        for(auto it = task_order.rbegin(); it != task_order.rend(); ++it) {\n            int task_id = *it;\n            Task* task = get_task(task_id);\n            if(!task) continue;\n            \n            Date latest = project_end;\n            for(auto& [other_id, other_task] : tasks) {\n                vector<int> deps = other_task->get_dependencies();\n                if(find(deps.begin(), deps.end(), task_id) != deps.end()) {\n                    Date other_latest = latest_start[other_id];\n                    Date task_latest = other_latest.add_days(-task->get_duration());\n                    if(task_latest < latest) {\n                        latest = task_latest;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n            latest_start[task_id] = latest;\n        }\n        \n        cout << \"Critical Tasks:\" << endl;\n        for(int task_id : task_order) {\n            Date earliest = earliest_start[task_id];\n            Date latest = latest_start[task_id];\n            \n            if(earliest.days_between(latest) == 0) {\n                Task* task = get_task(task_id);\n                if(task) {\n                    cout << \"  \" << task->get_name() << \" (ID: \" << task_id << \")\" << endl;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    void display_project_summary() const {\n        cout << \"\\n=== Project Summary: \" << name << \" ===\" << endl;\n        cout << \"Description: \" << description << endl;\n        cout << \"Start Date: \" << start_date.str() << endl;\n        cout << \"End Date: \" << end_date.str() << endl;\n        cout << \"Duration: \" << start_date.days_between(end_date) << \" days\" << endl;\n        cout << \"Total Tasks: \" << tasks.size() << endl;\n        \n        int completed = 0, in_progress = 0, not_started = 0, blocked = 0;\n        double total_progress = 0.0;\n        \n        for(const auto& [id, task] : tasks) {\n            total_progress += task->get_progress();\n            switch(task->get_status()) {\n                case TaskStatus::COMPLETED: completed++; break;\n                case TaskStatus::IN_PROGRESS: in_progress++; break;\n                case TaskStatus::NOT_STARTED: not_started++; break;\n                case TaskStatus::BLOCKED: blocked++; break;\n            }\n        }\n        \n        cout << \"\\nTask Status:\" << endl;\n        cout << \"  Completed: \" << completed << endl;\n        cout << \"  In Progress: \" << in_progress << endl;\n        cout << \"  Not Started: \" << not_started << endl;\n        cout << \"  Blocked: \" << blocked << endl;\n        \n        cout << \"\\nOverall Progress: \" << fixed << setprecision(1) \n             << (tasks.empty() ? 0.0 : total_progress / tasks.size()) << \"%\" << endl;\n        \n        Date today = Date::today();\n        int overdue = 0;\n        for(const auto& [id, task] : tasks) {\n            if(task->is_overdue(today)) {\n                overdue++;\n            }\n        }\n        cout << \"Overdue Tasks: \" << overdue << endl;\n    }\n    \n    void display_all_tasks() const {\n        cout << \"\\n=== All Tasks ===\" << endl;\n        cout << left << setw(6) << \"ID\" \n             << setw(25) << \"Name\" \n             << setw(15) << \"Status\" \n             << setw(12) << \"Priority\" \n             << setw(12) << \"Start\" \n             << setw(12) << \"End\" \n             << setw(10) << \"Duration\" \n             << setw(10) << \"Progress\" \n             << setw(15) << \"Assigned To\" \n             << setw(10) << \"Deps\" \n             << setw(10) << \"Subtasks\" << endl;\n        cout << string(138, '-') << endl;\n        \n        for(const auto& [id, task] : tasks) {\n            task->display();\n        }\n    }\n    \n    vector<Task*> get_tasks_by_status(TaskStatus status) {\n        vector<Task*> result;\n        for(auto& [id, task] : tasks) {\n            if(task->get_status() == status) {\n                result.push_back(task.get());\n            }\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n    \n    vector<Task*> get_overdue_tasks(Date current_date) {\n        vector<Task*> result;\n        for(auto& [id, task] : tasks) {\n            if(task->is_overdue(current_date)) {\n                result.push_back(task.get());\n            }\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n    \n    double calculate_project_progress() const {\n        if(tasks.empty()) return 0.0;\n        double total = 0.0;\n        for(const auto& [id, task] : tasks) {\n            total += task->get_progress();\n        }\n        return total / tasks.size();\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    cout << \"=== Project Management System ===\" << endl;\n    \n    Project project(\"Website Redesign\", \"Complete redesign of company website\", #include <iostream>\n#include <functional>\nusing namespace std;\n\nclass Data {\npublic:\n    int value;\n    string name;\n    \n    Data(int v, const string& n) : value(v), name(n) {}\n    \n    void print() const {\n        cout << name << \": \" << value << endl;\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    Data data(42, \"Пример\");\n    \n    // Ссылки на члены класса\n    int& valueRef = data.value;\n    string& nameRef = data.name;\n    \n    // Модификация через ссылки\n    valueRef = 100;\n    nameRef = \"Измененный пример\";\n    \n    data.print();\n    \n    // Ссылка на константный член через константный объект\n    const Data constData(200, \"Константа\");\n    const int& constValueRef = constData.value;\n    // constValueRef = 300; // Ошибка: константная ссылка на константный член\n    \n    cout << \"constData.value = \" << constValueRef << endl;\n    \n    // Использование reference_wrapper\n    reference_wrapper<int> valueWrapper = data.value;\n    valueWrapper.get() = 500; // Модификация через reference_wrapper\n    \n    cout << \"После reference_wrapper: \";\n    data.print();\n    \n    // Массив ссылок на члены разных объектов (невозможно напрямую)\n    // Но можно использовать указатели на члены\n    int Data::*valuePtr = &Data::value;\n    data.*valuePtr = 600;\n    \n    cout << \"После указателя на член: \";\n    data.print();\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <cmath>\n#include <vector>\n#include <algorithm>\n\nint main() {\n    std::cout << \"Анализ системы нелинейных уравнений\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"1. Система двух уравнений второй степени\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"2. Система трех уравнений\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"3. Смешанная система\" << std::endl;\n    \n    int choice;\n    std::cin >> choice;\n    \n    switch(choice) {\n        case 1: {\n            double a1, b1, c1, d1, e1, f1;\n            double a2, b2, c2, d2, e2, f2;\n            \n            std::cout << \"Введите коэффициенты первого уравнения (a1 x^2 + b1 y^2 + c1 xy + d1 x + e1 y + f1 = 0):\" << std::endl;\n            std::cin >> a1 >> b1 >> c1 >> d1 >> e1 >> f1;\n            std::cout << \"Введите коэффициенты второго уравнения (a2 x^2 + b2 y^2 + c2 xy + d2 x + e2 y + f2 = 0):\" << std::endl;\n            std::cin >> a2 >> b2 >> c2 >> d2 >> e2 >> f2;\n            \n            std::cout << \"\\nАнализ системы:\" << std::endl;\n            std::cout << \"1. В общем случае система двух уравнений второй степени имеет до 4 решений\" << std::endl;\n            std::cout << \"2. Решения могут быть действительными или комплексными\" << std::endl;\n            std::cout << \"3. Возможны случаи бесконечного множества решений (вырожденные случаи)\" << std::endl;\n            \n            double det = a1*b2 - a2*b1;\n            double det_linear = d1*e2 - d2*e1;\n            \n            if(std::fabs(det) < 1e-9 && std::fabs(det_linear) < 1e-9) {\n                std::cout << \"4. Система может быть вырожденной (бесконечно много решений или нет решений)\" << std::endl;\n            }\n            \n            std::cout << \"\\nМетоды решения:\" << std::endl;\n            std::cout << \"1. Метод подстановки\" << std::endl;\n            std::cout << \"2. Метод исключения\" << std::endl;\n            std::cout << \"3. Метод графического анализа\" << std::endl;\n            std::cout << \"4. Численные методы (метод Ньютона)\" << std::endl;\n            \n            std::cout << \"\\nГеометрическая интерпретация:\" << std::endl;\n            if(std::fabs(a1) < 1e-9 && std::fabs(b1) < 1e-9 && std::fabs(c1) < 1e-9) {\n                std::cout << \"Первое уравнение - прямая линия\" << std::endl;\n            } else {\n                std::cout << \"Первое уравнение - кривая второго порядка\" << std::endl;\n            }\n            if(std::fabs(a2) < 1e-9 && std::fabs(b2) < 1e-9 && std::fabs(c2) < 1e-9) {\n                std::cout << \"Второе уравнение - прямая линия\" << std::endl;\n            } else {\n                std::cout << \"Второе уравнение - кривая второго порядка\" << std::endl;\n            }\n            break;\n        }\n        case 2: {\n            std::cout << \"\\nСистема трех уравнений (общий случай):\" << std::endl;\n            std::cout << \"1. Может иметь от 0 до 8 решений (теорема Безу)\" << std::endl;\n            std::cout << \"2. Решения могут быть изолированными точками\" << std::endl;\n            std::cout << \"3. Возможны кривые решений (бесконечное множество)\" << std::endl;\n            std::cout << \"\\nМетоды решения:\" << std::endl;\n            std::cout << \"1. Метод исключения Гаусса для полиномиальных систем\" << std::endl;\n            std::cout << \"2. Метод базисов Грёбнера\" << std::endl;\n            std::cout << \"3. Численные методы (метод Ньютона для систем)\" << std::endl;\n            std::cout << \"4. Метод гомотопий\" << std::endl;\n            break;\n        }\n        case 3: {\n            std::cout << \"\\nСмешанная система (разные степени):\" << std::endl;\n            std::cout << \"1. Количество решений зависит от старшей степени\" << std::endl;\n            std::cout << \"2. Может быть исследована методами алгебраической геометрии\" << std::endl;\n            std::cout << \"3. Часто требуются численные методы\" << std::endl;\n            std::cout << \"\\nПример: система x^2 + y^2 = 1 и x + y = 1\" << std::endl;\n            std::cout << \"Эта система имеет 2 решения\" << std::endl;\n            break;\n        }\n        default:\n            std::cout << \"Неверный выбор\" << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\nОбщие рекомендации:\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"1. Для точного анализа используйте компьютерные алгебраические системы\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"2. Численные методы дают приближенные решения\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"3. Графический анализ помогает понять геометрию\" << std::endl;\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <string>\n#include <vector>\n#include <cctype>\n#include <algorithm>\nusing namespace std;\n\nstring formatPhoneNumber(const string& input) {\n    // Извлекаем только цифры\n    string digits;\n    for(char c : input) {\n        if(isdigit(c)) {\n            digits.push_back(c);\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // Проверяем длину номера\n    if(digits.length() != 10) {\n        if(digits.length() == 11 && digits[0] == '1') {\n            digits = digits.substr(1); // Убираем лидирующую 1\n        } else {\n            return \"Invalid phone number\";\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // Форматируем номер\n    return \"(\" + digits.substr(0, 3) + \") \" + \n           digits.substr(3, 3) + \"-\" + \n           digits.substr(6, 4);\n}\n\nvector<string> extractPhoneNumbers(const string& text) {\n    vector<string> phone_numbers;\n    string current_number;\n    \n    for(size_t i = 0; i < text.length(); i++) {\n        if(isdigit(text[i])) {\n            current_number.push_back(text[i]);\n            \n            // Если накопили 10-11 цифр, пытаемся форматировать\n            if(current_number.length() >= 10) {\n                string formatted = formatPhoneNumber(current_number);\n                if(formatted != \"Invalid phone number\") {\n                    phone_numbers.push_back(formatted);\n                    current_number.clear();\n                } else if(current_number.length() > 11) {\n                    // Если слишком длинное число, начинаем заново\n                    current_number.clear();\n                }\n            }\n        } else if(!current_number.empty() && current_number.length() < 10) {\n            // Сбрасываем если встретили не-цифру до набора 10 цифр\n            current_number.clear();\n        }\n    }\n    \n    return phone_numbers;\n}\n\nstring normalizePhoneNumber(const string& phone) {\n    string normalized;\n    \n    // Убираем все не-цифры\n    for(char c : phone) {\n        if(isdigit(c)) {\n            normalized.push_back(c);\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // Добавляем код страны если нужно\n    if(normalized.length() == 10) {\n        normalized = \"1\" + normalized;\n    }\n    \n    return normalized;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    vector<string> test_cases = {\n        \"1234567890\",\n        \"(123)456-7890\",\n        \"123-456-7890\",\n        \"1-123-456-7890\",\n        \"+1 (123) 456-7890\",\n        \"abc1234567890xyz\",\n        \"12345\",\n        \"123456789012\",\n        \"Call me at 1234567890 or 9876543210\",\n        \"Phone: 1-800-555-1234\"\n    };\n    \n    cout << \"Phone Number Formatting:\\n\";\n    for(const string& test : test_cases) {\n        string formatted = formatPhoneNumber(test);\n        cout << \"Input: \\\"\" << test << \"\\\"\" << endl;\n        cout << \"Formatted: \" << formatted << endl;\n        \n        string normalized = normalizePhoneNumber(test);\n        cout << \"Normalized: \" << normalized << endl;\n        cout << endl;\n    }\n    \n    // Тест извлечения номеров из текста\n    string text = \"Contact us at 1234567890 or (987)654-3210. Also try 1-800-555-1234.\";\n    cout << \"\\nExtracting phone numbers from text:\\n\";\n    cout << \"Text: \\\"\" << text << \"\\\"\" << endl;\n    \n    vector<string> extracted = extractPhoneNumbers(text);\n    cout << \"Extracted numbers: \";\n    for(const string& num : extracted) {\n        cout << num << \" \";\n    }\n    cout << endl;\n    \n    // Валидация номеров\n    cout << \"\\nPhone Number Validation:\\n\";\n    vector<string> validation_tests = {\n        \"(123) 456-7890\",\n        \"123-456-7890\",\n        \"123.456.7890\",\n        \"+1 123 456 7890\",\n        \"12345\",\n        \"123456789012345\"\n    };\n    \n    for(const string& test : validation_tests) {\n        string formatted = formatPhoneNumber(test);\n        bool valid = (formatted != \"Invalid phone number\");\n        cout << \"Number: \\\"\" << test << \"\\\" is \" \n             << (valid ? \"VALID\" : \"INVALID\");\n        if(valid) {\n            cout << \" -> \" << formatted;\n        }\n        cout << endl;\n    }\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <vector>\n#include <cmath>\n#include <type_traits>\n#include <stdexcept>\nusing namespace std;\n\n// Type traits для числовых типов\ntemplate<typename T>\nstruct is_arithmetic_type {\n    static constexpr bool value = false;\n};\n\ntemplate<>\nstruct is_arithmetic_type<int> {\n    static constexpr bool value = true;\n};\n\ntemplate<>\nstruct is_arithmetic_type<float> {\n    static constexpr bool value = true;\n};\n\ntemplate<>\nstruct is_arithmetic_type<double> {\n    static constexpr bool value = true;\n};\n\ntemplate<>\nstruct is_arithmetic_type<long double> {\n    static constexpr bool value = true;\n};\n\n// SFINAE для проверки интерфейса матрицы\ntemplate<typename Container, typename = void>\nstruct is_matrix_like : false_type {};\n\ntemplate<typename Container>\nstruct is_matrix_like<Container, void_t<\n    decltype(declval<Container>().rows()),\n    decltype(declval<Container>().cols()),\n    decltype(declval<Container>()(0, 0))\n>> : true_type {};\n\n// Шаблонный класс матрицы\ntemplate<typename T>\nclass Matrix {\n    static_assert(is_arithmetic_type<T>::value, \"Matrix requires arithmetic type\");\n    \n    vector<vector<T>> data;\n    size_t rows_, cols_;\n    \npublic:\n    using value_type = T;\n    \n    Matrix(size_t rows, size_t cols) : rows_(rows), cols_(cols) {\n        data.resize(rows, vector<T>(cols, T{}));\n    }\n    \n    Matrix(size_t rows, size_t cols, T init_value) : rows_(rows), cols_(cols) {\n        data.resize(rows, vector<T>(cols, init_value));\n    }\n    \n    size_t rows() const { return rows_; }\n    size_t cols() const { return cols_; }\n    \n    T& operator()(size_t i, size_t j) {\n        return data[i][j];\n    }\n    \n    const T& operator()(size_t i, size_t j) const {\n        return data[i][j];\n    }\n    \n    // Сложение матриц (только для совместимых размеров)\n    template<typename Other>\n    typename enable_if<is_matrix_like<Other>::value && \n                       is_same<typename Other::value_type, T>::value, \n                       Matrix<T>>::type\n    operator+(const Other& other) const {\n        if (rows() != other.rows() || cols() != other.cols()) {\n            throw runtime_error(\"Matrix dimensions don't match\");\n        }\n        \n        Matrix result(rows(), cols());\n        for (size_t i = 0; i < rows(); i++) {\n            for (size_t j = 0; j < cols(); j++) {\n                result(i, j) = (*this)(i, j) + other(i, j);\n            }\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n    \n    // Умножение на скаляр\n    Matrix operator*(T scalar) const {\n        Matrix result(rows(), cols());\n        for (size_t i = 0; i < rows(); i++) {\n            for (size_t j = 0; j < cols(); j++) {\n                result(i, j) = (*this)(i, j) * scalar;\n            }\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n    \n    void print() const {\n        for (size_t i = 0; i < rows(); i++) {\n            for (size_t j = 0; j < cols(); j++) {\n                cout << (*this)(i, j) << \"\\t\";\n            }\n            cout << endl;\n        }\n    }\n};\n\n// Специализированная функция для числовых матриц\ntemplate<typename Mat>\ntypename enable_if<is_matrix_like<Mat>::value && \n                   is_arithmetic_type<typename Mat::value_type>::value, \n                   typename Mat::value_type>::type\ndeterminant2x2(const Mat& mat) {\n    if (mat.rows() != 2 || mat.cols() != 2) {\n        throw runtime_error(\"Determinant only for 2x2 matrices\");\n    }\n    return mat(0, 0) * mat(1, 1) - mat(0, 1) * mat(1, 0);\n}\n\nint main() {\n    Matrix<double> m1(2, 2, 1.0);\n    m1(0, 1) = 2.0;\n    m1(1, 0) = 3.0;\n    m1(1, 1) = 4.0;\n    \n    Matrix<double> m2(2, 2, 2.0);\n    \n    cout << \"Matrix 1:\" << endl;\n    m1.print();\n    \n    cout << \"\\nMatrix 2:\" << endl;\n    m2.print();\n    \n    cout << \"\\nMatrix 1 + Matrix 2:\" << endl;\n    auto m3 = m1 + m2;\n    m3.print();\n    \n    cout << \"\\nMatrix 1 * 2.5:\" << endl;\n    auto m4 = m1 * 2.5;\n    m4.print();\n    \n    cout << \"\\nDeterminant of Matrix 1: \" << determinant2x2(m1) << endl;\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\nusing namespace std;\n\nstruct Vector2D {\n    double x, y;\n    \n    Vector2D opposite() const {\n        Vector2D result;\n        result.x = -x;\n        result.y = -y;\n        return result;\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    Vector2D v = {3.0, -4.0};\n    Vector2D opp = v.opposite();\n    \n    cout << \"Противоположный вектор: (\" << opp.x << \", \" << opp.y << \")\" << endl;\n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <string>\n#include <vector>\n#include <iomanip>\n#include <sstream>\n#include <cstdint>\n#include <bitset>\nusing namespace std;\n\n// Упрощенная версия SHA-256 для демонстрации\nclass SimpleSHA256 {\nprivate:\n    static const uint32_t K[64];\n    \n    static uint32_t rotr(uint32_t x, int n) {\n        return (x >> n) | (x << (32 - n));\n    }\n    \n    static uint32_t ch(uint32_t x, uint32_t y, uint32_t z) {\n        return (x & y) ^ (~x & z);\n    }\n    \n    static uint32_t maj(uint32_t x, uint32_t y, uint32_t z) {\n        return (x & y) ^ (x & z) ^ (y & z);\n    }\n    \n    static uint32_t sigma0(uint32_t x) {\n        return rotr(x, 2) ^ rotr(x, 13) ^ rotr(x, 22);\n    }\n    \n    static uint32_t sigma1(uint32_t x) {\n        return rotr(x, 6) ^ rotr(x, 11) ^ rotr(x, 25);\n    }\n    \n    static uint32_t gamma0(uint32_t x) {\n        return rotr(x, 7) ^ rotr(x, 18) ^ (x >> 3);\n    }\n    \n    static uint32_t gamma1(uint32_t x) {\n        return rotr(x, 17) ^ rotr(x, 19) ^ (x >> 10);\n    }\n    \npublic:\n    static string hash(const string& message) {\n        // Начальные значения\n        uint32_t H[8] = {\n            0x6a09e667, 0xbb67ae85, 0x3c6ef372, 0xa54ff53a,\n            0x510e527f, 0x9b05688c, 0x1f83d9ab, 0x5be0cd19\n        };\n        \n        // Преобразование сообщения в биты\n        uint64_t bit_length = message.length() * 8;\n        \n        // Добавление бита '1'\n        vector<uint8_t> padded(message.begin(), message.end());\n        padded.push_back(0x80);\n        \n        // Добавление нулей до длины 448 бит (по модулю 512)\n        while((padded.size() * 8) % 512 != 448) {\n            padded.push_back(0x00);\n        }\n        \n        // Добавление длины сообщения (64 бита)\n        for(int i = 7; i >= 0; i--) {\n            padded.push_back((bit_length >> (i * 8)) & 0xFF);\n        }\n        \n        // Обработка блоков\n        for(size_t chunk = 0; chunk < padded.size(); chunk += 64) {\n            uint32_t w[64] = {0};\n            \n            // Копирование данных в массив слов\n            for(int i = 0; i < 16; i++) {\n                w[i] = (padded[chunk + i*4] << 24) |\n                       (padded[chunk + i*4 + 1] << 16) |\n                       (padded[chunk + i*4 + 2] << 8) |\n                       (padded[chunk + i*4 + 3]);\n            }\n            \n            // Расширение сообщения\n            for(int i = 16; i < 64; i++) {\n                w[i] = gamma1(w[i-2]) + w[i-7] + gamma0(w[i-15]) + w[i-16];\n            }\n            \n            // Инициализация рабочих переменных\n            uint32_t a = H[0], b = H[1], c = H[2], d = H[3];\n            uint32_t e = H[4], f = H[5], g = H[6], h = H[7];\n            \n            // Основной цикл\n            for(int i = 0; i < 64; i++) {\n                uint32_t t1 = h + sigma1(e) + ch(e, f, g) + K[i] + w[i];\n                uint32_t t2 = sigma0(a) + maj(a, b, c);\n                \n                h = g;\n                g = f;\n                f = e;\n                e = d + t1;\n                d = c;\n                c = b;\n                b = a;\n                a = t1 + t2;\n            }\n            \n            // Добавление сжатого блока к текущему хешу\n            H[0] += a; H[1] += b; H[2] += c; H[3] += d;\n            H[4] += e; H[5] += f; H[6] += g; H[7] += h;\n        }\n        \n        // Формирование итогового хеша\n        stringstream ss;\n        for(int i = 0; i < 8; i++) {\n            ss << hex << setfill('0') << setw(8) << H[i];\n        }\n        \n        return ss.str();\n    }\n};\n\nconst uint32_t SimpleSHA256::K[64] = {\n    0x428a2f98, 0x71374491, 0xb5c0fbcf, 0xe9b5dba5,\n    0x3956c25b, 0x59f111f1, 0x923f82a4, 0xab1c5ed5,\n    // ... (полный массив констант)\n    0xc67178f2\n};\n\nint main() {\n    vector<string> test_messages = {\n        \"\",\n        \"Hello, World!\",\n        \"The quick brown fox jumps over the lazy dog\",\n        \"abc\",\n        \"1234567890\",\n        \"SHA-256\",\n        \"Test message for hashing algorithm\"\n    };\n    \n    cout << \"SHA-256 Hash Demo (Simplified):\\n\";\n    cout << \"Note: This is a simplified version for educational purposes\\n\";\n    cout << \"      Not suitable for cryptographic use!\\n\\n\";\n    \n    for(const string& message : test_messages) {\n        string hash = SimpleSHA256::hash(message);\n        cout << \"Message: \\\"\" << message << \"\\\"\" << endl;\n        cout << \"Hash: \" << hash << endl;\n        cout << \"Length: \" << hash.length() << \" characters\" << endl;\n        \n        // Проверка изменения хеша при небольшом изменении сообщения\n        if(!message.empty()) {\n            string modified = message;\n            modified[modified.length()-1]++;\n            string modified_hash = SimpleSHA256::hash(modified);\n            \n            int diff_count = 0;\n            for(size_t i = 0; i < hash.length(); i++) {\n                if(hash[i] != modified_hash[i]) diff_count++;\n            }\n            \n            cout << \"Avalanche effect: \" << diff_count << \" chars differ\" << endl;\n        }\n        cout << endl;\n    }\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n\nclass Time {\n    int hours, minutes, seconds;\npublic:\n    Time() : Time(0, 0, 0) {} // Делегирует конструктору с параметрами\n    Time(int h) : Time(h, 0, 0) {} // Делегирует конструктору с параметрами\n    Time(int h, int m) : Time(h, m, 0) {} // Делегирует конструктору с параметрами\n    Time(int h, int m, int s) : hours(h), minutes(m), seconds(s) {\n        normalize();\n        std::cout << \"Time object created: \";\n        display();\n    }\n    void normalize() {\n        minutes += seconds / 60;\n        seconds %= 60;\n        hours += minutes / 60;\n        minutes %= 60;\n        hours %= 24;\n    }\n    void display() const {\n        printf(\"%02d:%02d:%02d\\n\", hours, minutes, seconds);\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    Time t1;\n    Time t2(25);\n    Time t3(2, 70);\n    Time t4(1, 30, 90);\n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <cmath>\nusing namespace std;\n\nclass Complex {\n    double real, imag;\npublic:\n    Complex(double r = 0, double i = 0) : real(r), imag(i) {}\n    Complex operator+(const Complex& other) const {\n        return Complex(real + other.real, imag + other.imag);\n    }\n    Complex operator-(const Complex& other) const {\n        return Complex(real - other.real, imag - other.imag);\n    }\n    Complex operator*(const Complex& other) const {\n        return Complex(real * other.real - imag * other.imag,\n                      real * other.imag + imag * other.real);\n    }\n    Complex operator/(const Complex& other) const {\n        double denom = other.real * other.real + other.imag * other.imag;\n        return Complex((real * other.real + imag * other.imag) / denom,\n                      (imag * other.real - real * other.imag) / denom);\n    }\n    Complex& operator+=(const Complex& other) {\n        real += other.real;\n        imag += other.imag;\n        return *this;\n    }\n    Complex& operator-=(const Complex& other) {\n        real -= other.real;\n        imag -= other.imag;\n        return *this;\n    }\n    bool operator==(const Complex& other) const {\n        return real == other.real && imag == other.imag;\n    }\n    bool operator!=(const Complex& other) const {\n        return !(*this == other);\n    }\n    friend ostream& operator<<(ostream& os, const Complex& c) {\n        os << c.real;\n        if (c.imag >= 0) os << \" + \" << c.imag << \"i\";\n        else os << \" - \" << -c.imag << \"i\";\n        return os;\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    Complex a(3, 4), b(1, -2);\n    cout << \"a = \" << a << endl;\n    cout << \"b = \" << b << endl;\n    cout << \"a + b = \" << a + b << endl;\n    cout << \"a - b = \" << a - b << endl;\n    cout << \"a * b = \" << a * b << endl;\n    cout << \"a / b = \" << a / b << endl;\n    a += b;\n    cout << \"After a += b: \" << a << endl;\n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <vector>\nusing namespace std;\n\n// Expression template для векторных операций\ntemplate<typename E>\nclass VecExpression {\npublic:\n    double operator[](size_t i) const { \n        return static_cast<const E&>(*this)[i]; \n    }\n    size_t size() const { \n        return static_cast<const E&>(*this).size(); \n    }\n};\n\nclass Vec : public VecExpression<Vec> {\nprivate:\n    vector<double> data;\n\npublic:\n    Vec(size_t n = 0) : data(n) {}\n    Vec(initializer_list<double> init) : data(init) {}\n    \n    template<typename E>\n    Vec(const VecExpression<E>& expr) {\n        data.resize(expr.size());\n        for (size_t i = 0; i < expr.size(); i++) {\n            data[i] = expr[i];\n        }\n    }\n    \n    double& operator[](size_t i) { return data[i]; }\n    double operator[](size_t i) const { return data[i]; }\n    size_t size() const { return data.size(); }\n    \n    void print() const {\n        for (double x : data) {\n            cout << x << \" \";\n        }\n        cout << endl;\n    }\n};\n\n// Оператор сложения\ntemplate<typename E1, typename E2>\nclass VecSum : public VecExpression<VecSum<E1, E2>> {\nprivate:\n    const E1& lhs;\n    const E2& rhs;\n\npublic:\n    VecSum(const E1& l, const E2& r) : lhs(l), rhs(r) {}\n    \n    double operator[](size_t i) const { \n        return lhs[i] + rhs[i]; \n    }\n    \n    size_t size() const { \n        return lhs.size(); \n    }\n};\n\n// Функция для создания выражения сложения\ntemplate<typename E1, typename E2>\nVecSum<E1, E2> operator+(const VecExpression<E1>& lhs, const VecExpression<E2>& rhs) {\n    return VecSum<E1, E2>(static_cast<const E1&>(lhs), static_cast<const E2&>(rhs));\n}\n\nint main() {\n    Vec a = {1, 2, 3, 4, 5};\n    Vec b = {5, 4, 3, 2, 1};\n    Vec c = {2, 2, 2, 2, 2};\n    \n    // Ленивое вычисление: сложение происходит только при присваивании\n    Vec result = a + b + c;\n    \n    cout << \"Вектор a: \";\n    a.print();\n    cout << \"Вектор b: \";\n    b.print();\n    cout << \"Вектор c: \";\n    c.print();\n    cout << \"Результат a + b + c: \";\n    result.print();\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <vector>\n#include <map>\n#include <string>\n#include <functional>\n#include <memory>\n#include <algorithm>\n#include <random>\n\nclass Event {\npublic:\n    virtual ~Event() = default;\n    virtual std::string getType() const = 0;\n};\n\nclass Observer {\n    int id;\n    static int nextId;\npublic:\n    Observer() : id(++nextId) {}\n    virtual ~Observer() = default;\n    virtual void update(const Event& event) = 0;\n    int getId() const { return id; }\n};\nint Observer::nextId = 0;\n\nclass Subject {\n    std::map<std::string, std::vector<Observer*>> observersByType;\n    \npublic:\n    void attach(const std::string& eventType, Observer* observer) {\n        observersByType[eventType].push_back(observer);\n        std::cout << \"Observer \" << observer->getId() << \" attached to event type: \" << eventType << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    void detach(const std::string& eventType, Observer* observer) {\n        auto& observers = observersByType[eventType];\n        auto it = std::remove(observers.begin(), observers.end(), observer);\n        if (it != observers.end()) {\n            observers.erase(it, observers.end());\n            std::cout << \"Observer \" << observer->getId() << \" detached from event type: \" << eventType << std::endl;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    void notify(const Event& event) {\n        std::string type = event.getType();\n        auto it = observersByType.find(type);\n        if (it != observersByType.end()) {\n            std::cout << \"\\nNotifying \" << it->second.size() << \" observers about event: \" << type << std::endl;\n            for (auto observer : it->second) {\n                observer->update(event);\n            }\n        } else {\n            std::cout << \"No observers for event type: \" << type << std::endl;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    std::size_t getObserverCount(const std::string& eventType) const {\n        auto it = observersByType.find(eventType);\n        return it != observersByType.end() ? it->second.size() : 0;\n    }\n    \n    std::vector<std::string> getEventTypes() const {\n        std::vector<std::string> types;\n        for (const auto& pair : observersByType) {\n            types.push_back(pair.first);\n        }\n        return types;\n    }\n};\n\n// Конкретные события\nclass DataChangedEvent : public Event {\n    std::string data;\npublic:\n    DataChangedEvent(const std::string& d) : data(d) {}\n    std::string getType() const override { return \"DataChanged\"; }\n    std::string getData() const { return data; }\n};\n\nclass StatusEvent : public Event {\n    bool isOnline;\npublic:\n    StatusEvent(bool online) : isOnline(online) {}\n    std::string getType() const override { return \"StatusChanged\"; }\n    bool getIsOnline() const { return isOnline; }\n};\n\nclass ErrorEvent : public Event {\n    int errorCode;\n    std::string errorMessage;\npublic:\n    ErrorEvent(int code, const std::string& msg) : errorCode(code), errorMessage(msg) {}\n    std::string getType() const override { return \"Error\"; }\n    int getErrorCode() const { return errorCode; }\n    std::string getErrorMessage() const { return errorMessage; }\n};\n\n// Конкретные наблюдатели\nclass LoggerObserver : public Observer {\npublic:\n    void update(const Event& event) override {\n        if (event.getType() == \"DataChanged\") {\n            auto& dataEvent = dynamic_cast<const DataChangedEvent&>(event);\n            std::cout << \"Logger [\" << getId() << \"]: Data changed to '\" \n                      << dataEvent.getData() << \"'\" << std::endl;\n        } else if (event.getType() == \"StatusChanged\") {\n            auto& statusEvent = dynamic_cast<const StatusEvent&>(event);\n            std::cout << \"Logger [\" << getId() << \"]: Status changed to \" \n                      << (statusEvent.getIsOnline() ? \"Online\" : \"Offline\") << std::endl;\n        } else if (event.getType() == \"Error\") {\n            auto& errorEvent = dynamic_cast<const ErrorEvent&>(event);\n            std::cout << \"Logger [\" << getId() << \"]: ERROR #\" \n                      << errorEvent.getErrorCode() << \": \" << errorEvent.getErrorMessage() << std::endl;\n        }\n    }\n};\n\nclass MonitorObserver : public Observer {\npublic:\n    void update(const Event& event) override {\n        std::cout << \"Monitor [\" << getId() << \"]: Received event type: \" \n                  << event.getType() << std::endl;\n    }\n};\n\nclass StatisticsObserver : public Observer {\n    std::map<std::string, int> eventCounts;\npublic:\n    void update(const Event& event) override {\n        eventCounts[event.getType()]++;\n        std::cout << \"Statistics [\" << getId() << \"]: Event '\" << event.getType() \n                  << \"' received. Total count: \" << eventCounts[event.getType()] << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    void printStats() const {\n        std::cout << \"\\n=== Event Statistics ===\" << std::endl;\n        for (const auto& pair : eventCounts) {\n            std::cout << \"Event '\" << pair.first << \"': \" << pair.second << \" times\" << std::endl;\n        }\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    std::cout << \"=== Observer Pattern with Event Type Support ===\" << std::endl;\n    \n    Subject subject;\n    \n    // Создаем наблюдателей\n    LoggerObserver logger1, logger2;\n    MonitorObserver monitor;\n    StatisticsObserver stats;\n    \n    // Прикрепляем наблюдателей к разным типам событий\n    subject.attach(\"DataChanged\", &logger1);\n    subject.attach(\"StatusChanged\", &logger1);\n    subject.attach(\"Error\", &logger1);\n    \n    subject.attach(\"DataChanged\", &logger2);\n    subject.attach(\"Error\", &logger2);\n    \n    subject.attach(\"DataChanged\", &monitor);\n    subject.attach(\"StatusChanged\", &monitor);\n    subject.attach(\"Error\", &monitor);\n    \n    subject.attach(\"DataChanged\", &stats);\n    subject.attach(\"StatusChanged\", &stats);\n    subject.attach(\"Error\", &stats);\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\n=== Initial Observer Counts ===\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"DataChanged observers: \" << subject.getObserverCount(\"DataChanged\") << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"StatusChanged observers: \" << subject.getObserverCount(\"StatusChanged\") << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"Error observers: \" << subject.getObserverCount(\"Error\") << std::endl;\n    \n    // Генерируем события\n    std::cout << \"\\n=== Generating Events ===\" << std::endl;\n    \n    DataChangedEvent dataEvent1(\"Initial configuration\");\n    subject.notify(dataEvent1);\n    \n    StatusEvent statusEvent1(true);\n    subject.notify(statusEvent1);\n    \n    ErrorEvent errorEvent1(404, \"Resource not found\");\n    subject.notify(errorEvent1);\n    \n    DataChangedEvent dataEvent2(\"Updated settings\");\n    subject.notify(dataEvent2);\n    \n    StatusEvent statusEvent2(false);\n    subject.notify(statusEvent2);\n    \n    // Демонстрация detach\n    std::cout << \"\\n=== Detaching logger2 from DataChanged events ===\" << std::endl;\n    subject.detach(\"DataChanged\", &logger2);\n    \n    DataChangedEvent dataEvent3(\"Final configuration\");\n    subject.notify(dataEvent3);\n    \n    // Показываем статистику\n    stats.printStats();\n    \n    // Тестирование события без наблюдателей\n    std::cout << \"\\n=== Testing event without observers ===\" << std::endl;\n    class CustomEvent : public Event {\n    public:\n        std::string getType() const override { return \"CustomEvent\"; }\n    };\n    \n    CustomEvent customEvent;\n    subject.notify(customEvent);\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\n=== Program Completed ===\" << std::endl;\n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <vector>\n#include <algorithm>\nusing namespace std;\n\nvoid backtrack(vector<int>& nums, int start, vector<vector<int>>& result) {\n    if (start == nums.size()) {\n        result.push_back(nums);\n        return;\n    }\n    for (int i = start; i < nums.size(); i++) {\n        swap(nums[start], nums[i]);\n        backtrack(nums, start + 1, result);\n        swap(nums[start], nums[i]);\n    }\n}\n\nvector<vector<int>> permute(vector<int>& nums) {\n    vector<vector<int>> result;\n    backtrack(nums, 0, result);\n    return result;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    vector<int> nums = {1,2,3};\n    vector<vector<int>> perms = permute(nums);\n    for (auto& perm : perms) {\n        for (int num : perm) cout << num << \" \";\n        cout << endl;\n    }\n    return 0;\n}

#include <unistd.h>\n#include <sys/wait.h>\n#include <iostream>\n#include <cstring>\n#include <vector>\n#include <string>\nusing namespace std;\nvoid execute_command(const vector<string>& args) {\n    vector<char*> c_args;\n    for(const auto& arg : args) {\n        c_args.push_back(const_cast<char*>(arg.c_str()));\n    }\n    c_args.push_back(nullptr);\n    execvp(c_args[0], c_args.data());\n    perror(\"execvp\");\n    _exit(1);\n}\nint main() {\n    string input;\n    while(true) {\n        cout << \"myshell> \";\n        getline(cin, input);\n        if(input == \"exit\") break;\n        vector<string> args;\n        size_t start = 0;\n        for(size_t i = 0; i <= input.size(); i++) {\n            if(i == input.size() || input[i] == ' ') {\n                if(i > start) args.push_back(input.substr(start, i - start));\n                start = i + 1;\n            }\n        }\n        if(args.empty()) continue;\n        pid_t pid = fork();\n        if(pid == 0) {\n            execute_command(args);\n        } else if(pid > 0) {\n            wait(nullptr);\n        } else {\n            perror(\"fork\");\n        }\n    }\n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <cstring>\nusing namespace std;\n\nstruct TaggedData {\n    enum DataType { INTEGER, DOUBLE, TEXT } type;\n    \n    union {\n        int int_value;\n        double double_value;\n        char* text_value;\n    };\n    \n    TaggedData(int val) : type(INTEGER) { int_value = val; }\n    TaggedData(double val) : type(DOUBLE) { double_value = val; }\n    TaggedData(const char* text) : type(TEXT) {\n        text_value = new char[strlen(text) + 1];\n        strcpy(text_value, text);\n    }\n    \n    ~TaggedData() {\n        if (type == TEXT) {\n            delete[] text_value;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    TaggedData(const TaggedData& other) : type(other.type) {\n        switch (type) {\n            case INTEGER: int_value = other.int_value; break;\n            case DOUBLE: double_value = other.double_value; break;\n            case TEXT: \n                text_value = new char[strlen(other.text_value) + 1];\n                strcpy(text_value, other.text_value);\n                break;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    void print() const {\n        switch (type) {\n            case INTEGER: cout << \"Integer: \" << int_value; break;\n            case DOUBLE: cout << \"Double: \" << double_value; break;\n            case TEXT: cout << \"Text: \\\"\" << text_value << \"\\\"\"; break;\n        }\n        cout << endl;\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    TaggedData data1(42);\n    TaggedData data2(3.14159);\n    TaggedData data3(\"Hello World\");\n    \n    cout << \"Данные:\" << endl;\n    data1.print();\n    data2.print();\n    data3.print();\n    \n    TaggedData data4 = data3;\n    cout << \"\\nСкопированные данные:\" << endl;\n    data4.print();\n    \n    cout << \"\\nРазмер TaggedData: \" << sizeof(TaggedData) << \" байт\" << endl;\n    \n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <string>\n#include <unordered_map>\nusing namespace std;\n\nint main() {\n    string text = \"HELLO WORLD\";\n    unordered_map<char, char> cipher;\n    \n    // Создаем простой шифр сдвига на 3 позиции\n    for(char c = 'A'; c <= 'Z'; c++) {\n        cipher[c] = 'A' + ((c - 'A' + 3) % 26);\n    }\n    \n    string encrypted;\n    for(char c : text) {\n        if(cipher.find(c) != cipher.end()) {\n            encrypted += cipher[c];\n        } else {\n            encrypted += c; // пробелы и другие символы остаются\n        }\n    }\n    \n    cout << \"Исходный: \" << text << endl;\n    cout << \"Зашифрованный: \" << encrypted << endl;\n    \n    // Дешифровка\n    string decrypted;\n    unordered_map<char, char> decipher;\n    for(const auto& pair : cipher) {\n        decipher[pair.second] = pair.first;\n    }\n    \n    for(char c : encrypted) {\n        if(decipher.find(c) != decipher.end()) {\n            decrypted += decipher[c];\n        } else {\n            decrypted += c;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    cout << \"Расшифрованный: \" << decrypted << endl;\n    \n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\nusing namespace std;\n\nvoid rotateArray(int arr[], int size, int k) {\n    k = k % size;\n    \n    int temp[k];\n    for (int i = 0; i < k; i++) {\n        temp[i] = arr[size - k + i];\n    }\n    \n    for (int i = size - 1; i >= k; i--) {\n        arr[i] = arr[i - k];\n    }\n    \n    for (int i = 0; i < k; i++) {\n        arr[i] = temp[i];\n    }\n}\n\nvoid printArray(int arr[], int size) {\n    for (int i = 0; i < size; i++) {\n        cout << arr[i] << \" \";\n    }\n    cout << endl;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    int arr[] = {1, 2, 3, 4, 5};\n    rotateArray(arr, 5, 2);\n    printArray(arr, 5);\n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\nusing namespace std;\n\nclass Strategy {\npublic:\n    virtual int execute(int a, int b) = 0;\n};\n\nclass Add : public Strategy {\npublic:\n    int execute(int a, int b) override { return a + b; }\n};\n\nclass Subtract : public Strategy {\npublic:\n    int execute(int a, int b) override { return a - b; }\n};\n\nclass Context {\n    Strategy* strategy;\npublic:\n    void setStrategy(Strategy* s) { strategy = s; }\n    int execute(int a, int b) { return strategy->execute(a, b); }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    Context ctx;\n    Add add;\n    ctx.setStrategy(&add);\n    cout << ctx.execute(5, 3) << endl;\n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <cstdlib>\n#include <ctime>\n\nint main() {\n    std::srand(std::time(0));\n    const int MAX_ATTEMPTS = 7;\n    const int MIN_NUM = 1;\n    const int MAX_NUM = 100;\n    \n    int secretNumber = MIN_NUM + std::rand() % (MAX_NUM - MIN_NUM + 1);\n    int userGuess;\n    int attempts = 0;\n    bool guessed = false;\n    \n    std::cout << \"=== Игра 'Угадай число' ===\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"Компьютер загадал число от \" << MIN_NUM << \" до \" << MAX_NUM << \".\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"У вас есть \" << MAX_ATTEMPTS << \" попыток, чтобы угадать его.\" << std::endl;\n    \n    while (attempts < MAX_ATTEMPTS && !guessed) {\n        attempts++;\n        std::cout << \"\\nПопытка №\" << attempts << \"/\" << MAX_ATTEMPTS << \". Ваш вариант: \";\n        std::cin >> userGuess;\n        \n        if (userGuess < MIN_NUM || userGuess > MAX_NUM) {\n            std::cout << \"Число должно быть в диапазоне от \" << MIN_NUM << \" до \" << MAX_NUM << \"!\" << std::endl;\n            attempts--;\n            continue;\n        }\n        \n        if (userGuess == secretNumber) {\n            guessed = true;\n            std::cout << \"Поздравляю! Вы угадали число \" << secretNumber << \" за \" << attempts << \" попыток!\" << std::endl;\n        } else if (userGuess < secretNumber) {\n            std::cout << \"Загаданное число БОЛЬШЕ.\";\n            if (attempts == MAX_ATTEMPTS - 1) {\n                std::cout << \" Осторожно, осталась 1 попытка!\";\n            } else if (attempts < MAX_ATTEMPTS - 1) {\n                std::cout << \" Осталось попыток: \" << (MAX_ATTEMPTS - attempts);\n            }\n            std::cout << std::endl;\n        } else {\n            std::cout << \"Загаданное число МЕНЬШЕ.\";\n            if (attempts == MAX_ATTEMPTS - 1) {\n                std::cout << \" Осторожно, осталась 1 попытка!\";\n            } else if (attempts < MAX_ATTEMPTS - 1) {\n                std::cout << \" Осталось попыток: \" << (MAX_ATTEMPTS - attempts);\n            }\n            std::cout << std::endl;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    if (!guessed) {\n        std::cout << \"\\nК сожалению, вы исчерпали все попытки. Загаданное число было: \" << secretNumber << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\nСпасибо за игру!\" << std::endl;\n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <vector>\n#include <climits>\n\nint main() {\n    int n;\n    \n    std::cout << \"Алгоритм Кадане для поиска максимальной суммы подмассива\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"Введите размер массива: \";\n    std::cin >> n;\n    \n    if (n <= 0) {\n        std::cout << \"Размер массива должен быть положительным!\" << std::endl;\n        return 1;\n    }\n    \n    std::vector<int> arr(n);\n    std::cout << \"Введите \" << n << \" чисел: \";\n    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {\n        std::cin >> arr[i];\n    }\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\nМассив: \";\n    for (int num : arr) {\n        std::cout << num << \" \";\n    }\n    std::cout << std::endl;\n    \n    // Алгоритм Кадане\n    int maxSoFar = INT_MIN;\n    int maxEndingHere = 0;\n    int start = 0, end = 0, tempStart = 0;\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\nВыполнение алгоритма Кадане:\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"i\\tЭлемент\\tТекущая сумма\\tМакс. сумма\\tНачало\\tКонец\" << std::endl;\n    \n    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {\n        maxEndingHere += arr[i];\n        \n        // Если текущая сумма стала меньше элемента, начинаем новый подмассив\n        if (arr[i] > maxEndingHere) {\n            maxEndingHere = arr[i];\n            tempStart = i;\n        }\n        \n        // Обновляем максимальную сумму, если текущая сумма больше\n        if (maxEndingHere > maxSoFar) {\n            maxSoFar = maxEndingHere;\n            start = tempStart;\n            end = i;\n        }\n        \n        std::cout << i << \"\\t\" << arr[i] << \"\\t\" << maxEndingHere << \"\\t\\t\" \n                  << maxSoFar << \"\\t\\t\" << start << \"\\t\" << end << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\nРезультат:\" << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"Максимальная сумма подмассива: \" << maxSoFar << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"Подмассив: \";\n    for (int i = start; i <= end; i++) {\n        std::cout << arr[i] << \" \";\n    }\n    std::cout << std::endl;\n    \n    // Альтернативный алгоритм для проверки (полный перебор)\n    std::cout << \"\\nПроверка полным перебором:\" << std::endl;\n    int bruteMax = INT_MIN;\n    int bruteStart = 0, bruteEnd = 0;\n    \n    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {\n        int currentSum = 0;\n        for (int j = i; j < n; j++) {\n            currentSum += arr[j];\n            if (currentSum > bruteMax) {\n                bruteMax = currentSum;\n                bruteStart = i;\n                bruteEnd = j;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    std::cout << \"Максимальная сумма (перебор): \" << bruteMax << std::endl;\n    std::cout << \"Подмассив (перебор): \";\n    for (int i = bruteStart; i <= bruteEnd; i++) {\n        std::cout << arr[i] << \" \";\n    }\n    std::cout << std::endl;\n    \n    if (maxSoFar == bruteMax && start == bruteStart && end == bruteEnd) {\n        std::cout << \"\\n✓ Алгоритм Кадане работает правильно!\" << std::endl;\n    } else {\n        std::cout << \"\\n✗ Ошибка в алгоритме Кадане!\" << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <thread>\n#include <chrono>\n#include <ctime>\nusing namespace std;\n\nvoid worker_with_sleep_for(int id) {\n    cout << \"Поток \" << id << \" начал работу\" << endl;\n    this_thread::sleep_for(chrono::milliseconds(id * 200));\n    cout << \"Поток \" << id << \" завершил работу после sleep_for\" << endl;\n}\n\nvoid worker_with_sleep_until(int id) {\n    auto wakeup_time = chrono::system_clock::now() + chrono::seconds(1);\n    \n    cout << \"Поток \" << id << \" ожидает до определенного времени\" << endl;\n    this_thread::sleep_until(wakeup_time);\n    cout << \"Поток \" << id << \" проснулся в \" \n         << chrono::system_clock::to_time_t(chrono::system_clock::now()) << endl;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    thread t1(worker_with_sleep_for, 1);\n    thread t2(worker_with_sleep_for, 2);\n    thread t3(worker_with_sleep_until, 3);\n    \n    t1.join();\n    t2.join();\n    t3.join();\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\nusing namespace std;\n\nclass Base {\npublic:\n    virtual void func(int x) {\n        cout << \"Base::func(int)\" << endl;\n    }\n};\n\nclass Derived : public Base {\npublic:\n    void func(double x) { // Не переопределяет, а скрывает\n        cout << \"Derived::func(double)\" << endl;\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    Derived d;\n    Base* b = &d;\n    b->func(5);\n    d.func(5.5);\n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n\nclass Base {\npublic:\n    virtual void foo() { std::cout << \"Base::foo\" << std::endl; }\n    virtual ~Base() = default;\n};\n\nclass Middle1 : virtual public Base {\npublic:\n    void foo() override { std::cout << \"Middle1::foo\" << std::endl; }\n};\n\nclass Middle2 : virtual public Base {\npublic:\n    void foo() override { std::cout << \"Middle2::foo\" << std::endl; }\n};\n\nclass Final : public Middle1, public Middle2 {\npublic:\n    void foo() override { \n        Middle1::foo();\n        std::cout << \"Final::foo\" << std::endl; \n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    Final f;\n    f.foo();\n    Base* b = &f;\n    b->foo();\n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\nusing namespace std;\n\nclass Base {\npublic:\n    virtual void risky() {\n        cout << \"Base safe\" << endl;\n    }\n};\n\nclass Derived : public Base {\npublic:\n    void risky() override {\n        cout << \"Derived throwing\" << endl;\n        throw runtime_error(\"Error\");\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    try {\n        Derived d;\n        Base& b = d;\n        b.risky();\n    } catch (const exception& e) {\n        cout << \"Caught: \" << e.what() << endl;\n    }\n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <vector>\nusing namespace std;\n\nint findMissingNumber(vector<int>& nums, int n) {\n    int expectedSum = n * (n + 1) / 2;\n    int actualSum = 0;\n    \n    for (int num : nums) {\n        actualSum += num;\n    }\n    \n    return expectedSum - actualSum;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    vector<int> nums = {1, 2, 4, 5, 6};\n    cout << findMissingNumber(nums, 6) << endl;\n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <vector>\n#include <stdexcept>\n\nclass TransactionalOperation {\n    std::vector<std::string> steps;\n    std::vector<std::string> executed;\n    \n    void rollback() {\n        std::cout << \"Rolling back \" << executed.size() << \" steps\" << std::endl;\n        while (!executed.empty()) {\n            std::cout << \"Undoing: \" << executed.back() << std::endl;\n            executed.pop_back();\n        }\n    }\n    \npublic:\n    // Конструкторы\n    TransactionalOperation() = default;\n    \n    // Запрещаем копирование и присваивание\n    TransactionalOperation(const TransactionalOperation&) = delete;\n    TransactionalOperation& operator=(const TransactionalOperation&) = delete;\n    \n    // Деструктор выполняет rollback если операция не завершена\n    ~TransactionalOperation() noexcept {\n        if (!executed.empty()) {\n            try {\n                rollback();\n            } catch (...) {\n                // Деструкторы не должны выбрасывать исключения\n                std::cerr << \"Warning: Exception during rollback in destructor\" << std::endl;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // Методы\n    void add_step(const std::string& step) { \n        steps.push_back(step); \n    }\n    \n    void execute() {\n        for (const auto& step : steps) {\n            std::cout << \"Executing: \" << step << std::endl;\n            \n            // Имитация возможного сбоя\n            if (step.find(\"fail\") != std::string::npos) {\n                throw std::runtime_error(\"Step failed: \" + step);\n            }\n            \n            executed.push_back(step);\n        }\n        \n        std::cout << \"All steps completed successfully\" << std::endl;\n        executed.clear(); // Очищаем список выполненных шагов\n    }\n    \n    // Дополнительные методы для демонстрации\n    std::size_t get_step_count() const { return steps.size(); }\n    std::size_t get_executed_count() const { return executed.size(); }\n    void clear() { \n        steps.clear(); \n        executed.clear(); \n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    std::cout << \"=== RAII with Rollback Demo ===\\n\" << std::endl;\n    \n    // Тест 1: Успешное выполнение\n    std::cout << \"Test 1: Successful operation\" << std::endl;\n    try {\n        TransactionalOperation op1;\n        op1.add_step(\"create user\");\n        op1.add_step(\"update profile\");\n        op1.add_step(\"send email\");\n        op1.execute();\n        std::cout << \"Operation completed without rollback\\n\" << std::endl;\n    } catch (const std::exception& e) {\n        std::cout << \"Unexpected error: \" << e.what() << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    // Тест 2: Сбой в середине операции\n    std::cout << \"Test 2: Failure in the middle\" << std::endl;\n    try {\n        TransactionalOperation op2;\n        op2.add_step(\"create user\");\n        op2.add_step(\"update profile\");\n        op2.add_step(\"fail here\");\n        op2.add_step(\"send email\");\n        op2.execute();\n    } catch (const std::exception& e) {\n        std::cout << \"Caught: \" << e.what() << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"Rollback performed automatically in destructor\\n\" << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    // Тест 3: Другой сценарий сбоя\n    std::cout << \"Test 3: Multiple steps with late failure\" << std::endl;\n    try {\n        TransactionalOperation op3;\n        op3.add_step(\"allocate memory\");\n        op3.add_step(\"open file\");\n        op3.add_step(\"write data\");\n        op3.add_step(\"critical operation fail\");\n        op3.add_step(\"close file\");\n        op3.add_step(\"free memory\");\n        \n        std::cout << \"Steps to execute: \" << op3.get_step_count() << std::endl;\n        op3.execute();\n    } catch (const std::exception& e) {\n        std::cout << \"Caught: \" << e.what() << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"Rollback executed for completed steps\\n\" << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    // Тест 4: Вложенные операции\n    std::cout << \"Test 4: Nested operations\" << std::endl;\n    try {\n        TransactionalOperation outer;\n        outer.add_step(\"Outer step 1\");\n        \n        {\n            TransactionalOperation inner;\n            inner.add_step(\"Inner step 1\");\n            inner.add_step(\"Inner step fail\");\n            inner.add_step(\"Inner step 3\");\n            inner.execute();\n        } // inner разрушается здесь, выполняется rollback\n        \n        outer.add_step(\"Outer step 2\");\n        outer.execute();\n    } catch (const std::exception& e) {\n        std::cout << \"Caught: \" << e.what() << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    std::cout << \"\\n=== Demo completed ===\" << std::endl;\n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <string>\nusing namespace std;\n\nenum class State {\n Idle,\n Running,\n Paused,\n Stopped\n};\n\nState handleCommand(State current, const string& cmd) {\n if (cmd == \"start\") {\n return (current == State::Idle) ? State::Running : current;\n } else if (cmd == \"pause\") {\n return (current == State::Running) ? State::Paused : current;\n } else if (cmd == \"resume\") {\n return (current == State::Paused) ? State::Running : current;\n } else if (cmd == \"stop\") {\n return State::Stopped;\n }\n return current;\n}\n\nint main() {\n State s = State::Idle;\n cout << \"Начальное состояние: Idle\" << endl;\n \n s = handleCommand(s, \"start\");\n cout << \"После 'start': \" << static_cast<int>(s) << endl;\n \n s = handleCommand(s, \"pause\");\n cout << \"После 'pause': \" << static_cast<int>(s) << endl;\n \n s = handleCommand(s, \"stop\");\n cout << \"Финальное состояние: \" << static_cast<int>(s) << endl;\n \n return 0;\n}
