#include <iostream>\n#include <string>\n#include <cctype>\nusing namespace std;\n\nbool isNumber(string s) {\n    int i = 0;\n    int n = s.length();\n    while (i < n && s[i] == ' ') i++;\n    if (i < n && (s[i] == '+' || s[i] == '-')) i++;\n    bool is_numeric = false;\n    while (i < n && isdigit(s[i])) {\n        i++;\n        is_numeric = true;\n    }\n    if (i < n && s[i] == '.') {\n        i++;\n        while (i < n && isdigit(s[i])) {\n            i++;\n            is_numeric = true;\n        }\n    }\n    if (is_numeric && i < n && (s[i] == 'e' || s[i] == 'E')) {\n        i++;\n        if (i < n && (s[i] == '+' || s[i] == '-')) i++;\n        is_numeric = false;\n        while (i < n && isdigit(s[i])) {\n            i++;\n            is_numeric = true;\n        }\n    }\n    while (i < n && s[i] == ' ') i++;\n    return is_numeric && i == n;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    string s = \" -123.456e789 \";\n    cout << (isNumber(s) ? \"true\" : \"false\") << endl;\n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <vector>\n#include <string>\n#include <map>\n#include <algorithm>\n#include <memory>\n#include <iomanip>\n\nclass Course;\nclass Student;\n\nclass Grade {\nprivate:\n    std::string courseId;\n    char grade;\n    int credits;\npublic:\n    Grade(std::string cid, char g, int cr) : courseId(cid), grade(g), credits(cr) {}\n    \n    double getGradePoints() const {\n        std::map<char, double> gradePoints = {\n            {'A', 4.0}, {'B', 3.0}, {'C', 2.0}, {'D', 1.0}, {'F', 0.0}\n        };\n        return gradePoints[grade];\n    }\n    \n    std::string getCourseId() const { return courseId; }\n    char getGrade() const { return grade; }\n    int getCredits() const { return credits; }\n    \n    void display() const {\n        std::cout << courseId << \": \" << grade << \" (\" << credits << \" credits)\";\n    }\n};\n\nclass Student {\nprivate:\n    std::string studentId;\n    std::string name;\n    std::string major;\n    int year;\n    std::vector<Grade> grades;\n    \npublic:\n    Student(std::string id, std::string n, std::string m, int y) \n        : studentId(id), name(n), major(m), year(y) {}\n    \n    void addGrade(const Grade& grade) {\n        grades.push_back(grade);\n    }\n    \n    double calculateGPA() const {\n        if(grades.empty()) return 0.0;\n        \n        double totalPoints = 0;\n        int totalCredits = 0;\n        \n        for(const auto& grade : grades) {\n            totalPoints += grade.getGradePoints() * grade.getCredits();\n            totalCredits += grade.getCredits();\n        }\n        \n        return totalCredits > 0 ? totalPoints / totalCredits : 0.0;\n    }\n    \n    std::vector<Grade> getGrades() const { return grades; }\n    \n    void displayTranscript() const {\n        std::cout << \"\\n=== Transcript for \" << name << \" ===\" << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"Student ID: \" << studentId << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"Major: \" << major << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"Year: \" << year << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"GPA: \" << std::fixed << std::setprecision(2) << calculateGPA() << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"\\nGrades:\" << std::endl;\n        std::cout << std::string(40, '-') << std::endl;\n        \n        for(const auto& grade : grades) {\n            grade.display();\n            std::cout << std::endl;\n        }\n        std::cout << std::string(40, '-') << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    std::string getStudentId() const { return studentId; }\n    std::string getName() const { return name; }\n    std::string getMajor() const { return major; }\n    int getYear() const { return year; }\n    \n    bool isHonors() const {\n        return calculateGPA() >= 3.5;\n    }\n};\n\nclass Course {\nprivate:\n    std::string courseId;\n    std::string courseName;\n    std::string department;\n    int credits;\n    int capacity;\n    std::vector<std::string> enrolledStudents;\n    \npublic:\n    Course(std::string id, std::string name, std::string dept, int cr, int cap) \n        : courseId(id), courseName(name), department(dept), credits(cr), capacity(cap) {}\n    \n    bool enrollStudent(std::string studentId) {\n        if(enrolledStudents.size() >= capacity) {\n            return false;\n        }\n        \n        if(std::find(enrolledStudents.begin(), enrolledStudents.end(), studentId) != enrolledStudents.end()) {\n            return false;\n        }\n        \n        enrolledStudents.push_back(studentId);\n        return true;\n    }\n    \n    bool dropStudent(std::string studentId) {\n        auto it = std::find(enrolledStudents.begin(), enrolledStudents.end(), studentId);\n        if(it != enrolledStudents.end()) {\n            enrolledStudents.erase(it);\n            return true;\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n    \n    void displayCourseInfo() const {\n        std::cout << std::left << std::setw(10) << courseId \n                  << std::setw(30) << courseName \n                  << std::setw(15) << department \n                  << std::setw(8) << credits \n                  << std::setw(10) << enrolledStudents.size() << \"/\" << capacity << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    std::string getCourseId() const { return courseId; }\n    std::string getCourseName() const { return courseName; }\n    std::string getDepartment() const { return department; }\n    int getCredits() const { return credits; }\n    int getEnrollmentCount() const { return enrolledStudents.size(); }\n    int getCapacity() const { return capacity; }\n    bool isFull() const { return enrolledStudents.size() >= capacity; }\n    \n    std::vector<std::string> getEnrolledStudents() const { return enrolledStudents; }\n};\n\nclass University {\nprivate:\n    std::string name;\n    std::map<std::string, std::shared_ptr<Student>> students;\n    std::map<std::string, std::shared_ptr<Course>> courses;\n    \npublic:\n    University(std::string n) : name(n) {}\n    \n    void addStudent(std::shared_ptr<Student> student) {\n        students[student->getStudentId()] = student;\n    }\n    \n    void addCourse(std::shared_ptr<Course> course) {\n        courses[course->getCourseId()] = course;\n    }\n    \n    bool enrollStudentInCourse(std::string studentId, std::string courseId) {\n        auto studentIt = students.find(studentId);\n        auto courseIt = courses.find(courseId);\n        \n        if(studentIt == students.end() || courseIt == courses.end()) {\n            return false;\n        }\n        \n        return courseIt->second->enrollStudent(studentId);\n    }\n    \n    bool dropStudentFromCourse(std::string studentId, std::string courseId) {\n        auto courseIt = courses.find(courseId);\n        if(courseIt == courses.end()) {\n            return false;\n        }\n        \n        return courseIt->second->dropStudent(studentId);\n    }\n    \n    bool assignGrade(std::string studentId, std::string courseId, char grade) {\n        auto studentIt = students.find(studentId);\n        auto courseIt = courses.find(courseId);\n        \n        if(studentIt == students.end() || courseIt == courses.end()) {\n            return false;\n        }\n        \n        studentIt->second->addGrade(Grade(courseId, grade, courseIt->second->getCredits()));\n        return true;\n    }\n    \n    void displayAllStudents() const {\n        std::cout << \"\\n=== All Students ===\" << std::endl;\n        std::cout << std::left << std::setw(15) << \"Student ID\" \n                  << std::setw(25) << \"Name\" \n                  << std::setw(20) << \"Major\" \n                  << std::setw(8) << \"Year\" \n                  << std::setw(8) << \"GPA\" \n                  << std::setw(10) << \"Honors\" << std::endl;\n        std::cout << std::string(86, '-') << std::endl;\n        \n        for(const auto& [id, student] : students) {\n            std::cout << std::left << std::setw(15) << student->getStudentId()\n                      << std::setw(25) << student->getName()\n                      << std::setw(20) << student->getMajor()\n                      << std::setw(8) << student->getYear()\n                      << std::setw(8) << std::fixed << std::setprecision(2) << student->calculateGPA()\n                      << (student->isHonors() ? \"Yes\" : \"No\") << std::endl;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    void displayAllCourses() const {\n        std::cout << \"\\n=== All Courses ===\" << std::endl;\n        std::cout << std::left << std::setw(10) << \"Course ID\" \n                  << std::setw(30) << \"Course Name\" \n                  << std::setw(15) << \"Department\" \n                  << std::setw(8) << \"Credits\" \n                  << std::setw(12) << \"Enrollment\" << std::endl;\n        std::cout << std::string(75, '-') << std::endl;\n        \n        for(const auto& [id, course] : courses) {\n            course->displayCourseInfo();\n        }\n    }\n    \n    void displayCourseEnrollment(std::string courseId) const {\n        auto it = courses.find(courseId);\n        if(it == courses.end()) {\n            std::cout << \"Course not found.\" << std::endl;\n            return;\n        }\n        \n        std::cout << \"\\n=== Enrollment for \" << it->second->getCourseName() << \" ===\" << std::endl;\n        std::vector<std::string> enrolled = it->second->getEnrolledStudents();\n        \n        if(enrolled.empty()) {\n            std::cout << \"No students enrolled.\" << std::endl;\n            return;\n        }\n        \n        for(const auto& studentId : enrolled) {\n            auto studentIt = students.find(studentId);\n            if(studentIt != students.end()) {\n                std::cout << studentId << \": \" << studentIt->second->getName() << std::endl;\n            }\n        }\n        std::cout << \"Total: \" << enrolled.size() << \" students\" << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    void displayStudentSchedule(std::string studentId) const {\n        auto it = students.find(studentId);\n        if(it == students.end()) {\n            std::cout << \"Student not found.\" << std::endl;\n            return;\n        }\n        \n        std::cout << \"\\n=== Schedule for \" << it->second->getName() << \" ===\" << std::endl;\n        \n        int enrolledCount = 0;\n        for(const auto& [courseId, course] : courses) {\n            std::vector<std::string> enrolled = course->getEnrolledStudents();\n            if(std::find(enrolled.begin(), enrolled.end(), studentId) != enrolled.end()) {\n                course->displayCourseInfo();\n                enrolledCount++;\n            }\n        }\n        \n        if(enrolledCount == 0) {\n            std::cout << \"Student is not enrolled in any courses.\" << std::endl;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    void displayUniversityStats() const {\n        std::cout << \"\\n=== University Statistics ===\" << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"University: \" << name << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"Total Students: \" << students.size() << std::endl;\n        std::cout << \"Total Courses: \" << courses.size() << std::endl;\n        \n        int totalEnrollment = 0;\n        for(const auto& [id, course] : courses) {\n            totalEnrollment += course->getEnrollmentCount();\n        }\n        std::cout << \"Total Course Enrollments: \" << totalEnrollment << std::endl;\n        \n        double totalGPA = 0;\n        int studentCount = 0;\n        for(const auto& [id, student] : students) {\n            totalGPA += student->calculateGPA();\n            studentCount++;\n        }\n        std::cout << \"Average GPA: \" << std::fixed << std::setprecision(2) \n                  << (studentCount > 0 ? totalGPA / studentCount : 0) << std::endl;\n        \n        int honorsCount = 0;\n        for(const auto& [id, student] : students) {\n            if(student->isHonors()) honorsCount++;\n        }\n        std::cout << \"Honors Students: \" << honorsCount << std::endl;\n    }\n    \n    std::shared_ptr<Student> getStudent(std::string studentId) {\n        auto it = students.find(studentId);\n courses.end() ? it->second : nullptr;\n    }\n};\n\nint main() {\n    University university(\"Tech University\");\n    \n    auto student1 = std::make_shared<Student>(\"S1001\", \"John Doe\", #include <iostream>\n#include <string>\n\nclass SecretVault {\nprivate:\n    std::string secret;\npublic:\n    SecretVault() : secret(\"Золотой ключ\") {}\n    friend std::string checkAccess(const SecretVault& vault, const std::string& password);\n};\n\nstd::string checkAccess(const SecretVault& vault, const std::string& password) {\n    if (password == \"12345\") {\n        return vault.secret;\n    } else {\n        return \"Доступ запрещен\";\n    }\n}\n\nint main() {\n    SecretVault vault;\n    std::string input;\n    std::cout << \"Введите пароль: \";\n    std::cin >> input;\n    std::cout << checkAccess(vault, input) << std::endl;\n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <string>\n#include <unordered_map>\n#include <cctype>\n#include <algorithm>\nusing namespace std;\n\nbool areAnagramsWithPunctuation(const string& str1, const string& str2) {\n    unordered_map<char, int> charCount;\n    \n    for(char c : str1) {\n        if(isalnum(c)) {\n            char lowerC = tolower(c);\n            charCount[lowerC]++;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    for(char c : str2) {\n        if(isalnum(c)) {\n            char lowerC = tolower(c);\n            if(charCount.find(lowerC) == charCount.end() || charCount[lowerC] == 0) {\n                return false;\n            }\n            charCount[lowerC]--;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    // Проверяем что все счетчики обнулились\n    for(const auto& pair : charCount) {\n        if(pair.second != 0) {\n            return false;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    return true;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    string test1 = \"A gentleman\";\n    string test2 = \"Elegant man\";\n    string test3 = \"Hello\";\n    string test4 = \"World\";\n    \n    cout << test1 << \" и \" << test2 << (areAnagramsWithPunctuation(test1, test2) ? \" - анаграммы\" : \" - не анаграммы\") << endl;\n    cout << test3 << \" и \" << test4 << (areAnagramsWithPunctuation(test3, test4) ? \" - анаграммы\" : \" - не анаграммы\") << endl;\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <string>\n#include <vector>\n\nint main() {\n    std::vector<std::string> words = {\"apple\", \"banana\", \"cherry\", \"date\"};\n    std::string delimiter = \", \";\n    std::string result;\n    \n    for(size_t i = 0; i < words.size(); i++) {\n        result += words[i];\n        if(i != words.size() - 1) {\n            result += delimiter;\n        }\n    }\n    \n    std::cout << \"Результат: \" << result << std::endl;\n    \n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <string>\n#include <stdexcept>\nusing namespace std;\n\nvoid validate_email(const string& email) {\n    if (email.find('@') == string::npos) {\n        throw invalid_argument(\"Email must contain @ symbol\");\n    }\n    cout << \"Email \\\"\" << email << \"\\\" is valid\" << endl;\n}\n\nint main() {\n    try {\n        validate_email(\"user@example.com\");\n        validate_email(\"invalid-email\");\n    } catch (const invalid_argument& e) {\n        cout << \"Error: \" << e.what() << endl;\n    }\n    return 0;\n}

#include <iostream>\n#include <fstream>\nint main() {\n    std::ifstream file(\"input.bin\", std::ios::binary | std::ios::ate);\n    std::streamsize size = file.tellg();\n    file.seekg(0, std::ios::beg);\n    char* buffer = new char[size];\n    file.read(buffer, size);\n    file.close();\n    delete[] buffer;\n    return 0;\n}
#include <iostream>\n#include <string>\n\nstd::string reverseString(const std::string& str) {\n    if(str.empty()) return \"\";\n    return reverseString(str.substr(1)) + str[0];\n}\n\nint main() {\n    std::string str = \"hello\";\n    std::cout << \"Реверс: \" << reverseString(str) << std::endl;\n    return 0;\n}
